lohasya trayo daśabhedānāṃ madhyāt kenāpi bhedena sahayogaḥ kārya iti lohaśabdena dhvanitam ।।

abhra sattva induction of cāraṇa
vaṃgamatho ghanasatvaṃ tālakaṣaḍbhāgasāritaṃ carati ।
abhiṣavayogāccarati vrajati raso nātra sandehaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

lohayogamuktvā vaṅgayogamāha vaṅgamityādi ।।
atha lohakathanānantaraṃ vaṅgaṃ khurasaṃjñakaṃ abhrakaṃ ca etaddvayaṃ tālakaṣaḍbhāgasāritaṃ tālakasya ṣaḍaṃśena ekaśarīratāṃ nītaṃ tatsvarūpaṃ rasaścarati ।।
kasmāt abhiṣavayogāt abhiṣavaḥ saṃmardanaṃ tadyogāt ṣuñ abhiṣave ityasya dhāto rūpaṃ abhiṣavaḥ ।।
punaḥ rasaścarati milati ।।
cāritaṃ yat taddravati taddrutaṃ rase vrajati pṛthaktvāt saṃ milati nātrasandehaḥ niḥ saṃdigdhamiva ।।
vaṅgasya laghudravitvāt ṣaḍaṃśayogastālakasya yuktaḥ lohajāteḥ kāṭhiṇyāt samabhāgatvaṃ uditam ।।

abhra sattva induction of cāraṇa
bahalaṃ suvarṇavarṇaṃ niculapuṭaiḥ patati pañcabhiḥ satvam ।
vaṭakīkṛtamṛtagaganaṃ nirañjanaṃ kiṭṭarahitaṃ ca ।।
taccūrṇīkṛtya tataḥ kṣārāmlairbhāvitaṃ ghanaṃ bahuśaḥ ।
sṛṣṭitrayanīrakaṇātumbururasamarditaṃ carati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

abhrasatvavidhānamāha bahalamityādi ।।
vaṭakīkṛtaṃ ca tanmṛtaṃ ca gaganaṃ tathoktaṃ na vaṭako vaṭakaḥ kriyata iti vaṭakīkṛtaṃ atra abhūtatadbhāve cviḥpratyayaḥ ।।
pañcabhirniculapuṭaiḥ pañcasaṃkhyābhirvetasavṛkṣadravabhāvanābhir bhāvitaṃ yanmṛtagaganaṃ mṛtābhraṃ vaṭakīkṛtaṃ satsatvaṃ patati taddrāvakauṣadhayogaṃ vidhāya vahninā vidhamanāditi śeṣaḥ ।।
kiyanmānaṃ satvaṃ patati bahalaṃ bahu anyavidheradhikam ।।
kīdṛśaṃ svarṇavarṇaṃ pītaśvetaṃ prakāśākhyaṃ punarnirañjanaṃ nirmalaṃ kiṭṭarahitaṃ ca ।।
asmin satve kācakiṭṭābhāvaḥ ।।
sarvotkṛṣṭavidhirayaṃ pūrvamuditāt bahalasatvapātādityarthaḥ ।।
kevalasatvacāraṇavidhānamāha tadityādi ।।
tatastadabhrasatvapātanavidheranantaraṃ tadevābhrasatvaṃ cūrṇīkṛtya kalkaṃ vidhāya kṣārāmlairbhāvitaṃ kuryāt kṣārāḥ svarjikādayaḥ amlā jambīrādayaḥ tairbahuśo bahuvāraṃ gharmapuṭitaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ ।।
punaḥ sṛṣṭitrayanīrakaṇātumbururasamarditaṃ sṛṣṭiḥ pūrvoktā tattrayaṃ mūtraśukraśoṇitamiti nīrakaṇā jalapippalī tumbaru pratītaṃ eteṣāṃ rasena marditaṃ kuryāt ।।
abhrasattvamevaṃ kṛtaṃ sat carati grasati rasaḥ ityadhyāhāraḥ ।।

śulvābhra production
ghanasatvaśulbamākṣikasamabhāganiyojitaṃ tathā militam ।
tacchulbābhraṃ kathitaṃ carati raso jīryati kṣipram ।।
iti tāpyaśulbasahitaṃ ghanasatvaṃ lohakhalvake mṛditam ।
carati rasendraḥ kāñjikavetasajambīrabījapūrāmlaiḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha śulbābhramāha ghanetyādi ।।
ghanasatvaśulbamākṣikasamabhāganiyojitaṃ ghanasatvam abhrasatvaṃ śulbaṃ tāmraṃ mākṣikaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ samabhāgena tulyabhāgena niyojitaṃ prayuktaṃ tanmilitaṃ sat śulbābhraṃ kathitam ।।
atra śulbaṃ kīdṛśaṃ prayojyaṃ tadāha ।
dvāvarkau mlecchanepālau rase nepāla uttamaḥ ।
ghanaghātasahaḥ snigdho raktapatro'malo mṛduḥ ।।
mlecchastu kṣālitaḥ kṛṣṇo rūkṣasnigdho ghanāsahaḥ ।
miśrito nāgalohābhyāṃ na śreṣṭho rasakarmaṇi ।
iti ato nepālakaṃ grāhyamityarthaḥ ।।
tacchulvābhraṃ rasaḥ kṣipraṃ carati punaḥ kṣipraṃ śīghraṃ tacchulbaṃ jīryati jāraṇamāpnoti ।।
atra mākṣikayogaḥ śulbābhrasatvamelanārthaṃ rasaprītyeti bhāvaḥ ।।
śulbābhracāraṇavidhānamāha itītyādi ।।
iti pūrvoktaṃ tāpyaśulbasahitaṃ tāpyaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ śulbaṃ tāmraṃ nepālasaṃjñakaṃ tābhyāṃ sahitaṃ miśritaṃ ghanasatvaṃ taptalohakhalvake mṛditaṃ kāryaṃ mardanīyaṃ kaiḥ kṛtvā kāñjikavetasajambīrabījapūrāmlaiḥ kāñjikamuktavidhānaṃ sauvīraṃ vetasaṃ cukraṃ jambīraṃ prasiddhaṃ bījapūro mātuluṅgaḥ eteṣāmamlaiḥ dravarūpaiḥ ।।
tataḥ śulvābhraṃ rasendraḥ pāradaścarati grasati ।।
lohakhalvasya kathanāt taptakhalvake mardanaṃ kuryāditi tātparyārthaḥ ।।

bhasman rañjana
iti tīkṣṇaśulbanāgaṃ mākṣikayuktaṃ ca tatkṛtaṃ khoṭam ।
tadbhasma ca puṭavidhinā nirvyūḍhaṃ satvarañjakaṃ bhavati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

prakārāntaramāha itītyādi ।।
iti pūrvoktalakṣaṇaṃ tīkṣṇaśulbanāgaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ tāmraṃ nāgaṃ ca etattrayaṃ mākṣikayuktaṃ svarṇamākṣikayutaṃ samaṃ tulyabhāgaṃ kuryāt ।।
tatkṛtaṃ khoṭaṃ taiḥ sarvaiḥ piṣṭīstambhena khoṭabhasma kāryam ।।
puṭavidhinā vahnipuṭavidhānena tatkṛtaṃ khoṭaṃ bhasma kāryaṃ punaḥ tadbhasma satve nirvyūḍhaṃ nirvāhitaṃ sat satvarañjakaṃ bhavati khasatve abhrasatve rāgadāyi bhavati rañjitaṃ tatsatvaṃ rasarañjakaṃ bhavediti ।।

cāryaṃ yatnena rase ghanasatvaṃ tadvidhaṃ ghanaṃ tasya ।
saṃyojya sarvabījaṃ nirvāhya dvandvasaṃkarataḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

rañjitaghanasatvasya cāraṇamāha cāryamityādi ।।
tadvidhaṃ pūrvarañjitaṃ ghanasatvam abhrasatvaṃ ca ghanaṃ kevalaghanodbhavaṃ satvaṃ arañjitaṃ rase pārade cāryaṃ grāsagrasanamānenaitad abhrasatvaṃ rase saṃyojyam ।।
vā satve sarvabījaṃ sarvaṃ rāgadāyi dravyaṃ saṃyojya nirvāhyaṃ nirvāhitaṃ kuryāt ।।
kutaḥ dvandvasaṃkarataḥ dvandvānāṃ saṃkaro melāpaḥ saṅkaro'vakara ityamaraḥ ।।
nirvāhyaṃ iti vaha prāpaṇe ityasya rūpaṃ pūrvavat ।।
niravyayaṃ niścayārthaṃ nirniścayaniṣedhayoḥ ityamaraḥ ।।

abhrakacāraṇamādau garbhadruticāraṇaṃ ca hemno'nte ।
yo jānāti na vādī vṛthaiva so'rthakṣayaṃ kurute ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha rasacāraṇe jñeyamāha abhraketyādi ।।
yo vādī rasakartā ādau prathamaṃ abhracāraṇaṃ na jānāti yathā raso'bhrakaṃ carati grasati punaḥ tatpaścāt garbhadruticāraṇaṃ yadrasagarbhe drutaṃ dravarūpaṃ tiṣṭhatyabhrādikaṃ tasya cāraṇaṃ grasanaṃ punarante hemnaḥ svarṇasya cāraṇaṃ grasanaṃ na jānāti sa vṛthaiva mithyaiva arthakṣayaṃ dhananāśaṃ kurute kāryasiddherabhāvāt ।।
sarvajña eva rasakriyāyāṃ pravarteteti bhāvaḥ ।।

abhra sattva grāsa only abhra part is "eaten"
gaganagrāsarahasyaṃ vakṣyāmyekaṃ ghanārkasaṃyogāt ।
kevalamabhrakasatvaṃ grasate yatnānna sarvāṅgam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

grāsarahasyamāha gaganetyādi ।।
ahaṃ śrīmadgovindabhagavatpūjyapādācāryaḥ ekamadvitīyaṃ gaganagrāsarahasyaṃ abhrakakavalane grāsakautukaṃ vakṣyāmi kathayāmi ।।
kasmāt ghanārkasaṃyogāt ghanaṃ abhrakasatvaṃ arkastāmraṃ etayoḥ saṃyogaḥ tasmāt ubhayasatvakṛtakhoṭaṃ cāryam ।।
athaśabdaḥ pakṣāntarasūcakaḥ ।।
abhrasatvasya yasya dhāto rūpaṃ tena saha yasya dhātorvā saṃyogo bhavati dvandvabhāvāt saṅkarataḥ tatsaṃyuktamabhidhānaṃ bhavati yathā śulvābhraṃ nāgābhraṃ vaṅgābhraṃ mākṣikābhraṃ hemābhram iti evaṃ sarvatra saṃyogānnāmaniṣpattiḥ ।।
grastasya drāvaṇaṃ garbhe garbhadrutirudāhṛtā bahireva dravīkṛtya ghanasatvādikaṃ khalu ।
jāraṇāya rasendrasya sā bāhyadrutirucyate ।।

yadi ghanasatvaṃ garbhe na patati no vā dravanti bījāni ।
na ca bāhyadrutiyogastatkathamiha badhyate sūtaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vāco marīcibhistaptaṃ toṣaya janakairavam ।
kumudāni ca kāsārodvartīni cirabhāsayā ।।
atha garbhadrutibāhyadrutipraśaṃsanamāha yadītyādi ।।
yadi ced ghanasatvam abhrasatvaṃ garbhe pāradasyāntarna patati dravatvaṃ nāpnoti vā bījāni śulbābhrādīni pāradasyodare no dravanti na rasarūpā bhavanti ca punaḥ bāhyadrutir na yujyate cedevaṃ na syāttarhi iha asyāṃ kriyāyāṃ prāptāyāṃ satyāṃ sūto rasaḥ kathaṃ badhyate anyathā na ko'pyupāyaḥ ।।

garbhadrutyā rahito grāsaścīrṇo'pi naikatāṃ yāti ।
ekībhāvena vinā na jīryate tena sā kāryā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

garbhadruterādhikyaṃ darśayannāha garbhetyādi ।।
cīrṇo api grāsaḥ cāraṇatāṃ prāpto api kavalaḥ yadi garbhadrutyā rahito bhavet rasasyodare rasarūpakaraṇavarjito bhavet tadā ekatāṃ na yāti rasarūpo na bhavati ।।
punarekībhāvena vinā grāso na jīryate jāraṇatvaṃ nāpnoti ।।
tena hetunā garbhadrutipūrvikā jāraṇā kāryā rasabandhe jāraṇaṃ heturiti bhāvaḥ ।।

bījānāṃ saṃskāraḥ kartavyaḥ ko'pi tādṛśaḥ prathamam ।
yena dravanti garbhe rasarājasyāmlavargeṇa ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

jāraṇāyāṃ prathamaṃ kartavyamāha bījānāmityādi ।।
bījānāṃ śulbābhrādīnāṃ ko'pyanirvacanīyaḥ saṃskāro garbhe drutikārakaḥ prathamaṃ kartavyaḥ saṃskriyata iti saṃskāraḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaḥ tādṛśaḥ taiḥ bījaiḥ sadṛśaḥ yathā bījāni śaktimanti santi tathā saṃskāro api śaktimān kartavya ityarthaḥ ।।
saṃskāraḥ kena kartavyaḥ amlavargeṇa jambīrādinā ।।
yena saṃskāreṇa rasarājasya garbhe rasodare bījāni dhātūpadhātujātāni śulbābhrādīni dravantītyarthaḥ ।।

garbhadrutiyogyabīja 
samamākṣikakṛtavāpaṃ samamākṣikasatvasaṃyutaṃ hema ।
garbhe dravati ca jarati ca jaritaṃ badhnāti nānyathā sūtam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

hemabījapraśaṃsanamāha sametyādi ।।
samamākṣikakṛtavāpaṃ samabhāgaṃ tulyāṃśaṃ hemnā yanmākṣikaṃ tasya kṛtvā vāpo vāraṃ vāram ākṣepo agniyogād yasmin tathoktaṃ punastaddhema samamākṣikasatvasaṃyutaṃ hemnā samaṃ tulyaṃ yanmākṣikasatvaṃ tena saṃyutaṃ kṛtakhoṭaṃ kuryāt ।।
tatkhoṭarūpaṃ hema garbhe pāradāntardravati ।।
punastaddrāvitaṃ hema jarati jīrṇatām āpnoti ।।
taddhema jaritaṃ sat sūtaṃ raseśvaraṃ badhnāti ।।
anyathā anyaprakāreṇa sūto bandhanaṃ nāpnoti ।।
mākṣikasya vāpo hemno varṇotkarṣaprada iti bhāvaḥ ।।

tārāriṣṭa
mākṣikasatvaṃ hemnā pādādikajāritaṃ drutaṃ sūte ।
tārāriṣṭaṃ kurute varakanakaṃ pattralepena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

mākṣikasatvacāraṇādrase guṇotkarṣam āha mākṣikasatvamityādi ।।
mākṣikasatvaṃ vahnyauṣadhayogadrutaṃ yaddhemamākṣikasāraṃ hemnā kanakena saha sūte pārade pūrvaṃ yadgutaṃ punaḥ pādādikajāritaṃ pādādikavibhāgena pādārdhasatvena niḥśeṣatāmāptaṃ sat ayaṃ sūtaḥ tārāriṣṭaṃ tāraṃ rūpyādi ariṣṭaṃ śubhaṃ varakanakaṃ kurute pūrṇavarṇamityarthaḥ ।।
kena vidhānena pattralepanena patraṃ kaṇṭakabhedi tatra yo'sau lepaḥ vahniyogāditi śeṣaḥ tena ।।
hemamākṣikasatvajāritasya rūpyapatralepena kanakaṃ syāditi vyaktārthaḥ ।।

samarasatāṃ yadi yāto vastrādgalito'dhikaśca tulanāyām ।
grāso drutaḥ sa garbhe drutvāsau jīryate kṣipram ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

garbhadruter lakṣaṇamāha sametyādi ।।
yadi grāsaḥ samarasatāṃ yāto bhavedrasatulyarūpatāṃ prāpto bhavet punarvastrādgalito bhavet caturguṇaśvetavastrānniḥsṛto bhavet punastulanāyāṃ tulākarmaṇi yadādhiko'pi syāttadā garbhe pāradasyāntar druto grāso jñātavyaḥ garbhadruto raso veditavya iti vyaktārthaḥ ।।
punarasau raso drutvā dravarūpaṃ śīghraṃ prāpto jīryati dhātūnapi vidhāneneti śeṣaḥ ।।

na biḍairnāpi kṣārairna snehairdravati hemaṃ tāraṃ vā ।
mākṣikasatvena vinā tridinaṃ nihitena raktena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

mākṣikasatvotkarṣamāha netyādi ।।
mākṣikasatvena vinā svarṇamākṣikasāram antareṇa hema kanakaṃ vā tāraṃ rūpyaṃ na dravati ।।
kaiḥ kṛtvā viḍaiḥ kṛtvā śaṅkhacūrṇārkakṣārādikṛtapiṇḍaiḥ kṛtvā granthāntare ca ।
lavaṇakṣāroparasair ebhir amlairbiḍo mataḥ ।
same garbhe tu saṃsthāpyo hyanenaiva dravībhavet ।
iti ।।
na kevalaṃ biḍaiḥ kiṃtu kṣārairapi na kṣāraiḥ svarjikāyavakṣāraṭaṅkaṇādyaiḥ ।।

iti ।।
tailairapi na dravati ।
punarmākṣikasatvena garbhe drutirjāyate ।।

raktacandanasaṃyukto raktavargaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।

mercury cāraṇa, garbhadruti
lavaṇaṃ devīsvarasaplutam ahipatraṃ vicūrṇitaṃ śilayā ।
etat puṭanatritayāt sumṛtaṃ saṃsthāpayedayaḥpātre ।।
vihitārdhāṃgulanimnā sphuṭavikaṭakaṭorikā mukhādhārā ।
tasyoparyādeyā kaṭorikā cāṅgulotsedhā ।।
vihitacchidratritayā śastā caturaṃgulordhvachidreṣu ।
lohaśalākā yojyāstatrāpi ca hemapatrāṇi ।।
saṃsthāpya vidhūpyante yantrādhastāt pradīpayedagnim ।
dhūmopalepamātrādbhavanti kṛṣṇāni hemapatrāṇi ।।
tānyagnitāpitāni ca paścādyantre mṛtāni dhūmena ।
pācitahemavidhānāccarati rasendro dravati garbhe ca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

svarṇajāraṇayantravidhānamāha lavaṇamityādi ।।
prathamaṃ lavaṇaṃ saindhavaṃ devīsvarasaplutaṃ kuryāt brāhmīsvakīyarasena saṃmiśraṃ kuryāt ।।
punar brāhmīrasaplutaṃ lavaṇaṃ ca ahipatraṃ tāmbūlidalaṃ tacca dvayaṃ śilayā vitatagrāveṇa cūrṇitaṃ peṣitaṃ kuryāt ।।
punaretad ayaḥpātre lohabhājane saṃsthāpayet ।।
etat sthāpitaṃ dravyaṃ puṭatritayāt tripuṭakaraṇādagnisaṃyogena sumṛtaṃ syāt ।।
tasya devīsvarasaplutasya sumṛtasaindhavasya mukhādhārā sphuṭavikaṭakaṭorikā pātrī kāryā mukhameva ādhāro yasyāḥ sā evaṃvidhā sphuṭā prakaṭā vikaṭā viparītā adhomukhetyarthaḥ sā kaṭorikā vihitā kāryā ayaḥpātrasya ।।
tasyāḥ kaṭorikāyā upari ūrdhvabhāge eṣā kaṭorikā ādeyā sthāpyā ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭā aṅgulotsedhā aṅgula utsedhaḥ parimāṇaṃ yasyāḥ sā tathoktā ।।
punaḥ kiṃviśiṣṭā ardhāṅgulanimnā ardhāṅgulaparimāṇanimnā madhyagā ।।
punaḥ kiṃviśiṣṭā vihitachidratritayā vihitāni kṛtāni chidratritayāni yasyāṃ sā evaṃvidhā śastā ca saṃtulavihitachidratritayā ।।
caturaṅgulordhvā taduparibhāge kaṭorikā caturaṅgulipramāṇonnateti bhāvaḥ ।।
punaśchidreṣu triṣu śalākā yojyā lohaśalākāḥ kṣepyāḥ punastatrāpi chidreṣu hemapatrāṇi kaṇṭakavedhīni kanakapatrāṇi yojyānīti ।।
evaṃvidhe pūrvaṃ nirmite yantre hemapatrāṇi sthāpya vidhūpyante ।।
tato'gniṃ pradīpayet yantrādhastād yantrādhobhāge vahniṃ prajvālayet tadā tāni hemapatrāṇi kṛṣṇāni śyāmavarṇāni bhavanti ।।
kasmāt dhūmopalepamātrāt dhūmaścāsāvupalepaśca dhūmopalepas tanmātrāt tatpramāṇāt ।।
yenauṣadhena dhūpo niruktastenauṣadhenopalepaḥ kāryaḥ patreṣviti ।।
punaḥ kiṃbhūtāni hemapatrāṇi rasendro jarati agnitāpitāni santi vahniyogāttaptāni kṛtāni ।।
svarṇajāraṇamidaṃ gaditam ।।
iti pañcabhiḥ ślokaiḥ kulakam ।।

tenaiva tārapatraṃ vidhinā saṃsvedya yantrayogena ।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha rūpyajāraṇamāha tenetyādi ।।
tenaiva vidhinā pūrvapidhānena tārapatraṃ rūpyadalaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ śyāmalaprabhaṃ jāyate ।।
kena saṃsvedya yantrayogena saṃsvedaḥ prabalāgnis tasyedaṃ sambandhi yadyantraṃ yasya yo yogastena ।।

athavā balinā vaṅgaṃ nāgābhidhānena yantrayogena ।
hemāhvaṃ tāraṃ vā dravati ca garbhe na sandehaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha yogāntaraṃ āha athavetyādi ।।
athaveti samuccaye ekārthaniṣṭhatvāt ।।
balinā gandhena saha vaṅgaṃ yantrayogena kṛṣṇaṃ jāyeta ।।
kevalaṃ vaṅgaṃ punarnāgābhidhānena saha nāgavidhānamapyevaṃ syāditi vyaktiḥ ।।
nāgābhidhāneneti nāganāmnā ākhyāhve abhidhānaṃ ca nāmadheyaṃ ca nāma ca ityamaraḥ ।।
evaṃvidhaṃ vaṅgaṃ vā nāgaṃ vā hemāhvaṃ hemapatraṃ vā tāraṃ tārapatraṃ vā etatsarvaṃ balinā kṛṣṇaṃ jāyeta mṛtaṃ ca sarvaṃ garbhe rasāntare dravati nātra saṃdehaḥ asaṃdigdhamidamuktam ।।
caśabdājjarati niḥśeṣatvamāpnoti ।।

rasaka garbhadruti 
rasakaṃ balinā yuktaṃ pūrvoktavidhānayogena ।
pakvaṃ cūrṇaṃ yāvadbhavati bhṛśaṃ dravati garbhe ca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

prayogāntaramāha rasakamityādi ।।
rasakaṃ kharparikaṃ balinā gandhena saha yuktaṃ sat militaṃ sat samabhāgena iti śeṣaḥ kena kṛtvā pūrvoktavidhānayogena pūrvoktaṃ yadvidhānaṃ yantrādikaṃ tasya yo'sau yogastena kṛtvā tāvadbhṛśamatyarthaṃ pakvaṃ kāryaṃ yāvadaśarīratāṃ yāti taccūrṇaṃ garbhe rasodare dravati garbhadrutirbhavati caśabdājjarati ca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

pūrvārthe vidhyantaramāha athavetyādi ।।

lead, tin combined māraṇa
rasadaradābhrakatāpyavimalāmṛtaśulbalohaparpaṭikā ।
snuhyarkadugdhapiṣṭaṃ kaṃkuṣṭhaśilāyutaṃ nāgam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha vidhyantaramāha rasetyādi ।।
rasadaradābhrakatāpyamiti rasaḥ pāradaḥ darado hiṅgulaḥ abhrakaṃ pratītaṃ tāpyaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ vimalā rukmamākṣikaṃ mṛtaṃ yacchulbaṃ tāmraṃ loho muṇḍādiśca eteṣāṃ rasādīnāṃ rasaparpaṭīvat parpaṭikā kāryā ।।
tayā yutaṃ nāgaṃ punaḥ kaṅkuṣṭhaśilāyutaṃ kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ haritapītavarṇo viṣaharapāṣāṇajātiḥ śilā manohvā tābhyāṃ yutaṃ miśritaṃ yannāgaṃ sīsakaḥ snuhyarkadugdhapiṣṭaṃ kāryaṃ snuhī sehuṇḍaḥ arkaḥ prasiddho viṭapī tayordugdhena piṣṭaṃ pāṃśubhūtaṃ mṛtaṃ yannāgaṃ kukkuṭapuṭavidhāneneti śeṣaḥ etadapi bījaṃ siddhaṃ garbhe dravati ca pūrvasaṃbandhāt ।।
atha vaṅgabījavidhānamāha abhraketyādi ।।
ciñcākṣāravimiśraṃ yadvaṅgaṃ amlikākṣārayuktaṃ vaṅgaṃ abhrakatālakaśaṅkharasasahitaṃ abhrakaṃ pratītaṃ tālakaṃ haritālaṃ śaṅkhaṃ kambugrīvaṃ rasaḥ pāradaḥ etaiścaturbhiḥ sahitaṃ yathā syāttathā punaḥ punaḥ vāraṃ vāraṃ nirutthaṃ yāvat tāvatpuṭitaṃ kuryāt ।।
etadauṣadhasyāṃśabhāgena saha puṭanādvaṅgaṃ nirjīvatāṃ yāti pañcatvamāpnoti etadapi bījaṃ siddhaṃ garbhadrāvaṇe jāraṇārthe ca pūrvasaṃbandhāt ।।
nāgavaṅgayor etad auṣadhaṃ kāraṇamityāha vidhinetyādi ।।
anena vidhinā uktavidhānena nāgaṃ sīsakaṃ puṭitaṃ sat mriyate mṛtaṃ bhavatīti vāmunā vidhānenaiva nirutthatāṃ gataṃ aśarīratāṃ prāptaṃ vaṅgaṃ sarvakarmasu cāraṇajāraṇabhakṣaṇādikāryeṣu niyujyate rasajñairiti śeṣaḥ ।।
nāgavaṅgamāraṇam ekavidham evoktam atas tadbhakṣaṇādiṣu parasparaṃ guṇādhikayogyaṃ natu jāraṇādiṣu ।।

mṛtanāgaṃ mṛtavaṅgaṃ mṛtavaraśulvaṃ mṛtaṃ tathā tīkṣṇam ।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

nāgavaṅgaśulvatīkṣṇānāṃ jāraṇavidhānamāha mṛtanāgamityādi ।।
mṛtanāgamiti mṛtaṃ nirjīvatāṃ gataṃ yannāgaṃ sīsakaṃ tathānena vidhānena mṛtaṃ vaṅgaṃ tathā mṛtaṃ nirutthatāṃ gataṃ varaśulbaṃ tāmraṃ tathā ca mṛtaṃ tīkṣṇam arivargeṇeti śeṣaḥ eṣāṃ madhye ekaikaṃ nāgaṃ vā vaṅgaṃ vā śulbaṃ vā tīkṣṇaṃ vā pṛthaktvena hemavare pūrṇavarṇe svarṇe śatanirvyūḍhaṃ hemnaḥ śataguṇanirvāhitaṃ kuryāt tatsiddhaṃ garbhe rasodare dravati caśabdājjarati ca ।।

gold mahābīja
samagarbhe drutikaraṇaṃ hemno vakṣyāmyahaṃ paraṃ yogam ।
bhrāmakasasyakacūrṇaṃ śatanirvyūḍhaṃ mahābījam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

mahābījaprabhāvaṃ darśayannāha samagarbha ityādi ।।
ihāsmiñśāstre vidhinā śāstroktarītyā yāni bījānyuktāni tāni kartavyāni sāmānyeneti bhāvaḥ paraṃ garbhadrutyarthaṃ ayaṃ vārttikendro yogaḥ vārttāsu kuśalā vārtikāḥ śāstropadeśarahitā ityarthaḥ atra bhāvādyarthe ikpratyayaḥ teṣu vārtikeṣu indraḥ pravaro yogaḥ tathānenaiva prakāreṇa ekamataścāyaṃ śāstropadeśikānāṃ śāstropadeśarahitānāṃ ca abhimata ityarthaḥ ।।

garbhadruti
athavā gandhakadhūmaṃ tālakadhūmaṃ śilāhvarasakasya ।
dattvādhomukhamūṣāṃ dīrghatamāṃ kharparasyārdhe ।।
ūrdhvaṃ lagnā piṣṭī sudṛḍhā ca yathā tathā ca kartavyā ।
dattvā kharparapṛṣṭhe daityendraṃ dāhayettadanu ।।
stokaṃ stokaṃ dattvā karṣāgnau dhmāpayenmṛdā liptām ।
garbhe dravati hi bījaṃ mriyate tathādhike dāhe ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

rasodare bījadrāvaṇavidhānamāha athavetyādi ।।
athaveti samuccaye ।।
ūrdhvaṃ dīrghatamamūṣāyantrasya talabhāge piṣṭī rasendrabījayor nirmitā piṣṭikā ca punaḥ sudṛḍhā yathā syāttathā lagnā kartavyā ।।
kiṃ kṛtvā kharparasyārdhe mṛnmayapātrasya khaṇḍārdhe khaṇḍaikadeśa ityarthaḥ dīrghatamāṃ adhobhāgamukhīṃ adhobhāge mukhaṃ yasyāḥ sā tathoktā tāṃ dattvā ।।
punaḥ kiṃ kṛtvā gandhakadhūmaṃ dattvā vā stokaṃ stokaṃ alpamalpaṃ tālakadhūmaṃ dattvā vā śilāhvarasakasya śilāhvā manaḥśilā rasakaḥ kharparaḥ cakavad bhāvasamāsaḥ tasya dhūmaṃ dattvā ।।
punastatkharparaṃ adhomukhamukhāṃ ca mṛdā liptāṃ mṛdveṣṭitāṃ karīṣāgnau dhmāpayet karīṣavahnāvityarthaḥ ।।
evaṃ adhomukhāṃ kharparaṃ ca dattvā daityendraṃ balināmānaṃ prastāvādgandhakaṃ tadanu tatkaraṇapaścād dāhayet ।।
evaṃ kṛte sati rasendramilitaṃ yadbījaṃ tadgarbhe rasendrāntardravati ।।
punarbījasahito rasendro adhike dāhe sati mriyata ityarthaḥ ।।
ślokatrayasaṃbandhādviśeṣakam ।।

viḍa production
gandhakatālakaśailāḥ sauvīrakarasakagairikaṃ daradam ।
kṣārāmlalavaṇāni viḍo mākṣikavaikrāntavimalasamabhāgaiḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha suvarṇajāraṇārthaṃ biḍamāha gandhaketyādi ।।
gandhakatālakaśailā iti gandhakaṃ pratītaṃ tālakaṃ haritālaṃ śailaḥ śilājatuḥ dvaṃdvaḥ samāsaḥ tena tathoktāḥ samabhāgāḥ kāryāḥ ।।
punaḥ sauvīrakaṃ śuklāñjanaṃ rasakaṃ kharparikaṃ gairikaṃ dhātugairikaṃ daradaṃ hiṅgulaṃ atraikavadbhāvasamāsaḥ tattathoktaṃ samabhāgaṃ kāryam ।।
punaḥ kṣārāmlalavaṇāni kṣārā yavakṣārādayaḥ amlaṃ jambīrādi lavaṇāni saindhavādīni etānyapi samabhāgāni ।।
kaiḥ saha mākṣikavaikrāntavimalasamabhāgaiḥ saha mākṣikaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ vaikrāntaṃ vajrabhūmijaṃ rajaḥ vimalaṃ rukmamākṣikaṃ etāni samabhāgāni tairbiḍa ucyate sarvaiḥ samabhāgaiḥ sumarditair biḍaḥ kārya ityarthaḥ ।।

viḍa for garbhadruti
kṛtvā suvarṇapiṣṭīṃ mṛditāṃ ca suveṣṭitāmanenaiva ।
tripuṭaistapte khalve mṛditā garbhe tathā dravati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

biḍayogādyathā bījaṃ garbhe dravati tathāha kṛtvetyādi ।।
pūrvoktā yā piṣṭī tāmanenaivoktabiḍayogena tapte khalve taptasaṃbandhāllohamaye tripuṭaiḥ karīṣāgnyātmakair mṛditā gharṣitā sati anenaiva ca veṣṭitā kāryā ।।
kiṃ kṛtvā suvarṇapiṣṭīṃ kanakapiṣṭīṃ vā anyasyāpi dhātoḥ suvarṇapiṣṭīṃ śobhanavarṇāṃ piṣṭīṃ kṛtvā ।।
khalve mṛditā satī tathā tenaiva prakāreṇa natvanyaprakāreṇa garbhe rasodare dravati salilarūpā tiṣṭhati ।।

viḍa for garbhadruti
rakte śatanirvyūḍhaṃ netrahitaṃ bhasma vaikrāntakaṃ cātha ।
vimalaṃ śatanirvyūḍhaṃ grasati samaṃ dravati garbhe ca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha vaikrāntagarbhadrutimāha rakta ityādi ।।
vaikrāntabhasma vajrabhūmijaṃ rajas tadudbhavaṃ bhasma rakte raktagaṇe śatanirvyūḍhaṃ śatavāraṃ nirvāhitaṃ kuryāt ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ netrahitaṃ netrahitaśabdena maṇitvaṃ darśitaṃ maṇayo netrahitā iti ।।
vimalaṃ rūpyamākṣikaṃ śvetavarṇaṃ yanmākṣikaṃ raktagaṇe śatanirvyūḍhaṃ kuryāt ।।
tadubhayaṃ vaikrāntaṃ vimalaṃ ca raktaśatanirvyūḍhaṃ sat raso grāsavidhānaṃ vihāya samaṃ grasati kavalayati stadgrasitaṃ garbhe rasāntardravati jarati ca iti caśabdārthaḥ ।।

viḍa for garbhadruti immer mit śatanirvāhaṇa
ye kecidviḍayogāḥ kṣārāmlalavaṇāni dīptavargāśca ।
sarve śatanirvyūḍhā garbhadrutikārakāḥ kathitāḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

raktagaṇādhikyaṃ darśayannāha ya ityādi ।।
ye kecidviḍayogā atra granthāntareṣvapi ca kathitāḥ tathā kṣārāmlalavaṇāni kathitāni kṣārā yavakṣārādayaḥ atha ca vṛkṣauṣadhisamudbhavāḥ amlā jambīrādayaḥ amlavṛkṣaśākasamudbhavāśca yānyetāni kathitāni ca punarye dīptavargāḥ kathitā dīptikarā yogā abhihitāḥ te sarve biḍakṣārāmlalavaṇadīptavargāḥ śatanirvyūḍhā garbhadrutikārakāḥ garbhe rasodare drutaṃ dravarūpaṃ kurvanti dhātumaṇiratnādīnīti śeṣaḥ ।।

Menge nirvāhaṇa grāsa, der assimiliert wird
śatanirvyūḍhe ca samaṃ pādonaṃ pañcasaptativyūḍhe ।
pañcāśati tadardhaṃ pādaḥ syātpañcaviṃśatike ।।
aṣṭāṃśaṃ tu tadardhe ṣoḍaśāṃśaṃ tadardhanirvyūḍhe ।
tasyārdhe dvātriṃśaccatuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśaṃ tadardhanirvyūḍhe ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

śatanirvāhitādau samādividhānamāha śatetyādi ।।
śatanirvyūḍha iti śatavāraṃ nirvāhite raktagaṇe iti śeṣaḥ samaṃ tulyaṃ grasati rasa iti śeṣaḥ ।।
punaḥ pañcasaptativyūḍhe sati pādonaṃ caturthāṃśavarjitaṃ samagraṃ grasatīti ।।
punaḥ pañcāśannirvyūḍhe sati tadardhaṃ samasyārdhamiti ।।
punaḥ pañcaviṃśatike sati pādaścaturthāṃśam ।।
nyūnādhike nirvyūḍhe sati nyūnādhikāṃśo jñeya iti viśeṣārthaḥ ।।
alpanirvyūḍhakramamāha aṣṭāṃśamityādi ।।
tu punastadardhe sārdhadvādaśake nirvyūḍhe sati aṣṭāṃśaṃ tadardhe ṣaḍvāranirvyūḍhe sati ṣoḍaśāṃśamiti punastasyārdhe trivāranirvyūḍhe sati dvātriṃśadaṃśaṃ tadardhanirvyūḍhe ekadvivāranirvyūḍhe sati catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśaṃ raso grasatītyarthaḥ ।।

garbhadruti
iti gaditāṃ garbhadrutimabhiṣavayogena cāmlavargeṇa ।
svedanavidhinā jñātvā mṛditāṃ tapte tu khalvatale ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

garbhadrutau satyāṃ kartavyamāha itītyādi ।।
ityuktavidhānena gaditāṃ kathitāṃ garbhadrutiṃ jñātvā tapte khalvatale lohamaye karīṣāgninā uṣṇatāṃ nīte mṛditāṃ kuryāt ।।
kena abhiṣavayogena abhiṣavaḥ saṃmardanaṃ tasya yogena na kevalamanena amlavargeṇa ca jambīrādinā na kevalamanenāpi svedanavidhinā ca svedanavidhiḥ svedanasaṃskāroktatvānnātrābhihitaḥ jāraṇahetoriti śeṣaḥ ।।

Durchfṃhrung von saṃskāra gemĪ“ den verwendeten bījas usw
jñātvā bījabalābalamardanayogaṃ kṛtaṃ ca rasarāje ।
svedavidhānaṃ ca puṭaṃ yantraṃ vā vihitarasakarma ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

mardanasvedanayoḥ pūrvopakaraṇaṃ darśayannāha jñātvetyādi ।।
bījabalābalamardanayogaṃ kṛtaṃ jñātvā bījānāṃ dhātūpadhātuyogajanitānāṃ balābale nyūnādhike yo'sau mardanayogastameva kṛtaṃ jñātvā viditvā rasarāje svedavidhānaṃ kuryāt vā puṭaṃ vahniyogaṃ kuryāt vā yantraṃ vihitarasakarma kuryāt vihitaṃ kṛtaṃ rasasya karma saṃskārarūpaṃ yatra tathoktaṃ garbhayantrādikamityarthaḥ ।।

sūtavaraṃ lakṣayate bījaṃ nopekṣatāṃ yathā yāti ।
tadvatkāryaṃ vidhinā sukarma gurupādanirdiṣṭam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sūtakarmaṇo durbodhatvādgurupādaṃ stuvannāha sūtetyādi ।।
yathā yena prakāreṇa sūtavaraṃ pāradaḥ lakṣayate jñāyate karmakṛteti śeṣaḥ punaryathā bījaṃ upekṣatāṃ na yāti samyak milati tadvattenaiva prakāreṇa gurupādanirdiṣṭaṃ karma ācāryavaryadarśitaṃ pūjyaṃ saṃskārarūpaṃ vidhinā ācāryoktavidhānena kuryāt ।।
gurupādalakṣaṇam ।
sarvaśāstraviśeṣajñaḥ kuśalo rasakarmaṇi ।
evaṃlakṣaṇasaṃyukto rasavidyāgururbhavet ।
iti ।।
iti garbhadrutijāraṇaprakaraṇam ।।

bāhyadruti
bāhyadrutirati vimalā sphurati hi keṣāṃcideva siddhānām ।
tebhyaḥ samyak jñātvā kalanāḥ kāryāstathā drutayaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

bāhyadrutiṃ praśaṃsannāha bāhyadrutir ityādi ।।
drutirdvidhoktā garbhadrutirbāhyadrutiśceti ।।
garbhadrutiḥ pūrvamuktā bāhyadrutir adhunābhidhīyate ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭā ativimalā nirmalatarā ।।
eṣā ca punaḥ keṣāṃcideva siddhānāṃ sphurati siddhā rasavidyāpāragā nityanāthādayaḥ teṣāṃ te jānantīti ।।
duṣprāpyatvāt bāhyadrutiriha viralā ।।
tebhyaḥ samyak jñātvā tathā tenaiva siddhodeśavidhānena drutayo bāhyadrutayaḥ ।।

jāraṇa of lead
varanāgaṃ rasarājaṃ bījavaraṃ sāritaṃ tathā tritayam ।
gandhakaśilālasahitaṃ nirnāgaṃ dīpavartito bhavati ।।
baddhvā sudṛḍhe vastre poṭalikāyāṃ śikhīkṛto dīpaḥ ।
taile magnaṃ kṛtvā nirnāgaṃ jāyate kṣipram ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha nāgajāraṇamāha varanāgamityādi ।।
varanāgaṃ śreṣṭhajāti sīsakaṃ jāraṇayogyaṃ rasarājaṃ uktasaṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛtaṃ pāradaṃ bījavaraṃ hemabījaṃ etattrayaṃ sāritaṃ militaṃ kāryaṃ punargandhakaśilālasahitaṃ gandhakaṃ pratītaṃ śilā manaḥśilā ālaṃ haritālaṃ dvandvastāni taiḥ sahitaṃ ca kāryaṃ etat sarvaṣaṭkaṃ dīpavartitaḥ prajvālitadīpavartiyogāt nirnāgaṃ nāgavarjitaṃ bhavati nāgaṃ jaratītyarthaḥ ।।
yathā nirṇāgaṃ syāttathā vidhānam āha baddhvetyādi ।।
tatpūrvoktaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ sudṛḍhe vastre nūtane vastre atropaśleṣike adhikaraṇe saptamī poṭalikāyāṃ baddhvā punastaile tilodbhave tatṣaṭkaṃ magnaṃ nimajjitaṃ kṛtvā tadadhaḥ śikhīkṛto dīpo'vadhāryaḥ na śikhī śikhāyuktaḥ kṛtaḥ śikhīkṛtaḥ śikhāvānityarthaḥ ।।
anena vidhinā kṣipraṃ śīghraṃ nirnāgaṃ syāditi ।।

jāraṇa of lead
kṛtvātra dīrghamūṣāṃ sudṛḍhāṃ dhmātaṃ tu bhasmagartāyām ।
kṣiptvā śilālacūrṇaṃ paścātsūtaṃ tataḥ śilācūrṇaṃ ।।
saṃsthāpya bhasmanāto dhmātaṃ syātsvāṃgaśītalaṃ yāvat ।
ākṛṣya tatra sūtaṃ jñātvā nāgaṃ subhakṣitaṃ sakalam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

nirnāgakaraṇe vidhānamāha kṛtvetyādi ।।
tu punaḥ dīrghāṃ gostanākārāṃ sudṛḍhāṃ nirvraṇavajropamāṃ mūṣāṃ kṛtvā tāṃ mūṣāṃ prati śilālacūrṇaṃ kṣiptvā śilā manohvā ālaṃ haritālaṃ etayoścūrṇaṃ paścātsūtaṃ pūrvoktaṃ pāradaṃ kṣiptvā tato'nantaraṃ śilācūrṇaṃ kṣiptvā tāmeva rasasaṃyuktāṃ mūṣāṃ bhasmagartāyāṃ bhasmanā yuktā yā gartā tasyāṃ dhmātaṃ kuryāt punastāvadbhasmanā ācchādya yāvatsvāṅgaśītalaṃ svayameva śītalaṃ syāt ।।
tatra tasyāṃ mūṣāyāṃ sakalaṃ samastaṃ nāgaṃ subhakṣitaṃ jīrṇatāṃ gataṃ jñātvā sūtaṃ ākṛṣya uddhārya nirnāgakaraṇavidhānam etat ।।

bīja of nāgajīrṇapārada
jñātvā nāgaṃ truṭitaṃ punarapi dadyādyathā bhavettriguṇam ।
paścācchuddhaṃ kṛtvā bījavaraṃ yojayettadanu ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

nirnāgānantaraṃ yatkartavyaṃ tadāha jñātvetyādi ।।
nāgaṃ sīsakaṃ truṭitaṃ buddhvā punarapi nāgaṃ dahyāt pūrvoktavidhānena pārade iti śeṣaḥ ।।
yathā nāgaṃ triguṇitaṃ bhavettathaiva kuryāt ।।
paścātsūtaṃ śuddhaṃ kṛtvā pāradaṃ nirnāgaṃ vidhāya tadanu nāgajāraṇānantaraṃ bījavaraṃ pūrvoktaṃ yojayet ।।

mercury jāraṇa of tin
athavā tāraṃ vaṅgaṃ sūtaṃ saṃsārya vaṅgaparihīnam ।
tālakayogena tathā nirvaṅgaṃ yantrayogena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha tārayogam āha athavetyādi ।।
athaveti vidhānāntaram ।।
tāraṃ vaṅgaṃ sūtam iti tāraṃ rūpyaṃ vaṅgaṃ khurakaṃ sūtaṃ saṃskṛtapāradaṃ etattritayaṃ saṃsārya melanaṃ vidhāya vaṅgaparihīnaṃ kuryāt tathā tenaiva vidhānena tālasya yo'sau yogastena yantrayogena ca dīrghamūṣāyogena ca nirvaṅgaṃ vaṅgavivarjitaṃ kuryāt ।।

mercury jāraṇa of tin
athavā vastranibaddhaṃ girijatusahitaṃ suveṣṭitaṃ māṣaiḥ ।
pakvaṃ taile vaṭakaṃ nirvaṅgaṃ jāyate nūnam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha athavetyādi ।।
athavā tāraṃ vaṅgaṃ vaṭakākāraṃ taile tilodbhave pakvaṃ kuryāt nūnaṃ niścitaṃ tadvaṭakaṃ tathā pakvaṃ kuryādyathā nirvaṅgaṃ jāyate vahniyogena iti śeṣaḥ ।।

bīja for garbhadruti
piṣṭīstambhaṃ kṛtvā bījavareṇaiva sāritaṃ tadanu ।
bīja for garbhadruti
athavā baddharasena tu sahitaṃ bījaṃ surañjitaṃ kṛtvā ।।
gandhakanihitaṃ sūtaṃ nihitānihitaṃ ca śṛṅkhalāyāṃ tat ।
yojitanirvyūḍharase garbhadrutikārakaṃ nūnam ।।
sūtakabhasmavareṇa tu bījaṃ kṛtvā rasendrake garbhe ।
mṛditā piṣṭī vidhinā hyabhiṣavayogāddravati garbhe ca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhānāntaramāha piṣṭītyādi ।।
bījavareṇaiva pūrvakanakabījenaiva sāritaṃ militaṃ sat piṣṭīstambhaṃ khoṭastambhaṃ kṛtvā tadanu tatpaścāt athaveti prakārāntaraṃ darśayati tu punaḥ baddharasena khoṭabaddharasena sahitaṃ surañjitaṃ śobhanavidhānena varṇavṛddhīkṛtaṃ bījaṃ svarṇabījaṃ saṃyutaṃ kuryāt yoga eva kārya iti dvividhānam uktam ।।
anyaccāha gandhaketyādi ।।
gandhakanihitaṃ gandhake nihitaṃ sthāpitaṃ sūtaṃ ūrdhvādho gandhakaṃ dattvā sūtaṃ madhyasthaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ ।।
ca punarevaṃvidhaṃ sūtaṃ śṛṅkhalāyāṃ śṛṅkhalīkaraṇayoge nihitānihitaṃ yannihitaṃ tadanihitam ajāritaṃ kāryaṃ nihitānihitasaṃyogāt śṛṅkhaleyaṃ nūnaṃ niścitaṃ yojitanirvyūḍharase pūrvaṃ yojitaṃ paścānnirvāhitaṃ nirvyūḍhaṃ yatra tattasminnevaṃvidharase garbhadrutiḥ pāradasyodare bījāni dravanti ।।
piṣṭīvidhinā jāraṇamāha sūtaketyādi ।।
tu punaḥ rasendrake garbhe rasendrakṛto yo'sau garbhastasmin bījaṃ kṛtvā vidhinā piṣṭīrvidheyā sā piṣṭī mṛditā kāryā kasmāt abhiṣavayogāt saṃmardanayogāt kena saha sūtakabhasmavareṇa saha sūtakasya yadbhasmavaraṃ tena sā piṣṭī garbhe dravati caśabdājjarati ca ।।

bīja for garbhadruti
patrābhrakaṃ ca satvaṃ kāṃkṣī vā kāntamākṣikaṃ puṭitam ।
nirguṇḍī gṛhakanyā cāṅgerī palāśaśākaiśca ।।
tāvatpuṭitaṃ kṛtvā yāvatsindūrasaprabhaṃ bhavati ।
tatpādaśeṣalavaṇaṃ haṇḍikapākena pācitaṃ sudṛḍham ।।
ekaikaṃ śatavyūḍhaṃ bījavaraṃ jārayedrasendrasya ।
garbhe dravati ca kṣipraṃ hyabhiṣavayogena mṛditamaṅgulyā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

bījavaravidhānamāha patrābhrakam ityādi ।।
patrābhrakamiti abhrakasya patrāṇi vābhrakasya satvaṃ punaḥ kāṃkṣī saurāṣṭrī kāntamākṣikaṃ kāntaścumbakaḥ mākṣikaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ eteṣāṃ dvandva ekatvaṃ punaretat nirguṇḍīgṛhakanyācāṅgerīpalāśaśākaiḥ puṭitaṃ nirguṇḍī sephālikā gṛhakanyā kumārī cāṅgerī amlaśākaḥ palāśo brahmavṛkṣaḥ śāko vṛkṣaviśeṣaḥ eteṣāṃ dvandvasamāsaḥ eteṣāṃ rasaṃ gṛhītvā pūrvauṣadhapuṭitaṃ kuryāt gharme iti śeṣaḥ ।।
tadauṣadhaṃ puṭitaṃ kṛtvā punastatpuṭitamauṣadhaṃ tatpādaśeṣaṃ caturthāṃśaṃ lavaṇaṃ saindhavaṃ dattvā haṇḍikāpākena haṇḍikāyāṃ mṛdbhājane yaḥ pākastena pācitaṃ vahnau puṭitaṃ tāvatkuryād yāvat sindūrasaṃprabhaṃ sindūratulyavarṇaṃ bhavati ।।
kathaṃ pācitaṃ kuryāt sudṛḍhaṃ yathā syāttathā ekaikaṃ śatavyūḍhamiti ।।
pūrvoktānāṃ sindūrīkṛtānām uparasānām adharāt ekaikaṃ ekaṃ ekaṃ pṛthaktvena śatavyūḍhaṃ śatavāraṃ vāhitaṃ bījavaraṃ jāyate kanake iti śeṣaḥ tadbījaṃ rasendrasya garbhe dravati caśabdāt kṣipraṃ śīghraṃ jarati ca ।।
kathaṃ aṅgulyā anāmikayā yo abhiṣavayogaḥ saṃmardanayogasteneti viśeṣakam ।।

gold, silver bīja with tin
vaṅgaṃ tu tena vidhinā hemavare kṣepya tālavāpena ।

atha vaṅgayogena bījamāha vaṅgamityādi ।।

rasāṅkuśa
yo niḥsṛto bhujaṅgād rasakeśarīvajrapañjaraḥ sa punaḥ ।
phaṇihemaguṇātkuṭilo rasāṅkuśo nāma vikhyātaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

suvarṇābhidhānabījapraśaṃsanamāha ya ityādi ।।
bhujaṅgāt sīsakāt niḥsṛtaḥ bhujaṅgaśilāvāpena kṣayaṃ nītvā yaḥ pṛthagbhūtaḥ sa rasakesarīvajrapañjaraḥ kathitaḥ rasa eva kesarī siṃhaḥ tadarthaṃ vajrapañjaraḥ vajreṇa vyadhitaḥ pañjaro'tidṛḍhatvāt siṃharakṣaṇasamartha ityarthaḥ ।।
punarviśeṣeṇocyate ayaṃ vajrapañjaro na kiṃtu ayaṃ rasāṅkuśaḥ raso gajarūpaḥ tasyāṅkuśaḥ vaśīkaraṇasamarthaḥ ।।
nāma saṃbhāvanāyām ।।
vikhyātaḥ prakathitaḥ ।।
kasmāt kuṭilāt kimapi vastuharaṇāt kuṭilo vakro bhavati duṣṭasvabhāva eva anena hemnā nāgaharaṇaṃ kṛtam ।।
kathaṃbhūtāt kuṭilāt phaṇī bhujaṅgaḥ hema svarṇaṃ tayorguṇā vidyante yasmin evaṃvidhāt kuṭilādeśo yuktaḥ aṅkuśo'pi vakro bhavatīti ।।
atra bhrāntimānalaṅkāraḥ hemabīje vajrapañjaragajāṅkuśadarśanād bhrāntirjāteti ।।

evaṃ pakvaṃ vidhinā bījavaraṃ sūtarāṭ tathāmlena ।

tailena tena vidhinā svinnā piṣṭī bhavedakhilam ।
athavā ślakṣṇaṃ śilayā nighṛṣṭabījaṃ bhavetpiṇḍī ।।
pāko vaṭakavidhinā kartavyastailayogena ।

evaṃ drutaṃ hi garbhe bījavaraṃ jarati rasarāje ।
garbhadrutyā rahitaṃ biḍayogairjarati garbhe ca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

bījasyāsya piṣṭīkaraṇamāha evamityādi ।।
evaṃ amunā prakāreṇa vidhinārthād upadeśena pakvaṃ yadbījavaraṃ tathā pūrvasaṃskṛtaḥ sūtarāṭ pāradaḥ amlena jambīrādinā saṃsvedyaḥ svedākhyo vidhiḥ kartavyaḥ ।।
atra kimavadhistatkartavyo yāvat ślakṣṇā spaṣṭā piṣṭī ekaśarīratā bhavet rasabījayoriti śeṣaḥ ।।
vidhyantaramāha tailenetyādinā ।।
tena pūrvoktena vidhinā vadhavidhānena tilatailena svinnā sveditā satī piṣṭirbhavati vahnāviti śeṣaḥ ।।
athaveti vidhānāntaraṃ darśayati ।।
śilayā dṛṣanmayayā nighṛṣṭabījaṃ nighṛṣṭaṃ gharṣitaṃ yadbījaṃ nāgākhyaṃ tat sūteneti śeṣaḥ akhilaṃ samastaṃ yathā syāttathā piṣṭirbhavatīti ।।
yathā vaṭakaḥ pācyastathāha pāka ityādi ।।
vaṭakavidhinā māṣavaṭakavidhinā tailayogena pākaḥ kartavyaḥ vahnau pācanaṃ vidheyamityarthaḥ ।।
kiṃ kṛtvā krāmaṇapiṇḍe kṣiptvā biḍapiṇḍamadhye sthāpya ca punarmāṣair annaviśeṣair dṛḍhapiṇḍatvaṃ syāt māṣacūrṇaveṣṭitaṃ krāmaṇapiṇḍaṃ dṛḍhaṃ bhavediti vyaktiḥ ।।
tadvidhānamāha mṛdvityādi ।।
māṣacūrṇitajātaṃ krāmaṇapiṇḍaṃ tāvat supakvaṃ kartavyaṃ yāvaddagdhaṃ na bhavet ।।
kena supakvaṃ mṛdvagninā komalavahninā puṭaḥ tatpiṇḍataḥ śeṣaṃ śiṣṭaṃ taṃ nirmalapāradaṃ ākṛṣya gṛhītvā piṇḍamanyasmin piṇḍe tathā pūrvaprakāreṇa pācyamiti ।।
aparaṃ cāha athavetyādi ।।
athaveti prakārāntare ।।
punarapi piṣṭīrdolātapte auṣadhapiṇḍe dolayottapte uṣṇatāṃ nīte krāmaṇauṣadhānāṃ piṇḍe kṣepya madhye sthāpya kasyopari kharpare mṛnmayapātropari ।।
kena vidhinā pūrvoktena tailena vā amleneti ।।
kiyatkālaṃ yāvadgarbhe rasodare piṣṭī dravati tāvadbiḍāntare piṇḍāntare kṣepyeti tātparyārthaḥ ।।
aparaṃ cāha evamityādi ।।
evaṃ amunā prakāreṇa garbhe rasodare jarati niḥśeṣatvaṃ rasodare prāpnoti ca punargarbhadrutyā rahitaṃ draveṇa varjitaṃ bījavaraṃ biḍairjarati drutabījamāraṇasamartho biḍa ityarthaḥ ।।
drutagrāsaparimāṇo biḍayantrādiyogataḥ ।

jāraṇa method

grāsamiti cārayitvā garbhadrutiṃ tato bhūrje ।
lavaṇakṣārāmlasudhāsurabhīmūtreṇa kṛtalepe ।।
dṛḍhavastrabāhyabaddhe dolāsvedena jārayedgrāsam ।
sauvīreṇārdhapūrṇe kumbhe sakṣāramūtrakairathavā ।।
amunā krameṇa divasaistribhistribhirjārayedgrāsam ।
garbhadrutijāraṇamāha grāsamityādi ।।
pūrvoktaprakāreṇa grāsaṃ kavalaṃ yathāsaṃkhyaṃ cārayitvā punargarbhadrutiṃ kṛtvā tatastadanantaraṃ tadgarbhadrutaṃ sūtaṃ bhūrje bhūrjavṛkṣatvakpuṭake sthāpayedityarthaḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭe bhūrje lavaṇakṣārāmlasudhāsurabhimūtreṇa kṛtalepe lavaṇāni saindhavādīni kṣārāḥ svarjikādayaḥ amlo jambīrādiḥ sudhā śukticūrṇaṃ surabhī dhenustanmūtraṃ etena yogena kṛtvā kṛto lepo yasmin ।।
udaradrutiyuktaḥ sūtaḥ sthāpya ityarthaḥ ।।
jāraṇavidhānamāha dṛḍhetyādi ।।
dṛḍhavastrabāhyabaddhe iti dṛḍhaṃ nūtanaṃ ghanaṃ ca yadvastraṃ tena bāhye sarvato baddhe saṃyate pūrvoktena dolāsvedena dolāyantravidhinā yaḥ svedastaṃ kṛtvā grāsaṃ rasāntardrutaṃ kavalaṃ jārayet ।।
kutra kumbhe kalaśe kiṃviśiṣṭe sauvīreṇārdhapūrṇe sauvīreṇa svedanasaṃskāroditakāñjikena kṛtvā ardhapūrṇe ।।
athaveti vidhyantare ।।
sakṣāramūtrakaiḥ saha kṣāraḥ svarjikādibhiḥ vartante yāni mūtrāṇi go'jāvinārīṇāmiti śeṣaḥ etaiḥ ardhabhṛte kumbhe jārayedityarthaḥ ।।
atha rasajāraṇe kālasaṃkhyāmāha amunetyādi ।।
amunā krameṇeti uktaprakāreṇa tribhistribhirdivasaiḥ tribhiḥ saṃkhyākairdivasaiḥ grāse jāte anyagrāsaḥ kriyate garbhadrutagrāsaḥ kriyate garbhadrutagrāsaḥ tridivasairjaratīti bhāvaḥ ।।

jīrṇasya lakṣaṇamatho jñeyaṃ yantrātsamuddhṛtya ।।
Untersuchung, ob jāraṇa stattgefunden hat
uddhṛtamātraṃ pātre prakṣālya kāṃjikenātaḥ ।
samalaṃ ca kāṃjikamato haraṇārthaṃ vastrayogena ।।
tadanu sukhoṣṇe pātre saṃmardyo'sau yathā na hīye ।
tāvadyāvacchuṣyati tallagnaṃ kāñjikaṃ sakalam ।।
itthaṃ ca śoṣitajalaḥ karamardanataḥ sunirmalībhūtaḥ ।
pīḍyaḥ pātrasyopari vastreṇa caturguṇenaiva ।।
yadi parigalitaḥ sakalo vastrād grāsena caikatāṃ yātaḥ ।
na bhavati yadi daṇḍadharo jīrṇagrāsastadā jñeyaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atheti tridinasvedānantaraṃ jīrṇasya rasasya lakṣaṇaṃ jñeyaṃ grāso jīrṇo na veti jñātavyaḥ ।।
kiṃ kṛtvā yantrāddolikābhidhānād uddhṛtya yantrād bahir gṛhītveti ।।
rasamalāpanayanamāha uddhṛtetyādi ।।
uddhṛtamātramiti yantrād bahir gṛhītamātraṃ tatpātre bhājane mṛnmaye kāñjikena prakṣālya ।।
punar ato rasātsamalaṃ malasaṃyutaṃ kāñjikaṃ haraṇīyaṃ bahiḥ kāryam ।।
kena kṛtvā vastrayogena vastre kṣiptaṃ sat tadeva tiṣṭhati na kāñjikam ।।
tasyaiva vidhānaṃ cāha tadanvityādi ।।
tadanu vastrayogānantaraṃ sukhoṣṇe pātre asau rasaḥ saṃmardyaḥ ।।
kathaṃ yathā na hīyate nāśaṃ nāpnuyāt atyauṣṇyāt vā kāṃsyatāmranāgavaṅgakanakatārapātrāt vā dṛḍhakaraghātād raso hīna eva syāt ato'sau pāradas tāvan saṃmardyo yāvallagnakāñjikaṃ rasasaṃsargasauvīraṃ śuṣyati niḥśeṣatāṃ yātītyarthaḥ ।।
tasyaiva vidhānaṃ cāha itthamityādi ।।
itthaṃ amunā prakāreṇa karamardanataḥ hastatalamardanataḥ sunirmalībhūto malarahitaḥ śoṣitajalo rasaścaturguṇena vastreṇa kṛtvā pānasyopari pīḍyaḥ ।।
jīrṇagrāsalakṣaṇam āha yadītyādi ।।
tadā pārado jīrṇagrāso jñeyaḥ jīrṇo niḥśeṣatvamāpanno grāso yasmin sa tathoktaḥ ।।
yadi sakalaḥ sarvaḥ vastrātparigalitaḥ caturguṇavastrāt cyuto bhavati pātre iti śeṣaḥ ।।
punaryadi grāsena saha ekatāṃ yātaḥ san militaḥ san raso daṇḍadharo na bhavati sthirarūpo na syāt tadā jīrṇagrāso jñātavya ityarthaḥ ।।

grāsājīrṇa treatment
grāsādajīrṇapiṣṭīṃ sūtāduddhṛtya pātayedyantre ।
svastho bhavati rasendro grāsaḥ pakvaḥ punarjarati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

rasājīrṇalakṣaṇamāha grāsādityādi ।।
grāsāt kavalasaṃyogāt ajīrṇapiṣṭīṃ ajīrṇā aparipakvā yā piṣṭī pūrvoktalakṣaṇā tāṃ sūtāt rasāt yantre pātanakarmocite pātayet ।।
evaṃ grāsātpṛthakkṛtya patitaḥ svastho nirmalo bhavati ।।
punargrāsaḥ pakvo vahnitale dattvā pakvaḥ kṛtastaṃ rasendro jaratīti ।।

dolāyāṃ catvāro grāsā jāryā yathākrameṇaiva ।
śeṣāḥ kacchapayantre yāvad dviguṇādikaṃ jarati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

grāsajāraṇāyāṃ yantrādikaraṇamāha dolāyāmityādi ।।
yathākrameṇaiva catuḥṣaṣṭyādinaiva catvāro grāsā dolāyāṃ jāryāḥ śeṣā grāsāścatvāraḥ asaṃkhyā vā kacchapayantre jalayantre ca jāryāḥ ।।
śeṣāścatvāraḥ kutaḥ yato anyaśāstreṣu aṣṭaiva grāsāḥ ।।
jāraṇe kimavadhiḥ yāvaddviguṇādikaṃ jarati pāradāddviguṇitaṃ ādiśabdena dviguṇānnyūnaṃ na kāryaṃ adhikamadhikaṃ ca bhavatu ।।
śaktyavatare'ṣṭau bṛhacchāstre kvacid aṣṭau grāsā uktāḥ kvacidviṃśatigrāsā iti ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī
grāse'nirdiṣṭasaṃkhyatvaṃ darśayannāha netyādi ।।
atrāsmin śāstre ādau prathamaṃ grāsapramāṇaniyamaḥ kartuṃ na śakyaḥ ।।
yataḥ kāraṇāt gaganamabhraṃ sarvāṅgaṃ na grasate rasa iti śeṣaḥ ।।
tatsarvāṅgagrastaṃ gaganamabhraṃ lakṣaṇaireva jñātavyamityarthaḥ ।।
catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśādigrāse rasākāram āha yadītyādi ।।
yadi cedrasaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśān pramāṇato grāsaṃ grasati hi niścitaṃ tadā daṇḍaṃ dhārayet vastrānna kṣaratītyarthaḥ ।।
punaścatvāriṃśadbhāgapraveśato rasodare iti śeṣaḥ tadā pāyasākāraḥ kvathitadugdhākāro bhavet nibiḍatvāt ।।
tadevāha bhavatītyādi ।।
viṃśadbhāgāt triṃśadbhāgasya jāraṇato jalaukākāro bhavet rasa ityadhyāhāraḥ ।।
punaḥ viṃśatyā viṃśadbhāgajāraṇena avipluṣo bhaved āsanānna calati ।।
punaḥ ṣoḍaśāṃśāt ṣoḍaśāṃśabhāgajāraṇataḥ chedī bhavet kṣurikādibhiḥ chede kṛte pṛthaktvamāpnoti ।।
ataḥ ṣoḍaśabhāgādūrdhvaṃ grāso durjaro bhavet ।।

garbhadrāve nipuṇo jārayati bījaṃ kalāṃśena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha pañcabhirityādi ।।
evaṃ uktaprakāreṇa punargarbhadrāve nipuṇaḥ rasodare abhradhātvādīnāṃ drutikaraṇe pravīṇaḥ pumān kalāṃśena grāsaṃ yojayet ।।
kiṃ kṛtvā pañcabhiḥ pūrvoktaiḥ grāsaiścāru yathā syāttathā ghanasatvamādau jārayitvā pañcabhirgrāsair ghanasatvajāraṇānantaraṃ ṣoḍaśabhāgena bījaṃ jārayedityarthaḥ ।।

Ōnderung von phys Eig von Hg nach jāraṇa
dhūmraściṭiciṭiśabdo maṇḍūkagatistathā sakampaśca ।
niṣkampo bhavati raso vijñātavyo'bhrajīrṇastu ।।
kapilo'tha nirudgārī vipluṣabhāvaṃ ca muñcate sūtaḥ ।
niṣkampo gatirahito vijñātavyo'bhrajīrṇastu ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

abhrakajīrṇarasalakṣaṇam āha dhūmra ityādi ।।
abhrajīrṇarasa evaṃvidho bhavati abhraṃ jīrṇaṃ yasmin sa tathoktaḥ ।।
vahniyogāt prathamaṃ dhūmro dhūmrābho bhavati punaściṭiciṭiśabdo bhavati tato maṇḍūkagatirbhavati punastathā tena prakāreṇa dhṛte sati sakampo bhavati punarvahnau niṣkampaḥ svastho bhavati abhrasatvadrutasya lakṣaṇamiti ।।
tadevāha kapila ityādi ।।
punarevaṃvidho raso'bhrajīrṇo vijñātavyaḥ ।।
kīdṛśaḥ kapilaḥ varṇataḥ nirudgārī sthirabhāvaḥ punaḥ sa raso vipluṣabhāvaṃ cañcalatvaṃ muñcate ।।
punarniṣkampaḥ svasthaḥ punargatirahitaḥ pakṣacchinnaḥ iti lakṣaṇānyabhrajīrṇasya bhavanti ।।

kacchapayantra
jalapūrṇapātramadhye dattvā ghaṭakharparaṃ suvistīrṇam ।
tadupari madhyagataḥ sūtaḥ sthāpyastataḥ kuḍye ।।
laghulohakaṭorikayā kṛtapaṭamṛtsandhilepayācchādya ।
pūrṇaṃ tadghaṭakharparam aṅgāraiḥ karīṣatuṣamiśraiḥ ।।
svedanato mardanataḥ kacchapayantrasthito raso jarati ।
agnibalenaiva tato garbhadrutiḥ sarvalohānām ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

kacchapayantramāha jaletyādi ।।
jalapūrṇapātramadhye iti jalapūrṇaṃ yatpātraṃ tasya madhye suvistīrṇaṃ sundarāyataṃ ghaṭakharparaṃ kumbhakhaṇḍaṃ dattvā tadupari kharparopari biḍamadhyagataḥ sūtaḥ sthāpyaḥ ।।
kutra kuḍye mṛdā vinirmite viśālamukhe laghulohakaṭorikayā atilaghvī yā lohasya muṇḍādeḥ kaṭorikā pātraviśeṣaḥ tayā viḍāvṛtaṃ sūtaṃ ācchādya ā samantāt saṃrudhya ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭayā kṛtapaṭamṛtsandhilepayā kṛtaḥ paṭamṛdbhyāṃ sandherlepo rodho yasyāḥ sā tayā ।।
punastatkuḍyāntargataghaṭakharparaṃ aṅgāraiḥ pūrṇaṃ kiṃviśiṣṭaiḥ karīṣatuṣamiśraiḥ karīṣo gomayasya cūrṇaṃ tuṣāḥ śālyāderdhānyasya tair miśritairiti ।।
kacchapayantre yadvihitaṃ tadāha svedanata ityādi ।।
kacchapayantrastho raso jarati grāsaṃ iti śeṣaḥ ।।
kutaḥ svedanataḥ vahnau paritāpataḥ ।।
na kevalaṃ svedanato mardanataśca viḍādinā ityadhyāhāraḥ ।।
tato agnibalenaiva sarvalohānāṃ svarṇādīnāṃ asminnantarāle garbhadrutirbhavati atrāgnibalameva mukhyaṃ ।।

evaṃ dattvā jīryati na kṣayati raso yathā tathā kāryaḥ ।
kṣayameti kṣāraviḍaiḥ sa tūparasairgrāsamudgirati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

jāraṇāyāṃ vidhidvayamāha evamityādi ।।
evamamunā prakāreṇa kacchapayantre nidhāya jīryati grāsaṃ rasa iti śeṣaḥ ।।
yathā raso na kṣayati kṣayaṃ nāpnoti tathā kāryo vidhiḥ iti śeṣaḥ ।।
kāryasyāśrayarakṣaṇāyeti bhāvaḥ ।।
punaḥ kṣārabiḍaiḥ kṣayameti nāśamāpnoti grāsa ityadhyāhāraḥ ।।
punaḥ sa rasa uparasairgandhādibhiḥ grāsaṃ utprāvalyena girati gilatītyarthaḥ ।।
kṣārairamlaiśca gandhādyair mūtraiḥ paṭubhireva ca ।
rasagrāsasya jīrṇārthaṃ biḍaḥ sa parikīrtitaḥ ।
iti paribhāṣā ।।
biḍaśabdena piṇḍaḥ ।।

viḍa positive effects

grāsaṃ na muñcati na vāñchati taṃ ca bhūyaḥ kāṃścidguṇānbhajati bhuktavibhuktimātrāt ।
yajjīryate pracurakevalavahniyogāt tasmādviḍaiḥ suniviḍaiḥ saha jāraṇā syāt ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

biḍairjāraṇāyāḥ sugamatvamāha grāsamityādi ।।
grāsaṃ na muñcati ca punastam evānyagrāsaṃ na vāñchati bhūyaḥ punaḥ bhuktavibhuktimātrāt kāṃścidguṇān nityaṃ bhajati dadhāti grāsagrasanamātrāt guṇaṃ karotītyarthaḥ ।।
yato hetorbiḍairvakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇaiḥ kṛtvā jīryate grāsamityarthaḥ ।।
kutaḥ pracurakevalavahniyogāt pracura udagro yaḥ kevalavahniyogaḥ śuddhāgniyogastasmāt ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaiḥ sunibiḍaiḥ ghanaiḥ ।।
yato biḍāḥ śreṣṭhās tasmādviḍair eva jāraṇā syāt sugamatvāditi bhāvaḥ ।।

viḍa for jāraṇa of copper leafs
sauvarcalakaṭukatrayakākṣīkāsīsagandhakaiśca viḍaiḥ ।
śigro rasaśatabhāvyaistāmradalānyapi jārayati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

biḍavidhānamāha sauvarcaletyādi ।।
tāmradalānyapi jārayati buddhimān iti śeṣaḥ svarṇabījādīnāṃ kā katheti bhāvaḥ ।।
kaiḥ kṛtvā biḍaiḥ kṛtvā ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭair biḍaiḥ sauvarcalakaṭukatrayakāṃkṣīkāsīsagandhakaiḥ sauvarcalaṃ rucakaṃ kaṭutrayaṃ śuṇṭhīmaricapippalyātmakaṃ kākṣī saurāṣṭrī kāsīsaṃ puṣpakāsīsaṃ gandhakaṃ lelitakaṃ etānyauṣadhāni yeṣu viḍeṣu santi te tathoktāḥ taiḥ ।।
punaḥ kiṃviśiṣṭaiḥ śigro rasaśatabhāvyaiḥ śigroḥ saubhāñjanasya rasena śatavāraṃ bhāvyāḥ ye biḍāstaiḥ evaṃ niṣpannairviḍairniścitaṃ jāraṇā syāditi bhāvaḥ ।।

viḍa for jāraṇa of gold
sarvāṅgadagdhamūlakabhasma pratigālitaṃ surabhimūtreṇa ।
śatabhāvyaṃ balivasayā tatkṣaṇato jāryate hema ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

biḍāntaramāha sarvetyādi ।।
sarvāṅgadagdhamūlakabhasma pratigālitamiti sarvāṅgena mūlatvakpatrapuṣpaphalena saha dagdhaṃ bhasmatāṃ prāptaṃ yanmūlakakandaṃ tadbhasma surabhimūtreṇa gojalena gālitaṃ kāryaṃ kṣāro grāhya ityarthaḥ ।।
punarbalivasayā balamukhyā yā jalaukā maṇḍūkādīnāṃ vasā yathā ca ।
bhekamatsyavasā yā tu kukkuṭasya vasāthavā ।

ekā balivasā samyak sūtasya bandhinī param ।
rañjanaṃ caiva kurute maṇimūṣāvidhikramāt ।
iti ।।
balivasayā śataṃ śatavāraṃ kṣārabhūtaṃ bhasma bhāvyaṃ punaḥ tacchatabhāvyam auṣadhaṃ tatkṣaṇataḥ tatkālato hema svarṇaṃ jāryate raso grāsabhūtaṃ hema jaratīti biḍayogāditi bhāvaḥ ।।

viḍa for jāraṇa
kadalīpalāśatilaniculakanakasuradālivāstukairaṇḍāḥ ।
varṣābhūvṛṣamokṣakasahitāḥ kṣāro yathālābham ।।
ānīya kṣāravṛkṣān kusumaphalaśiphātvakpravālairupetān kṛtvātaḥ khaṇḍaśastān vipulataraśilāpiṣṭagātrātiśuṣkān ।
dagdhvā kāṇḍaistilānāṃ karisurabhihayāmbhobhir āsrāvya vastrair bhasma tyaktvā jalaṃ tanmṛduśikhini pacedvaṃśapākena bhūyaḥ ।।
tacchuṣyamāṇaṃ hi sabāṣpabudbudān yadā vidhatte kṣaṇabhaṅgurān bahūn ।
tadā kṣipettryūṣaṇahiṃgugandhakaṃ kṣāratrayaṃ ṣaḍlavaṇāni bhūkhagau ।।
dravyāṇi saṃmiśrya nivṛtya bhūtale vyavasthitaṃ śastrakaṭorikāpuṭe ।
saṃsthāpayetsaptadināni dhānyagataṃ prayojyaṃ rasajāraṇādikam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha kṣāravṛkṣagulmauṣadhiviśeṣānāha kadalītyādi ।।
yathālābhaṃ lābham anatikramya eṣāṃ kṣāraḥ kartavyaḥ ।।
te ke kadalīpalāśatilaniculakanakasuradālivāstukairaṇḍāḥ kadalī rambhā palāśo brahmavṛkṣaḥ tilāḥ pratītāḥ niculo vetasavṛkṣaḥ kanako dhattūraḥ suradālī devadālī vāstukaṃ kṣāraśākaṃ eraṇḍo vātāriḥ ete kṣārasaṃbhavāḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭā ete varṣābhūvṛṣamokṣakasahitāḥ varṣābhūḥ punarnavā vṛṣo vāsakaḥ mokṣako mokhāvṛkṣa iti pratītaḥ etaiḥ saṃyutā ityuddeśaḥ ।।
kṣārakaraṇavidhānam āhānīyetyādi ।।
prathamaṃ kṣāravṛkṣān pūrvoktān ānīya vanāntarādgṛhītvā ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭān kusumaphalaśiphātvakpalāśairupetān kusumāni prasūnāni pratītāni śiphā mūlaṃ tvaktvacā pravālā nūtanapallavāḥ etaiḥ pañcāṅgāhvayair upetān saṃyutān ।।
khaṇḍaśaḥ bahuśakalān kṛtvā ।।
na kevalaṃ khaṇḍaśaḥ vipulataraśilāpiṣṭagātrātiśuṣkān kṛtvā vipulatarā ativistīrṇā yā śilā tasyāṃ piṣṭāni gātrāṇi yeṣāṃ te'śuṣkā nirasāḥ tānevaṃvidhān kṛtvā ।।
punastāneva ca tilānāṃ kāṇḍairnālaiḥ saha dagdhvā ।।
punaḥ karisurabhihayāmbhobhiḥ hastigo'śvānāṃ mūtrairāsrāvya āplutya tadbhasma tyaktvā vastrair jalaṃ grāhyamiti śeṣaḥ ।।
tajjalaṃ mṛduśikhini komalāgnau pacet kena vaṃśapākena vaṃśānāṃ samavahnitvāt ।।
kṣārajalapākalakṣaṇamāha tadityādi ।।
tajjalaṃ kṣārapānīyaṃ śuṣyamāṇaṃ sat niścitaṃ yadā sabāṣpabudbudān vidhatte saha bāṣpeṇa jalātyayadhūmena vartante ye budbudāstān tadā kṣāro niṣpanno jñeyaḥ ।।
punastadā tryūṣaṇaṃ śuṇṭhīmaricapippalyaḥ hiṅgu rāmaṭhaṃ gandhakaṃ lelītakaṃ punaḥ kṣāratrayaṃ sarjikāyavāgrajaṭaṅkaṇāhvayaṃ lavaṇāni ṣaṭ saindhavādīni bhūḥ tuvarī khagaṃ kāsīsaṃ etāni kṣipet etatkṣāreṇārdreṇa saha miśraṃ kāryamityarthaḥ ।।
tathā ca dravyāṇi tryūṣaṇādīni saṃmiśrya ekīkṛtya nivṛtya ca saṃmardya śastrakaṭorikāpuṭe lohamayapātrasaṃpuṭe vyavasthitaṃ saptadināni dhānyagataṃ kasyaciddhānyasya madhyagataṃ sthāpayet kutra bhūtale pṛthivyā āsthāne tato'nantaraṃ tatsiddhaṃ rasajāraṇādikaṃ prati prayojyaṃ etadbiḍarūpaṃ rasajāraṇādiṣu praśastamityarthaḥ ।।

viḍa for garbhadruti
jambīrabījapūrakacāṅgerīvetasāmlasaṃyogāt ।
kṣārā bhavanti nitarāṃ garbhadrutijāraṇe śastāḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

jāraṇāyāṃ kṣāravidhānamāha jambīretyādi ।।
kṣārā uktavṛkṣodbhavāḥ nitarām atiśayena garbhadrutijāraṇe rasāntargrāsajāraṇe śastā utkṛṣṭā bhavanti ।।
kutaḥ jambīrabījapūrakacāṅgerīvetasāmlasaṃyogāt jambīraḥ pratītaḥ bījapūrako mātuluṅgaḥ cāṅgerī amlapatrikā vetasāmlaṃ cukrakaṃ eṣāṃ yo rasastasya saṃyogāt etairbhāvitāḥ kṣārā biḍavatkāryakarā iti bhāvaḥ ।।

viḍa how to use
viḍamadharottaramādau dattvā sūtasya cāṣṭamāṃśena ।
kuryājjāraṇamevaṃ kramakramādvardhayedagnim ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

rase viḍayojanamāha biḍamityādi ।।
ādau prathamaṃ sūtasya rasasyāṣṭamāṃśena pūrvanirmitaṃ viḍaṃ adharottaraṃ adha uparibhāgaṃ ca dattvā evaṃ amunā prakāreṇa jāraṇaṃ kuryāt punaḥ kramyate aneneti kramo biḍarūpaḥ tatkramaḥ paraṃparā tasmāt agniṃ vivardhayet karmakṛt ityadhyāhāraḥ vāraṃvāraṃ biḍasaṃprayogādagnirvardhate ।।

rañjana colour acc to abhra

jīrṇābhrako rasendro darśayati ghanānurūpiṇīṃ chāyām ।
kṛṣṇāṃ raktāṃ pītāṃ sitāṃ tathā saṃkarairmiśrām ।।
kṛṣṇābhrakeṇa balavadasitarāgairyujyate rasendrastu ।
śvetai raktaiḥ pītairvahneḥ khalu varṇato jñeyaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

dyotate divi candro asau jīrṇe'bhre kāntimattayā ।
tatheha tāmupāśritya śālate manujeṣu ca ।।
susiddhabiḍadhātvādijāraṇena rasasya hi ।
pītādirāgajananaṃ rañjanaṃ parikīrtitam ।
iti paribhāṣā ।।
abhrasya chāyāviśeṣam āha jīrṇābhraka ityādi ।।
rasendro yadā jīrṇābhro bhavati tadā ghanānurūpiṇīṃ jīrṇābhrasamavarṇāṃ chāyāṃ darśayati ।।
kṛṣṇe jīrṇe kṛṣṇāṃ rakte'bhre jīrṇe raktāṃ pīte pītāṃ tathā site śubhre sitāṃ evaṃ caturvidhāṃ chāyāṃ darśayati ।।
punardvayostrayāṇāṃ vā caturṇāṃ saṃkare melāpe sati dvitricaturṇām anurūpiṇīṃ chāyāṃ darśayatītyarthaḥ ।।
abhrayogād varṇaviśeṣamāha kṛṣṇetyādi ।।
kṛṣṇābhrakeṇa jīrṇena raso balavān bhavet tu punaḥ asitarāgaiḥ kṛṣṇarāgairyujyate ।।
tathā śvetena śvetai rāgair yujyate raktena raktaiḥ pītena pītaiḥ kapilāgnerdivyasyāpi sarvasyādarśanarūpaṃ kṣayakarasya balairdravyāṇāṃ tādṛśo varṇo rasavarṇato varṇakovidairjñeyaḥ ।।

mercury transfers own colour on other substances
atha nijakarme varṇaṃ na jahāti yadā sa rajyate rāgaiḥ ।
kramaśo hi vakṣyamāṇairnirṇikto raṃjanaṃ kurute ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

rañjitarasapraśaṃsām āha athetyādi ।।
athānantaraṃ rasaḥ rasendro yadā vakṣyamāṇaiḥ śvetādibhiḥ rāgaiḥ rajyate tadā nijakarme varṇaṃ svakīyameva svābhāvikaṃ rūpaṃ na jahāti na tyajati punastaireva rāgaiḥ nirṇikto raktaḥ san rañjanaṃ kurute rāgadāyī bhavatīti ।।
tathā no rakto na rañjanaṃ kurute avidyamānatvānniṣedhaḥ ।।

balamāste'bhrakasatve jāraṇarāgāḥ pratiṣṭhitāstīkṣṇe ।
bandhaśca sāralohe sārakamatha nāgavaṃgābhyām ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

abhrasatvādīnāṃ yoge rase vyavasthāmāha balamityādi ।।
abhrakasatve'dhikaraṇe balamāste abhrasatvasaṃyogena raso balamāpnotītyarthaḥ ।।
punastīkṣṇe lohabhede jāraṇarāgā jāraṇena tīkṣṇasthā rāgāḥ pratiṣṭhitā bhavantītyarthaḥ ।।
sāraṇamatha nāgavaṅgābhyām iti nāgavaṅgābhyāṃ duḥsaraṇaṃ sāraṇadravyaṃ sarata iti ।।

potency of tīkṣṇaloha
krāmati tīkṣṇena rasastīkṣṇena ca jīryate kṣaṇādgrāsaḥ ।
hemno yonistīkṣṇaṃ rāgān gṛhṇāti tīkṣṇena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sarvakāraṇaṃ tīkṣṇamāha krāmatītyādi ।।
tīkṣṇena lohabhedena rasaḥ krāmati krāmaṇaṃ vidadhāti punas tīkṣṇena kṛtvā grāsaḥ kṣaṇādalpakālato jīryate jāraṇam āpnoti punarhemnaḥ suvarṇasya yonirutpattisthānaṃ tīkṣṇamasti punaḥ rāgān rañjanabhāvān tīkṣṇena kṛtvā raso gṛhṇāti svasmin rāgān dadhātītyarthaḥ ।।

tīkṣṇaloha cāraṇa, jāraṇa
tadapi ca daradena hataṃ kṛtvā mākṣikeṇa ravisahitam ।
vāsitamapi vāsanayā ghanavaccāryaṃ ca jāryaṃ ca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

tīkṣṇasya hiṅgulayogena guṇādhikyamāha tadapītyādi ।।
api niścayena tat tīkṣṇaṃ daradena hiṅgulena hataṃ māritaṃ vā mākṣikena svarṇamākṣikena ravisahitaṃ tāmrasaṃyutaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ hataṃ māritaṃ punarvāsanayā vāsanauṣadhena vāsitaṃ paribhāvitaṃ ghanavad abhravat cāryaṃ jāryaṃ ca satvābhravat nānyathā ।।

rañjana suitable substances
kāntaṃ vā tīkṣṇaṃ vā kāñcīṃ vā vajrasasyakādīnām ।
ekatamaṃ sarvaṃ vā rasaraṃjane saṃkaro'bhīṣṭaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

tīkṣṇavadetānāha kāntam ityādi ।।
rasarañjane rasendre rāgakarmaṇi kāntaṃ cumbakapāṣāṇotthaṃ lohaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ veti samuccaye tīkṣṇaṃ lohabhedo vā kāñcīṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ vā vajrasasyakādīnāṃ vajrasasyakāvādiryeṣāṃ te teṣāṃ hīrakacapalādīnāṃ ekatamaṃ tanmadhyādekatamaṃ sarvaṃ vā atrābhīṣṭaśabdasya pratyekaṃ saṃbandhaḥ hīrakādīni ratnāni sasyakādyā upadhātavaḥ ।।
vā rasarañjane ayameva saṃkaraḥ sarveṣāṃ kāntādīnāṃ melāpaḥ sarvatrābhīṣṭaḥ ।।

kuṭile balamabhyadhikaṃ rāgastīkṣṇe tu pannage snehaḥ ।
rāgasnehabalāni tu kamale śaṃsanti dhātuvidaḥ ।।
mercury rañjana
sarvair ebhir lohair mākṣikanihataistathā drutairgarbhe ।
viḍayogena tu jīrṇo rasarājo rāgamupayāti ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sve sve vikāre vakṣyamāṇamāha balamityādi ।।
dhātuvido rasavaidyā iti śaṃsanti ।।
iti kiṃ kuṭile balaṃ abhyadhikaṃ sarvādhikaṃ punastīkṣṇe'bhyadhiko rāgaḥ rañjanaṃ tu punaḥ pannage nāge'bhyadhikaṃ snehaḥ snigdhatvaṃ tu punaḥ rāgasnehabalāni trīṇyevoktāni kamale tāmre kuṭilatīkṣṇapannagānāṃ jāraṇādrase yathā balarāgasnehā bhavanti tathaikatāmrajāraṇāt trayo bhavantītyarthaḥ ।।
rasabandhanopāyamāha sarvairityādi ।।
biḍayogena pūrvoktena jīrṇo jāraṇamāpanno rasarājo bandhamupayāti bandhanamādatte ।।
kaiḥ saha jīrṇaḥ ebhiḥ pūrvoktaiḥ sarvair lohairdhātubhiḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaiḥ mākṣikanihataiḥ svarṇamākṣikamāritaiḥ ।।
punaḥ kiṃviśiṣṭaiḥ garbhe rasodare drutairvidrutairiti ।।

mercury rañjana 
tālakadaradaśilābhiḥ snehakṣārāmlalavaṇasahitābhiḥ ।
samakadviguṇatriguṇān puṭo vahedvaṃgaśastrādīn ।।
raktasnehaniṣekaiḥ śeṣaṃ kuryādrasasya kṛṣṭiriyam ।
cāraṇajāraṇamātrātkurute rasamindragopanibham ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vakṣyamāṇadhātūnāṃ māraṇavidhānamāha tālaketyādi ।।
vaṅgaśastrādīn vaṅgaṃ trapuṣaṃ śastraṃ tīkṣṇaṃ te ādiryeṣāṃ te tān ।।
kābhiḥ saha puṭo vahet tālakadaradaśilābhiḥ tālakaṃ haritālaṃ daradaṃ hiṅgulaṃ śilā manaḥśilā tābhiḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭābhiḥ snehakṣārāmlalavaṇasahitābhiḥ snehaḥ tailaṃ kaṅguṇitumbinyādīnāṃ kṣāraḥ svarjikādiḥ amlaṃ jambīrādi lavaṇāni saindhavādīni etaiḥ sahitābhiḥ ।।
ekadhātuto dvādaśāṃśād ārabhya yāvatsamakadviguṇatriguṇabhāgāḥ samāpyante tāvatpuṭo vahediti vyaktiḥ ।।
puṭitadhātukṛtyam āha raktetyādi ।।
uktadhāturgarbhitaṃ rasaṃ raktasnehaniṣekaiḥ rakto raktavargaḥ snehaḥ kaṅguṇyādīnāṃ anayorniṣekāḥ siñcanāni taiḥ śeṣaṃ dhātuvarjitaṃ kuryāt iyaṃ rasasya kṛṣṭiḥ rasasya guṇākarṣaṇaṃ punariyaṃ kṛṣṭiḥ rasendraṃ indragopanibhaṃ kurute atiriktavarṇaṃ kurute ।।
kutaḥ cāraṇajāraṇamātrāt punaḥ puṭitadhātūnāṃ cāraṇaṃ ca jāraṇaṃ jīrṇaṃkaraṇaṃ ca tanmātrāt vā cāraṇasya dravyasya jāraṇaṃ tanmātrāt ubhayoḥ pakṣayoreka evārthaḥ paramuktiviśeṣaḥ ।।

mercury rañjana
athavā kevalam amalaṃ kamalaṃ daradena vāpitaṃ kurute ।
triguṇaṃ hi cīrṇajīrṇaṃ lākṣārasasannibhaṃ sūtam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

mukhyatvena tāmrapraṃśasanam āha athavetyādi ।।
athaveti vidhānāntare kevalaṃ śuddhaṃ vānyasaṃyogena varjitaṃ amalaṃ jātapūrvaśodhanaṃ triguṇaṃ cīrṇajīrṇaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ pūrvaṃ cīrṇaṃ cāraṇamāptaṃ paścājjīrṇaṃ jāraṇamāpannaṃ evaṃbhūtaṃ tāmraṃ sūtaṃ lākṣārasasannibhaṃ alaktakaprabhaṃ kurute ।।

mercury rañjana
raktagaṇagalitapaśujalabhāvitatāpyagandhakaśilānām ।
ekena vāpitamṛtaṃ kamalaṃ rañjayati rasarājam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha raktetyādi ।।
raktagaṇena dāḍimakiṃśukabandhūkādinā pūrvoktena galitaṃ yat paśujalaṃ gomūtraṃ tena bhāvitā yās tāpyagandhakamanaḥśilās tāsāṃ madhyād ekena tāpyena svarṇamākṣikena vā gandhakena vā śilayā vāpitamṛtaṃ sat kamalaṃ tāmraṃ rasaṃ rañjayati rāgaṃ dadātītyarthaḥ ।।

duration of colouring acc to substance
bāhyo gandhakarāgo vilulitarāge manaḥśilātāle ।
mākṣikasatvarasakau dvāveva hi rañjane śastau ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

rāgādhikārigandhakādīn āha ।।
tatra gandhakaḥ kīdṛśaṃ rāgaṃ dadāti tatsvarūpamāha bāhya ityādi ।।
gandhakarāgo bāhyo bahirbhavaḥ punarmanaḥśilātāle manaḥśilā manohvā tālaṃ haritālaṃ tāvubhe vilulitarāge cañcalarāge punar mākṣikasatvarasakau svarṇamākṣikasatvakharparikau dvāveva rañjane rasarāge śastau gandhakamanaḥśilātālebhyaḥ pradhānau atyadhikāvityarthaḥ ।।

rasarañjak 
kramavṛttau ravirasakau saṃśuddhau mūkamūṣikādhmātau ।
triguṇaṃ cīrṇo jīrṇo hemābho jāyate sūtaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

pradhānayostāmrakharparayoḥ kṛtyamāha kramavṛttāvityādi ।।
kramavṛttau ravirasakau saṃśuddhau viśeṣavidhānena śodhitau vā uttamajātīyau mūkamūṣikādhmātau andhamūṣāyāṃ dhmātau vahniyogīkṛtau kāryau etattriguṇaṃ yathā syāttathā cīrṇo jīrṇaśca sūtaḥ hemanibho jāyate etena cāraṇamāpannaḥ paścāttenaiva jāraṇām āpanno rasaḥ svarṇaprabho bhavedityarthaḥ ।।

rasarañjak 
atha kṛṣṇābhrakacūrṇaṃ puṭitaṃ raktaṃ bhavettathā sakalam ।
triguṇaṃ cīrṇo jīrṇo hemadrutisannibhaḥ sūtaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

abhrakayogamāha athetyādi ।।
atha rasakayogānantaraṃ kṛṣṇavarṇābhrakacūrṇaṃ śyāmavarṇābhrakarajaḥ tathā ravirasakavidhānena kharparakeṇa sahitaṃ puṭitaṃ sat sakalaṃ samastaṃ raktaṃ bhavet tadraktabhūtamabhraṃ triguṇaṃ yathā syāttathā cīrṇaḥ cāraṇamāpannas tato jīrṇo jāraṇamāpannaśca san sūto hemadrutisannibhaḥ svarṇadravasadṛśo bhaved ityarthaḥ ।।

mercury rañjana
triguṇena mākṣikeṇa tu kanakaṃ ca mṛtaṃ rasakatālayutam ।
paṭusahitaṃ tatpakvaṃ haṇḍikayā yāvadindragopanibham ।।
taccūrṇaṃ sūtavare triguṇaṃ cīrṇaṃ hi jīrṇaṃ tu ।
drutahemanibhaḥ sūto rañjati lohāni sarvāṇi ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha svarṇamāraṇamāha triguṇenetyādi ।।
tu punaḥ triguṇena mākṣikeṇa svarṇatriguṇitena tāpyena yatkanakaṃ mṛtaṃ tatkanakaṃ indragopako varṣākālīno raktavarṇo jīvaviśeṣaḥ tadvannibhā dīptiryasya tadindragopanibhaṃ bhavatīti śeṣaḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ kanakaṃ mṛtaṃ rasakatālayutaṃ rasakaṃ kharparaṃ tālaṃ haritālaṃ tābhyāṃ yutaṃ miśritaṃ sat yanmṛtaṃ pañcatvamāptamityarthaḥ ।।
punaḥ paṭusahitaṃ lavaṇamiśritaṃ punar haṇḍikayā bhājanena pakvaṃ vahnipuṭitaṃ tadapi pūrvavat ।।
mṛtakanakacūrṇaṃ sūtavare pārade triguṇaṃ cīrṇaṃ jīrṇaṃ cāritaṃ jāritaṃ ca sat sūto drutahemanibho bhavet galitasvarṇaprabha ityarthaḥ ।।
evaṃ rañjito rasaḥ sarvalohāni dhātūni kṛtrimākṛtrimāni navavidhāni rañjati svarṇarūpāṇi karotītyarthaḥ ।।

bījjāraṇ kā mahattv
patrādaṣṭaguṇaṃ satvaṃ satvādaṣṭaguṇā drutiḥ ।
druteraṣṭaguṇaṃ bījaṃ tasmādbījaṃ tu jārayet ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sarveṣāṃ dhāturasānāmuttarottaraṃ viśeṣatvam āha patrādityādi ।।
patrādaṣṭaguṇaṃ satvaṃ abhrapatre jīrṇe sati rase yo guṇastasmādaṣṭaguṇo guṇastatsatve ityarthaḥ punaḥ sattvāt drutistaddravarūpā aṣṭaguṇā punardruter bījaṃ dhātūparasasaṃyogajanitaṃ pūrvopavarṇitaṃ tadaṣṭaguṇaṃ tataḥ sarvotkṛṣṭatvādbījaṃ jārayennatvanyat ।।

bīja 

iti rakto'pi rasendro bījena vinā na karmakṛdbhavati ।
dvividhaṃ tatpītasitaṃ niyujyate siddhamevaitat ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

himāṃśuriva dīptyāsau caṇḍāṃśuriva tejasā ।
niśāhnoriva kartā ca durjanaiḥ sahanālayaḥ ।।
nirvāpaṇaviśeṣeṇa tadvadvarṇaṃ bhavedyadā ।
mṛdulaṃ citrasaṃskāraṃ tadbījamiti kathyate ।।
iti paribhāṣā ।।
bījapraśaṃsanamāha itītyādi ।।
ityuktavidhānena rakto'pi rasendro bījena vinā karmakṛnna bhavati bījenaiva karmakārī syādityarthaḥ ।।
tadbījaṃ dvividhaṃ dviprakāraṃ pītasitaṃ ekaṃ pītaṃ aparaṃ sitaṃ śvetaṃ svarṇarūpyakriyāyogyam ityarthaḥ ।।
tadbījaṃ siddhaṃ sarvalakṣaṇopetaṃ rase pārade niyojyaṃ nāsiddhamiti ।।

bīja śodhana necessary
tasya viśuddhirbahudhā gaganarasoparasalohacūrṇaiś ca ।
dvividhaṃ bījaṃ tairapi nāśuddhaiḥ śudhyate vai tat ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī
tasyetyādi ।।
tasya bījasya viśuddhiḥ śodhanaṃ bahudhā bahuprakāraiḥ kṛtvā rasoparasadhātūnāṃ bahuvidhatvāt ।।
kaiḥ kṛtvā gaganarasalohacūrṇaiḥ gaganamabhraṃ rasā vaikrāntādayo'ṣṭau vakṣyamāṇāḥ uparasā gandhakādayaḥ lohā dhātavaḥ teṣāṃ cūrṇāni taiḥ ।।
ca punaḥ tair gaganarasoparasalohacūrṇair aśuddhaiḥ śuddhivarjitaistadbījaṃ na śudhyate śuddhihīnaṃ syāt kāraṇānurūpaṃ kāryamitinyāyāt ।।

yaḥ punaretaiḥ kurute karmāśuddhairbhavedrasastasya ।
avyāpakaḥ pataṃgī na rase rasāyane yogyaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

aśuddhabījaprabhāvamāha ya ityādi ।।
punarviśeṣeṇa yaḥ saṃskārakṛdetairgaganādyair aśuddhaiḥ kṛtvā rasasya karma kurute tasya puruṣasya rasaḥ pārado avyāpako asaraṇaśīlo bhavet pataṅgī ūrdhvagāmī ca bhavet yantrasyādhobhāge na tiṣṭhatītyarthaḥ ।।

mahārasa
vaikrāntakāntasasyakamākṣikavimalādridaradarasakāśca ।
aṣṭau rasāstathaiṣāṃ sattvāni rasāyanāni syuḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

ete vakṣyamāṇā aṣṭau rasāḥ rasasaṃjñakāḥ syuḥ ।।
ete ke vaikrāntakāntasasyakamākṣikavimalādridaradarasakāś ceti vaikrāntaṃ vajrabhūmijaṃ rajaḥ kāntaṃ cumbakotthaṃ sasyakaṃ capalaṃ mākṣikaṃ tāpyaṃ vimalā raupyamākṣikaṃ adri śilājatu daradaṃ hiṅgulaṃ rasakaḥ kharparikaḥ ete rasasaṃjñikā jñeyāḥ ।।
tathā eṣāṃ satvāni sārāṇi rasāyanāni jarāvyādhināśanāni syuriti ।।

uparasa
gandhakagairikaśilālakṣitikhecaramañjanaṃ ca kaṃkuṣṭham ।

uparasasaṃjñakānāha gandhaketyādi ।।
idaṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ uparasasaṃjñakaṃ syāt ।।
kimidaṃ gandhakagairikaśilālakṣitikhecaram iti gandhakaṃ pratītaṃ gairikaṃ dhātugairikaṃ śilā manohvā ālaṃ haritālaṃ kṣitiḥ sphaṭikā khecaraṃ kāsīsaṃ etat sarvamiti ca punaḥ añjanaṃ nīlāñjanaṃ punaḥ kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ viraṅgaṃ ityaṣṭau uparasasaṃjñakā ityarthaḥ ।।

sāraloha
uparasasaṃjñakamidaṃ syāt śikhiśaśinau sāralohākhyau ।।
pūtiloha
tāmrāratīkṣṇakāntābhrasattvalohāni vaṅganāgau ca ।
kathitāstu pūtisaṃjñāsteṣāṃ saṃśodhanaṃ kāryam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

śikhiśaśinau svarṇatārakau sāralohākhyau sāralohasaṃjñakāvityarthaḥ ।।
pūtilohasaṃjñānāha tāmretyādi ।।
tāmrāratīkṣṇakāntābhrasatvalohānīti tāmraṃ nepālakaṃ āraṃ rājarītiḥ tīkṣṇaṃ sāraṃ kāntaṃ cumbakodbhavaṃ abhrasatvaṃ gaganasāraṃ lohaṃ muṇḍaṃ etānīti punarvaṅganāgau ete pūtisaṃjñakāḥ kathitāḥ ।।
teṣāṃ pūtilohasaṃjñakānāṃ śodhanaṃ samyaṅmalāpanayanaṃ kāryamiti ।।

ṣaḍlavaṇa
sauvarcalasaindhavakacūlikasāmudraromakabiḍāni ।

lavaṇakṣārasaṃjñe āha sauvarcaletyādi ।।
etāni vakṣyamāṇāni lavaṇasaṃjñānyāhuḥ ācāryāḥ iti śeṣaḥ ।।
kāni sauvarcalasaindhavakacūlikasāmudraromakabiḍānīti sauvarcalaṃ rucakaṃ saindhavaṃ maṇikamanthāhvayaṃ cūlikaṃ kācalavaṇaṃ sāmudraṃ kṣārābdhijaṃ romakaṃ pratītaṃ biḍaṃ lavaṇaviśeṣaḥ etānīti ।।

trikṣāra
ṣaṭ lavaṇānyetāni tu svarjīṭaṅkaṇayavakṣārāḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

punaḥ svarjī sarjikā ṭaṅkaṇaṃ saubhāgyaṃ yavakṣāraḥ pratītaḥ ete kṣārāḥ kṣārasaṃjñikāḥ rasakarmaṇi ityadhyāhāraḥ ।।

uparasa śodhana, sattvapātana
sūryāvartaḥ kadalī vandhyā kośātakī ca suradālī ।
śigruśca vajrakando nīrakaṇā kākamācī ca ।।
āsāmekarasena tu lavaṇakṣārāmlabhāvitā bahuśaḥ ।
śudhyanti rasoparasā dhmātāḥ sattvāni muñcanti ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sadrāvakaṃ śodhakagaṇamāha sūryāvarta ityādi ।।
sūryaṃ prati āvartako bhramaṇaṃ yasyetyevaṃvidhaḥ kadalī rambhā vandhyā phalarahitā karkoṭī kośātakī jālinī suradālī devadālī śigruḥ saubhāñjanaṃ vajrakando vadasūraṇakandaḥ nīrakaṇā jalapippalī kākamācī vāyasī iti gaṇaḥ śodhanadrāvaṇayogya iti ।।
śodhanadrāvakāṇāṃ śodhanadrāvaṇavidhānam āha āsāmityādi ।।
āsāṃ pūrvauṣadhīnāṃ madhyāt ekarasena ekasyā rasena rasoparasā vaikrāntādayo'ṣṭau rasāḥ gandhakādayo aṣṭāvuparasāḥ bahuśo'nekavāraṃ bhāvitā gharmapuṭitāḥ kāryāḥ punarlavaṇakṣārāmlabhāvitāśca lavaṇāni sauvarcalādīni ṣaṭ kṣārāḥ svarjikādayaḥ amlā jambīrādayaḥ tairbahuvāraṃ bhāvitās tīvragharmapuṭitā rasoparasāḥ śudhyanti doṣavarjitā bhavanti punaste dhmātāḥ santaḥ satvāni svīyasārāṇi muñcanti tyajantīti ।।

vaikrānta śodhana
svinnaṃ sakṣārāmlairdhmātaṃ vaikrāntakaṃ haṭhād dravati ।

rasānāṃ krameṇa śodhanamāha svinnamityādi ।।
sakṣārāmlairvaikrāntakaṃ svinnaṃ dolābhidhānena sveditaṃ kuryāt tat svinnaṃ vaikrāntaṃ haṭhāt prābalyāt dhmātaṃ sat dravati sāraṃ muñcati drutamātraṃ satvanirgamamātrameva śudhyati pūrvasaṃbandhāt dravati ।।

kānta śodhana
tad drutamātraṃ śudhyati kāntaṃ śaśaraktabhāvanayā ।।
sasyaka śodhana
sasyakamapi raktagaṇaiḥ subhāvitaṃ sneharāgasaṃsiktam ।
śudhyati vāraiḥ saptabhirataḥ paraṃ yujyate kārye ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha sasyakamityādi ।।
sasyakamapi capalamapi raktagaṇairdāḍimakiṃśukabandhūkādibhiḥ subhāvitaṃ kuryāt ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ sneharāgasaṃsiktaṃ snehaḥ kaṅguṇitumbunyādīnāṃ rāgo raktavarṇadravaḥ tābhyāṃ vahnau taptaṃ sasyakaṃ saṃsiktaṃ secitamiti ghṛtaiḥ saṃsiktaṃ komalaṃ bhāvanāyogyaṃ syāt ।।
katibhirvāraiḥ subhāvitaṃ kuryāt saptabhiḥ saptasaṃkhyākaiḥ ।।
ataḥ paraṃ kārye bījādike yujyate ।।

vimala, rasaka, darada, mākṣika śodhana
kṣāraiḥ snehairādau paścādamlena bhāvitaṃ vimalam ।
śudhyati tathā ca rasakaṃ daradaṃ mākṣikamapyevam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha kṣārairityādi ।।
vimalaṃ raupyamākṣikaṃ ādau prathamaṃ kṣāraiḥ svarjikādibhiḥ snehaistailaiḥ kaṅguṇyādīnāṃ bhāvitaṃ kuryāt paścādamlena jambīrādinā bhāvitaṃ kuryāt evaṃvidhaṃ kṛtaṃ sat śudhyati ।।
tathā tenaiva vidhinā rasakaṃ kharparakaṃ śudhyati daradaṃ hiṅgulaṃ caivaṃ mākṣikamapyeva śudhyati ।।

copper rañjana, śodhana
tanurapi patraṃ liptaṃ lavaṇakṣārāmlaravisnuhikṣīraiḥ ।
dhmātaṃ nirguṇḍīrasasaṃsiktaṃ bahuśo bhaveddhi raktaṃ ca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

svarṇarūpyayoḥ śodhanamāha tanurityādi ।।
lavaṇetyādi ।।
lavaṇāni sauvarcalādīni kṣārāḥ svarjikādayaḥ amlāḥ jambīrādayaḥ ravirarkaḥ snuhī sudhā tayoḥ kṣīrāṇi etaiḥ tanurapi sūkṣmamapi patraṃ dalaṃ sāralohākhyayoḥ iti śeṣaḥ liptaṃ dhmātaṃ sat bahuśo'nekavāraṃ nirguṇḍīrase saṃsiktaṃ śephālīdrave siñcitaṃ kuryāt ।।
tarhi svarṇaṃ rūpyaṃ ca raktaṃ āraktachaviyutaṃ bhavedityarthaḥ caśabdācchudhyati ।।

lead, tin, bronze, copper śodhana
śudhyati nāgo vaṃgo ghoṣo raviṇā ca vāramapi munibhiḥ ।
nirguṇḍīrasasekaistanmūlarajaḥ pravāpaiśca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

lohaśodhanamāha śudhyatītyādi ।।
nāgaḥ sīsakaḥ nirguṇḍīrasasekaiḥ śephālīrasaṃsecanaiḥ śudhyati nirdoṣo bhavati vaṅgaśca śudhyati ।।
evaṃ raviṇā tāmreṇa saha ghoṣo'pi kāṃsyamapi śudhyati ।।
kativāraṃ secanaiḥ munibhiḥ saptasaṃkhyākaiḥ tanmūlarajaḥ nirguṇḍīśiphācūrṇaṃ tatpravāpaiḥ galiteṣu nāgavaṅgaravighoṣeṣu rajo nikṣepaṇaiśca catvāraḥ śudhyantīti ।।

tīkṣṇaloha rañjana
raktagaṇagalitapaśujalabhāvitapuṭitaṃ hi rajyate tīkṣṇam ।
tīkṣṇaloha śodhana
śudhyati kadalīśikhirasabhāvitapuṭitaṃ tribhirvāraiḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha raktagaṇetyādi ।।
tīkṣṇaṃ sārākhyaṃ raktagaṇagalitapaśujalabhāvitaṃ puṭitaṃ sat raktagaṇena saha galitaṃ militaṃ yat paśujalaṃ gomūtraṃ tena bhāvitaṃ tato vahnipuṭitaṃ sat rajyate rāgamāpnoti ।।
punastīkṣṇaṃ kadalīśikhirasabhāvitapuṭitaṃ vā rambhācitrakarasabhāvitaṃ gharmapuṭitaṃ tato vahnipuṭitaṃ ca sat tribhirvāraiḥ śudhyatītyarthaḥ ।।

metals śodhana
sarvaṃ śudhyati loho rajyati suragopasannibho vāpāt ।
mākṣikadaradena bhṛśaṃ śulvaṃ vā gandhakena mṛtam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sāmānyena sarvalohānāṃ śodhanamāraṇamāha sarva ityādi ।।
sarvo loho dhātuvargaḥ śudhyati mṛtaśca bhavati punaḥ rajyati ca ।।
kena bhṛśaṃ atyarthaṃ yathā syāttathā mākṣikadaradena tāpyahiṅgulena kṛtvā yo vāpaḥ galiteṣu loheṣu mākṣikadaradaprakṣepaṇaṃ tasmāt suragopasaṃnibha indragopasadṛśaḥ sarvo loho bhavet ।।
vā śulbaṃ tāmraṃ mākṣikadaradavāpena suragopasannibhaṃ syāt vā gandhena gandhakavāpena mṛtamapyeva syādityarthaḥ ।।

atha satvanirgamamabhidhāsyate ।

sattva importance of ~

vaikrāntakāntasasyakamākṣikavimalādayo vinā satvam ।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

dattavānsatataṃ saukhyaṃ śuddhebhyaśca khalaṃ tathā ।
duḥkhamṛtyapyamātmānaḥ kopasya samakārakam ।।
vaikrāntādīnāṃ rasasaṃjñikānāṃ sattvapraśaṃsanam āha vaikrāntamityādi ।।
vaikrāntakāntasasyakamākṣikavimalādayaḥ śuddhā api dvandve na milanti ।।
vaikrāntaṃ vajrabhūmijaṃ rajaḥ kāntaṃ cumbakaṃ sasyakaścapalaḥ mākṣikaṃ tāpyaṃ vimalā raupyamākṣikam ityādayo gandhakādayaścoparasaṃjñakā na milanti ekaśarīratāṃ nāpnuvanti ।।
kva dvandve ubhayamelāpe ।।
punastān śuddhānapi rasaḥ sūto na grasati ।।

nāganāsikābhidhānaṃ candrodakam amṛtam āptakāṭhinyam ।
rasavaikrāntakam evaṃ badhnāti rasaṃ svasattvena ।।
śailodaka
nānāvidhasaṃsthānaṃ nirjaraśikhariśikharasambhūtam ।
dhārodambhasi śreṣṭhaṃ tadaśma śailodakaṃ prāpya ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vaikrāntaprādhānyam āha nāgetyādi ।।
evaṃlakṣaṇaṃ vaikrāntakaṃ jñātavyam ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ nāganāsikābhidhānaṃ nāgānāṃ phaṇināṃ nāsikā eva abhidhānaṃ saṃjñā yasya tat ।।
punaḥ kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ candrodakaṃ candramasaḥ sambandhi yadudakaṃ balaṃ tasmādevāmṛtaṃ ।।
āptakāṭhinyaṃ prāptaṃ kāṭhinyaṃ yena pūrvametacca mṛdūtpannamityarthaḥ ।।
evaṃvidhaṃ rasavaikrāntaṃ rasasaṃjñakaṃ vaikrāntaṃ rasaṃ sūtaṃ badhnāti ।।
kena svasatvena svīyasāreṇeti ।।
vaikrāntaprakāramāha nānetyādi ।।
pūrvamupavarṇitaṃ vaikrāntaṃ nānāvidhasaṃsthānamasti nānāvidhamanekaprakāraṃ saṃsthānaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ yasya tat saṃsthānaṃ vyañjanaṃ liṅgaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ cihnamākṛtiḥ iti mādhavanidānaṃ sitāsitaraktapītavarṇatvān nānāvidhasaṃsthānam ityarthaḥ ।।
punarnirjaraśikhariśikharasambhūtaṃ nirjarāṇāṃ devānāṃ yaḥ śikharī parvatastasya śikharaṃ śṛṅgaṃ tatra sambhūtam utpannam ।।
nānāvidhasaṃsthānaṃ kutaḥ dhārodambhasi dhārābhirudanta unmattamambho yatra samaye tasmin varṣākāle śailodakaṃ śilāsaṃbandhi yadudakaṃ jalaṃ tat prāpya śreṣṭhaṃ tadaśma vaikrāntābhidhānaṃ nānāvarṇaṃ bhavati yataḥ śilodakasya nānāvidhatvam ।।

vaikrānta sattva pātana
bhastrādvayena haṭhato dhmātavyaṃ pañcamāhiṣasubaddham ।
dattvā daśāṃśasvarjikapaṭuṭaṃkaṇaguñjikākṣārān ।।
tadgacchati kaṭhinatvaṃ muñcati satvaṃ sphuliṅgakākāram ।
muktānikaraprāyaṃ grāhyaṃ tat kācam adhivarjya ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vaikrāntasatvapātanamāha bhastretyādi ।।
tadvaikrāntaṃ pañcamāhiṣasubaddhaṃ dadhidugdhājyamūtraśakṛdbhiḥ pañcasaṃkhyākair māhiṣaiḥ saha subaddhaṃ piṇḍākṛti kṛtaṃ sat bhastrādvayena khallayugmena haṭhato balāt dhmātavyam ।।
kiṃ kṛtvā daśāṃśasarjikapaṭuṭaṅkaṇaguñjikākṣārān dattvā daśāṃśavibhāgena sarjikālavaṇasaubhāgyaraktikāyavakṣārān piṣṭavaikrānte kṣepyetyarthaḥ ।।
dhmātaṃ sat kiṃ syāttadāha tadityādi ।।
sphuliṅgakākāraṃ vahnikaṇanibhaṃ satvaṃ sāraṃ muñcati ।।
punastatsatvaṃ kaṭhinatvaṃ gacchati kaṭhinaṃ syādityarthaḥ ।।
tatsatvaṃ ākārato muktānikaraprāyaṃ mauktikarāśisadṛśaṃ syāt evaṃvidhaṃ satvaṃ kācaṃ adhivarjya dūrīkṛtya tat nirmalaṃ grāhyamityarthaḥ ।।
yugmam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

minerals sattvapātana

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

satvapātanavidhānamāha vajretyādi ।।
dṛḍhāṅgārair iti dṛḍhakathanāt khadirādīnāṃ pūrvoktatvādbhastrādvayena ca dhmātā satī vajrābhrakāntasasyakamākṣikaprabhṛtisakaladhātūnāṃ vajrasaṃjñakaṃ yadabhraṃ tadvajrābhraṃ kāntaṃ cumbakaṃ sasyakaṃ capalā mākṣikaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ itiprabhṛtayaḥ sakaladhātavaḥ sarvoparasāsteṣāṃ piṇḍī satvaṃ pātayati ।।

mākṣika sattva special alchem potency
hitvā mākṣikasatvaṃ nānyeṣāṃ śaktirasti lohaghnī ।
na patati tāvatsatvaṃ bhastrānte na yāvad āhriyet ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

śaktimattvena mākṣikasatvapraśaṃsanam āha hitvetyādi ।।
mākṣikasatvaṃ tāpyasāraṃ hitvā tyaktvā anyeṣāṃ rasoparasānāṃ śaktiḥ sāmarthyaṃ nāsti ।।
kiṃbhūtā śaktiḥ lohaghnīti lohān hantīti vigrahaḥ ।।
punastāvatsattvaṃ na patati yāvadbhastrā ante satvasamīpe na āhrīyeta na prāpyeta tasmādalpenāgninā satvāpravṛttirityarthaḥ ।।

mākṣika sattva phys properties
raktaṃ mṛdu nāgasamaṃ satvaṃ yasmāddhi mākṣikātpatitam ।
gandhāśmano'pi tadvatkāryaṃ yatnena mṛdubhāvam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

mākṣikasatvam udāsyānyasatvapravṛttim āha raktamityādi ।।
raktaṃ lohitaṃ nāgasamaṃ sīsakatulyaṃ mṛdu komalaṃ evaṃvidhaṃ satvaṃ yasmāddhetor mākṣikāt patati tāpyāt nirgacchati tadvattasmāddhetor vā tasmādvidhānataḥ gandhāśmano gandhakasya yatnena mṛdubhāvaṃ kāryaṃ yathā gandhako'pi mṛdurbhavatītyarthaḥ ।।

mākṣika sattva pātana
lavaṇāmlena supuṭitaṃ mākṣikamamlena marditaṃ vidhinā ।
muñcati soṣṇe grāsam āyasapātre tu piṣṭikā bhavati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

mākṣikasatvavidhānamāha lavaṇetyādi ।।
mākṣikaṃ tāpyaṃ lavaṇāmlena lavaṇaṃ mukhyatvāt granthāntarasāmyācca saindhavaṃ amlo jambīrādiḥ tena marditaṃ punaramlena jambīrādinā vidhinā uktarītyā puṭitaṃ vahnau pratāpitaṃ sat muñcati pūrvaślokasaṃbandhāt sattvaṃ iti śeṣaḥ ।।
itthaṃ patitaṃ satvaṃ grāhyam ।।
lavaṇāmlena gandhakamapi mṛdu syāt ।।
tu punaḥ soṣṇe āyasapātre vahnau tāpite lohapātre piṣṭikā bhavati raktavarṇarajorūpety arthaḥ ।।

sattva colour of diff ~
tutthāddhi tāpyajasamaṃ samasṛṣṭaṃ patati vai satvam ।
abhravaikrāntakāntaprabhṛtīnāṃ tatra lohanibham ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

tutthādīnāṃ satvapātanamāha tutthādityādi ।।
tutthāt tutthaṃ śikhigrīvaṃ tasmāt tāpyajasamamiti mākṣikasatvavat mākṣikasatvavidhānenāsya satvapāta ityarthaḥ ।।
samasṛṣṭaṃ samaṃ tāpyena tulyaṃ varṇamārdavābhyāṃ sṛṣṭaṃ kathitamityarthaḥ ।।
evaṃvidhaṃ tutthakasatvaṃ patati ।।
abhraketyādi abhrakaṃ pratītaṃ vaikrāntaṃ rasavaikrāntaṃ kāntaṃ cumbakaṃ itiprabhṛtīnām ityādīnāṃ tattvaṃ patrasatvapātanayoge lohanibhaṃ muṇḍavarṇam ityarthaḥ ।।

svarṇamākṣika sattvapātana 
strīvajrīdugdhabhāvitameraṇḍasnehabhāvitaṃ śataṃ dhmātam ।
evaṃ tribhiriha vāraiḥ śulvasamaṃ bhavati rañjakaṃ haimam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

punarmākṣikavidhānāntaram āha strītyādi ।
tāpyaṃ strīvajrīdugdhabhāvitaṃ strī nārī vajrī sehuṇḍaḥ tayordugdhaṃ tena bhāvitaṃ gharmapuṭitaṃ kuryāt ।।
punareraṇḍasnehena śataṃ śatavāraṃ bhāvitaṃ ca kuryāt ।।
tato vāraistribhireva dhmātaṃ sat haimaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ tasyedaṃ haimaṃ satvaṃ śulbasamaṃ tāmranibhaṃ bhavati rañjakaṃ rase rāgadāyī syātkanake'pi ca ।।

mākṣika, rasaka sattva pātana
kadalīrasaśatabhāvitamadhvairaṇḍatailaparipakvam ।
tāpyaṃ muñcati satvaṃ rasakaṃ caivaṃ trisantāpaiḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha kadalītyādi ।।
tāpyaṃ mākṣikaṃ kadalīrasaśatabhāvitamadhvairaṇḍatailaparipakvam iti prathamaṃ rambhādraveṇa śatavāraṃ bhāvitaṃ paścāt madhvairaṇḍatailābhyāṃ saha paripakvaṃ samyak pācitaṃ sat satvaṃ muñcati ।।
kaiḥ kṛtvā trisaṃtāpaiḥ trivāraṃ dhamanaiḥ ।।
evaṃ rasakaṃ kharparakamapi satvaṃ muñcatīti ।।

minerals sattva pātana
ūrṇāṭaṅkaṇaguḍapuralākṣāsarjarasaiḥ sarvadhātubhiḥ piṣṭaiḥ ।
chāgīkṣīreṇa kṛtā piṇḍī śastā hi satvavidhau ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

satvapātane piṇḍīmāha ūrṇetyādi ।।
ūrṇā iti ūrṇā meṣaroma ṭaṅkaṇaṃ saubhāgyaṃ guḍaḥ pratītaḥ puro gugguluḥ lākṣā jatu sarjaraso rālaḥ etaiḥ kiṃviśiṣṭaiḥ sarvadhātubhiḥ rasoparasairvā svarṇādibhiḥ saha piṣṭaiḥ peṣitaiḥ punaḥ chāgīkṣīreṇa ajāpayasā kṛtā yā piṇḍī sā satvavidhau satvapātanakarmaṇi śastā pradhānā ।।
dhāturasoparasānāṃ satvaṃ pātayatyeveti ।।

minerals sattva pātana
cūrṇitasatvasambhāraṃ triṃśatpalamādareṇa saṃgṛhya ।
ṭaṃkaṇapalasaptayutaṃ guṃjāpalatritayayojitaṃ caiva ।।
tilacūrṇakakiṭṭapalair matsyair āloḍya dviraṃśayuktaiśca ।
godhūmabaddhapiṇḍī gopañcakabhāvitā bahuśaḥ ।।
koṣṭhakadhamanavidhinā tīvraṃ bhastrānalena tatpatati ।
saṃdravati cābhrasattvaṃ tathaiva sarvāṇi satvāni ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha cūrṇitetyādi ।।
cūrṇitasatvasamānaṃ cūrṇitaṃ piṣṭaṃ yat satvaṃ sāraṃ tatsamānaṃ viśuddhatvāt satvasamānaṃ dhāturasoparasacūrṇaṃ iti śeṣaḥ ।।
evaṃvidhaṃ viśuddhaṃ cūrṇaṃ ādareṇa prītyā ādau saṃgṛhya ṭaṅkaṇapalasaptayutaṃ kuryāt saubhāgyasya palaiḥ saptasaṃkhyākaiḥ sahitaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ ।।
viśuddhe cūrṇe triṃśatpale saptapalaṃ saubhāgyaṃ yojyaṃ evaṃ ṭaṅkaṇavidhānena ca punaḥ guñjāpalatritayena raktikāpalatritayaparimāṇena yojitaṃ kuryād iti ।।
tilacūrṇakakiṭṭapalaiḥ tilaṃ pratītaṃ teṣāṃ cūrṇakaṃ kiṭṭaṃ muṇḍādīnāṃ malaṃ tayoḥ palaiḥ palamānairgodhūmabaddhapiṇḍī bahuśo bahuvāraṃ gopañcakabhāvitaṃ gavāṃ kṣīrājyadadhimūtraviṭkena bhāvitā kiṃ kṛtvā matsyair āloḍya matsyaiḥ kṣudrajalacarair āloḍya saṃmiśryetyarthaḥ ।।
koṣṭhake koṣṭhikāyantre dhamanavidhinā utkṣipyotkṣipya dhamanena bhastrānalena tat satvaṃ patati pūrvasaṃbandhāt tāpyādīnāṃ iti śeṣaḥ ।।
ca punarabhrasatvaṃ abhrakātsāraṃ saṃdravati ।।
tathaivoktavidhānena sarvāṇi samastāni satvāni sārāṇi patanti anuktānāṃ iti śeṣaḥ ।।

atha bījanirvāhaṇam ārabhyate ।

svarṇamākṣika for production of gold 

svīkṛtya sarvasarito gaṅgā jaladhau yathā tathā haimam ।
praviśati rase gṛhītvā saṃmiliti sarvalohaguṇān ।।
jīryati milati ca śulbe tatsatvaṃ kiṭṭatāṃ yāti ।
suvṛttaḥ sadrṛtārambhaḥ sujñaḥ saṃjñānadarśakaḥ ।
abhūcca dhanadharmajño hārī kuñjanasaṃpadām ।।
ādau haimapraśaṃsām āha svīkṛtyetyādi ।।
haimaṃ svarṇamākṣikasatvaṃ saṃmiliti kiṃkṛtvā sarvalohaguṇān sarvaloheṣu samastadhātuṣu saṃmilitā miśritāḥ ye guṇās tān gṛhītvā tathā rase praviśati yathā gaṅgā sarvā nadyaḥ saritaḥ svīkṛtya aṅgīkṛtya jaladhau samudre praviśati ।।
tāpyasatvādhikāram āha jīryatītyādi ।।
tat haimaṃ tāpyasatvaṃ śulbe tāmre milati sati sattvaṃ jīryati jāraṇatvamāpnoti rase iti śeṣaḥ ।।
tasmin satve śulbe milati sati kiṭṭatāṃ yāti lohamalasadṛśaṃ syāt ।।

hemakriyāsu kariṇā trapuṇā tārakriyāsu nirvyūḍham ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

prathamaṃ tatsatvaṃ kariṇā nāgena saha hemakriyāsu svarṇakāryeṣu nirvyūḍhaṃ rase nirvāhitaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ ।।
punastrapuṇā vaṅgena saha tārakriyāsu rūpyakāryeṣu nirvyūḍhaṃ kuryāt nāgavaṅgau sarvatra pītasitakāryeṣu praśastāvityarthaḥ ।।

Herstellung eines bījas
ghanasatvaṃ khalu raviṇā rasāyane dvaṃdvakaṃ yojyam ।
raktagaṇapātabhāvitagirijatumākṣikagairikadaradaiḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

abhrasatvayogamāha ghanasatvam ityādi ।।
khalu niścaye vākyālaṅkāre vā ghanasatvam abhrasāraṃ raviṇā tāmreṇa saha rasāyane jarāvyādhināśane dvaṃdvakaṃ ghanasatvatāmraṃ yojyaṃ punaḥ raktagaṇapātabhāvitagirijatumākṣikagairikadaradaiḥ raktagaṇasya yaḥ pātaḥ pātanaṃ nikṣepo vā tena bhāvitāni gharmapuṭitāni girijatumākṣikagairikadaradāni girijatu śilājatu mākṣikaṃ pratītaṃ daradaṃ hiṅgulaṃ etairbījaśeṣaṃ kuryād ityāgāmiślokājjñeyam ।।

gold bīja
mṛdulatāmrakāntaghanasatvaṃ mṛtanāgatīkṣṇakanakaṃ ca ।
kurvīta bījaśeṣaṃ daradaśilātālamākṣikairvāpāt ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha mṛduletyādi ।।
mṛdulaṃ nepālasaṃjñikaṃ tāmraṃ kāntaṃ lohajāti ghanasatvamabhrasāraṃ punarmṛtaṃ nāgaṃ sīsakaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ lohajāti kanakaṃ hema etattrayaṃ bījaṃ śulbāditrayaṃ ca bījasaṃjñakaṃ daradaśilātālamākṣikairvāpāt daradaṃ hiṅgulaṃ śilā manohvā tālaṃ haritālaṃ etaiḥ kṛtvā vāpaḥ vahnitapte parikṣepaḥ tasmāt bījaśeṣaṃ kurvīta ubhayorbīje abhrasatvahemnaḥ śeṣe kuryādityarthaḥ vā evaṃ kṛte yaccheṣaṃ tiṣṭhati tadbījamiti ।।

gold, silver bīja
mṛtanāgaṃ vaṅgaṃ vā śulvaṃ ghanasatvatārakanakaṃ vā ।
dhmātaṃ tadeva sarvaṃ giriṇādhikaśodhanairvāpāt ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha mṛtaṃ nāgam ityādi ।।
mayannāgaṃ sīsakaṃ tanmṛtanāgaṃ ca mṛtaṃ yadvaṅgaṃ raktagaṇāvāpamṛtaṃ ca yacchulvaṃ vā ghanasatvatārakanakaṃ ghanasatvamabhrasāraṃ tāraṃ rūpyaṃ kanakaṃ hema etannadugaṇasarvaṃ vā pratyekaṃ pṛthak giriṇā śilājatunā saha dhmātaṃ kuryāt adhikaśodhanaiḥ daradaśilātālairvāpāt bījaśeṣaṃ kuryāditi pūrvasaṃbandhaḥ ।।

gold bija 
raktagaṇaṃ pītaṃ vā mākṣikarājāvartam atho vimalam ।
ekatamaṃ vā gairikakunaṭīkṣitigandhakakhagairvā ।।
nirvyūḍhaireva raso rāgādi gṛhṇāti bandhamupayāti ।
mṛtalohoparasādyair nirvyūḍhaṃ bhavati śṛṅkhalābījam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

raktagaṇaṃ dāḍimakiṃśukādikaṃ vā pītagaṇaṃ yathā ।
kiṃśukaḥ karṇikāraśca haridrādvitayaṃ tathā ।
pītavargo'yamuddiṣṭo rasarājasya karmaṇi iti ।।
vā mākṣikaṃ tāpyaṃ vā rājāvartaṃ rājavarto lājavarada iti bhāṣāyāṃ atha vimalaṃ tāramākṣikaṃ ityekatamaṃ sarvameva vā gairikakunaṭīkṣitigandhakakhagaiḥ gairikaṃ pratītaṃ kunaṭī manohvā kṣitiḥ sphaṭakī gandhakaḥ pratītaḥ khagaḥ kāsīsaṃ etairiti ।।
etaiḥ pūrvoktaireva rase nirvyūḍhe raso rāgādi rañjanādi gṛhṇāti ādiśabdāt sāraṇaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ punarbandham upayāti bandhanamāpnoti punaḥ mṛtalohoparasādyaiḥ mṛtāśca te lohāśca dhātavaśca ta eva uparasā gandhakādyāḥ ādyaśabdāt rasā api tairnirvyūḍhaiḥ kṛtvā śṛṅkhalābījaṃ uttarottaraṃ rañjakaṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ ।।

bīja for rañjana and bandhana of mercury
āyasaśalākikābhyām advandvākhyaiśca saṅkarākhyaiśca ।
nirvyūḍhaṃ rasalohairjāraṇakarmocitaṃ bhavati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

rasalohairiti rasā vaikrāntādayo lohā dhātavaḥ pratītās tair nirvyūḍhaṃ kiṃviśiṣṭaiḥ advandvākhyaiḥ ekātmaiḥ saṃkarairvā sarvaiḥ saṃkaro'vakare ityamaraḥ evaṃ niṣpanne bījaṃ jāraṇayogyaṃ sadityarthaḥ ।।

bījamidaṃ raktagaṇe niṣecitaṃ tena kṛtavāpam ।
cāritajāritamātraṃ sūtaṃ rañjayati badhnāti ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

viśeṣavidhyantaramāha bījamityādi ।।
idaṃ niṣpannabījaṃ raktagaṇe niṣecitaṃ kuryāt ।।
punastena raktagaṇena kṛtavāpaṃ kṛto vāpo yasmin tat ।।
punastadbījaṃ cāritajāritamātraṃ pūrvaṃ ca paścāt jāritaṃ santaṃ sūtaṃ rañjayati rāgaṃ prāpayati badhnāti ceti ।।

bīja further processing
raktasnehaviśodhitamṛtaloharasādibhistu sarveṣām ।
bījānāṃ kuru vāpaṃ raktasnehe niṣekaṃ ca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha raktetyādi ।।
raktasneha iti raktagaṇo dāḍimakiṃśukādikaḥ snehaḥ kaṅguṇyādīnāṃ etairviśodhitāḥ paścānmṛtā ye dhātavo rasādayaśca rasoparasāstaiḥ sarveṣāṃ bījānāṃ pūrvoktānāṃ vāpaṃ kuru rase iti śeṣaḥ vā rakte raktavarṇe snehe snehavarge niṣekaṃ ca vidhānadvayamidam ।।

silver bījas
vaṅgābhram abhratāraṃ sitaśailamalāhatau ca sitavaṅgau ।
raktaṃ sitatāpyahataṃ ramati nirvyūḍhavaṅgābhram ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

pītakriyāyāṃ bījānyuktāni atha śvetakriyāyāṃ bījānyāha vaṅgetyādi ।।
vaṅgābhramiti vaṅgaṃ raṅgaṃ abhraṃ gaganaṃ ete bījahetave iti śeṣaḥ ।।
punarabhratāraṃ abhraṃ gaganaṃ tāraṃ rūpyaṃ iti ca sitaṃ śvetaṃ yacchailamalaṃ śilājatu tena āhatau samyak mṛtau sitavaṅgau tāraraṅgau kāryau punaḥ raktaṃ hema sitaṃ tāraṃ tāpyaṃ mākṣikaṃ tābhyāṃ hataṃ māritaṃ kuryāt ।।
punastāraṃ rūpyaṃ nirvyūḍhaṃ vaṅgaṃ cābhraṃ ca yatra tadevaṃvidhaṃ kuryāt ।।
etatsarvaṃ rase tārakriyāsu yojyamityarthaḥ ।।

nirvāhaṇavidhireṣaḥ prakāśito'śeṣadoṣaśamanāya ।
bījānāmapyevaṃ ghanasatvaṃ yujyate prathamam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

bīje'bhrasatvaṃ pradhānamāha nirvāhaṇetyādi ।।
eṣaḥ kimarthaḥ aśeṣadoṣaśamanāya dhātvādīnāṃ samastadoṣanāśanāyetyarthaḥ ।।
evamamunā prakāreṇa yathā dhātunirvāhaṇavidhistathā bījānāṃ rase nirvāhaṇaṃ kuryāt sarvabījanirvāhaṇe abhrakasatvaṃ prathamaṃ nirvāhyamiti jñeyam ।।

crucible for bījanirvāhaṇa
chāgāsthibhasmanirmitamūṣāṃ kṛtvaiva mallakākārām ।
dalayoge ghanarandhrāṃ ṭaṅkaṇaviṣaguñjākṛtalepām ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

nirvāhaṇavidhānamāha chāgetyādi ।।
evaṃvidhāṃ mūṣāṃ kṛtvā dhātunirvāhaṇaṃ kuryāt iti śeṣaḥ ।।
kiṃbhūtāṃ chāgāsthibhasmanirmitamūṣāmiti chāgo bastastasyāsthīni tadbhasmanā nirmitā kṛtā yā mūṣā tām ।।
punaḥ kiṃbhūtāṃ mallakākārāṃ gostanasadṛśīm ।।
punaḥ kiṃviśiṣṭāṃ ghanarandhrāṃ nibiḍachidrām ।।
punaḥ ṭaṅkaṇaviṣaguñjākṛtalepāṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ saubhāgyaṃ viṣaṃ saktukaṃ guñjā raktikā tābhiḥ kṛto lepo yasyāṃ sā tām ।।
evaṃbhūtā mūṣā dalayoge patramelane kāryetyarthaḥ ।।

atha dvandvamelanamabhidhāsyate ।

Motivation für dvandvamelana

yāvan nāṅgāṅgatayā na milanti lohāni sarvasattveṣu ।
tāvatsarvāṅgaṃ na ca carati raso dvandvayogena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vācāṃ vilāsena sudhānukārī nu jagatkaroti ।
kiṃcitsvayaṃ yatpuruṣatvameva sudhādvijihvāśritam ityadoṣaḥ ।।
atha dvandvayogaprakāramāha yāvadityādi ।।
yāvadityavadhau ।।
lohāni hemādīni nāgāṅgatayā bhujaṅgaśarīratayā na milanti sugamatvena ekaśarīratāṃ nāpnuvanti ।।
keṣu sarvasattveṣu abhrādīnāṃ sāreṣu sattvasya kāṭhinyādvinopāyaṃ naikatāṃ yānti lohāni ।।
atastāvadrasaḥ sarvāṅgaṃ na carati ।।
