kena kṛtvā satveṣu lohāni milanti dvandvayogena daradādinā vā guḍapuraṭaṅkaṇādineti ।।

metals preparation for dv~
mākṣīkarasakasasyakadaradānyatamena vāpitaṃ loham ।
saṃtyajati nibiḍabhāvaṃ satve saṃmilati sudhmātam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sattvamelanavidhānam āha mākṣiketyādi ।।
lohaṃ svarṇādi ।।
mākṣikaṃ tāpyaṃ rasakaṃ kharparikaṃ sasyakaṃ capalā daradaṃ hiṅgulaṃ etena catuṣkeṇa vā ebhyo anyatamenoktarasoparasena vāpitaṃ sudhmātaṃ śobhanayuktyā dhmātaṃ ca sat niviḍabhāvaṃ saṃtyajati sattve saṃmilati ca ।।

dvandvamelāpaka preparation
guḍapuraṭaṅkaṇalākṣāsarjarasair dhātakīsamāyuktaiḥ ।
strīstanyena tu piṣṭaiḥ rasāyane dvaṃdvitaṃ yojyam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha guḍetyādi ।।
idaṃ dvaṃdvitaṃ dvaṃdvīkṛtaṃ lohaṃ sattvena militaṃ rasāyane jarāvyādhināśane yojyam ।।
kairdvandvamelāpakaiḥ kṛtvā dvaṃdvitamityāha guḍetyādi ।।
guḍaḥ pratītaḥ puro gugguluḥ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ saubhāgyaṃ lākṣā jatu sarjaraso rālā etaiḥ dhātakīsamāyuktaiḥ dhātakī pratītā tatsamāyuktaiḥ punaḥ strīstanyena nārīdugdhena piṣṭairmarditaiḥ etairdvandvamelāpakaiḥ kṛtvā ।।

dvandvamelāpaka
ūrṇāṭaṅkaṇagirijatukarṇākṣimalendragopakarkaṭakaiḥ ।
nārīpayasā piṣṭaiḥ sarve dvandveṣu hi milanti ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sarve dvandveṣu satvaṃ prati dvandveṣu milanti ekībhavanti lohāni iti śeṣaḥ ।।
etaiḥ kaiḥ ūrṇādibhiḥ ।।
ūrṇā pratītā ṭaṅkaṇaṃ saubhāgyaṃ girijatu śilājatu karṇākṣimalaṃ manuṣyasya indragopako jīvaviśeṣaḥ karkaṭakaścakulīraḥ syātkulīraḥ karkaṭakaḥ ityamaraḥ etaiḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaiḥ nārīpayasā strīdugdhena piṣṭaiḥ kalkitaiḥ trayo'pi dvandvamelāpakayogā iti ।।

dva~ of rasavaikrānta and gold bandhana of mercury
rasavaikrāntakamevaṃ milati dvandvānvitaṃ samaṃ hemnā ।
nirvyūḍhaṃ tatsatvaṃ tena raso bandhamupayāti ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha rasetyādi ।।
evamuktavidhānena rasavaikrāntakaṃ dvandvānvitaṃ svakīyadvandvasahitaṃ milati pṛthagbhāvaṃ tyajati ।।
kena samaṃ hemnā saha ।।
tadrasavaikrāntasattvaṃ hemnā saha nirvyūḍhaṃ kuryāt tena rasavaikrāntasattvahemayogena raso bandhamupayāti baddho bhavatīti ।।

dvandvamelāpaka
śastaṃ sarvadvandve girijatulelītakendragopādyaiḥ ।
mahiṣīkarṇamalādyaiḥ syādbījaṃ ṭaṅkaṇālaviṣaiḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha viśeṣavidhyantaramāha śastamityādi ।।
evaṃvidhaṃ bījaṃ śastaṃ kva sarvadvandve ।।
punaretaiḥ kṛtvā bījaṃ śastaṃ syāt ।।
kaiḥ girijatulelītakendragopādyaiḥ girijatu śilājatu lelītako gandhakaḥ indragopaḥ surendragopo jīvaviśeṣaḥ ete ādyā yeṣāṃ taiḥ ।।
na kevalametair mahiṣīkarṇamalādyaiśca mahiṣyāḥ karṇayormala ādyo yeṣāṃ te ādyaśabdānnāsākṣimalaṃ ca ।।
punaṣṭaṅkaṇālaviṣaiḥ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ saubhāgyaṃ ālaṃ haritālaṃ viṣaṃ kandajaṃ etaiḥ piṣṭairdvandvamelāpaḥ syāditi punaḥ saṃbandhaḥ ।।

dvandvamelāpaka
madhusahitairapyetaistārābhraṃ milati tāpyakanakaṃ ca ।
eraṇḍatailaṭaṅkaṇakaṃkuṣṭhaśilendragopaistu ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha madhvityādi ।।
etaiḥ pūrvoktair yogaiḥ madhusahitaiḥ kṣaudrayutaiḥ tārābhraṃ rūpyagaganaṃ milati ।।
ca punastāpyakanakaṃ mākṣikasvarṇaṃ idaṃ dvandvaṃ ca milati ।।
na kevalaṃ pūrvoktayogair milati punaretair eraṇḍatailaṭaṅkaṇakaṅkuṣṭhaśilendragopaiśca eraṇḍatailaṃ vātārisnehaḥ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ saubhāgyaṃ kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ viraṅgaṃ śilā manohvā indragopako jīvaviśeṣaḥ etaiśca madhusahitaiḥ kṛtvā dvandvaṃ milatītyavaśyam ।।

melāpana of mercury, gold, and abhra
sūtena śuddhakanakaṃ niṣpiṣya samābhrayojitaṃ kṛtvā ।
pādena tu pūrvoktadvandvānyatamakaṃ kalpyam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

tadvidhānamāha sūtenetyādi ।।
prathamaṃ sūtena rasena saha śuddhakanakaṃ niṣpiṣya saṃmardya punaḥ samābhrayojitaṃ kṛtvā samaṃ ca tadabhraṃ ca tena yojitaṃ kṛtvā paścātpādena caturthāṃśavibhāgena pūrvoktadvandvānyatamakaṃ kalpyaṃ pūrvoktadvandvam eraṇḍatailādikaṃ girijatvādikaṃ ca tebhyo anyatamakaṃ dvandvaṃ yojyamiti ।।

melāpana of gold and abhra
rasoparasasya hemno dviguṇaṃ śuddhamākṣikaṃ dattvā ।
svarasena kākamācyā rambhākandena mṛdnīyāt ।।
kṛtamityetatpiṇḍaṃ hemābhraṃ milati vajramūṣāyām ।
vidhyantaramāha rasetyādi ।।
rasoparasasya vaikrāntagandhakādermadhye śuddhamākṣikaṃ nirdoṣaṃ tāpyaṃ hemno dviguṇaṃ kanakāddviguṇitaṃ dattvā dviguṇamākṣikayutaṃ hema dattvetyarthaḥ ।।
etadrasoparasādikaṃ kākamācyā vāyasyāḥ svarasena mṛdnīyāt mardanaṃ kuryāt ।।
rambhākandena ca kadalīkandenāpītyarthaḥ ।।
etatpūrvauṣadhaṃ piṇḍaṃ golākāraṃ kuryāt ।।
itividhānena hemābhraṃ milati hematāpyaṃ ceti ।।
kva vajramūṣāyām ।।
tathāha ।
mṛdastribhāgāḥ śaṇaladdibhāgau bhāgaśca nirdagdhatuṣopalādeḥ ।
kiṭṭārdhabhāgaṃ parikhaṇḍya vajramūṣāṃ vidadhyātkhalu satvapāte ।
iti ।।

melāpana of abhrasattva with diff substances
raviśaśitīkṣṇairevaṃ milanti gaganādisatvāni ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

evam amunā vidhinā raviśaśitīkṣṇaiḥ saha ravistāmraṃ śaśī rūpyaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ lohajātiḥ etaiḥ sārdhaṃ gaganādisatvāni abhrādīnāṃ sārāṇi milantīti yugmam ।।

melāpana for saṅkarabījas
saṅkarabījānāmapi vidhānamityādi gaganasatvayogena ।
mākṣīkayogādanyaṃ yojyamavaśyaṃ tu sarvatra ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

abhrasatvasyādhikāramāha saṃkaretyādi ।।
saṅkarabījānāmapi vidhānaṃ kartavyārthopadeśa iti yāvat ।।
ityādi pūrvoktaṃ tu punaḥ gaganasatvayogena abhrakasattvena sārdhaṃ mākṣīkayogād anyaṃ yojyaṃ abhrasatvena saha mākṣīkaṃ na syāditi vyaktiḥ ।।

kāntamukhaṃ sarveṣāṃ sattvānāṃ melakaṃ prathamam ।
pūrvoktakalkasahitaṃ mākṣīkamṛtanāgatālaśilam ।।

iti paramahaṃsaparivrājakācāryaśrīmadgovindabhagavatpādaviracite rasahṛdayatantre dvandvādhikārātmako dvādaśo'vabodhaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

kāntetyādi ।।
mākṣikeṇa mṛtaṃ yannāgaṃ tālaṃ haritālaṃ śilā manohvā ca tattathā pūrvoktakalkasahitaṃ yatkalkaṃ rasoparasādīnāṃ tena sahitaṃ yuktaṃ kāntamukhaṃ yathā ।
abhāve'bhrakasattvasya kāntasattvaṃ pradāpayet ।
kāntasatvasya vābhāve tīkṣṇalohaṃ tu dāpayet ।
iti ।।

mākṣīkakāntatīkṣṇaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ mākṣīkam abhrakaṃ bījam ।
mākṣīkakāntaśulbaṃ tīkṣṇābhrakaṃ mahābījam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

madhuni mādhava eva madhuvrataḥ prakurute mudito madhuraṃ ravam ।
vararavo'pi satāṃ ca samāgamaṃ śabalatā kimupaiti na cārutām ।।
saṃkarabījānāṃ madhye mahābījasaṃjñānyāha mākṣiketyādi ।।
etattrikaṃ mahābījaṃ kimetat mākṣīkakāntatīkṣṇaṃ mākṣīkakāntaśulbaṃ tīkṣṇābhrakaṃ ca mākṣīkaṃ tāpyaṃ kāntaṃ cumbakaṃ śulbaṃ tāmraṃ tīkṣṇaṃ lohajātir abhrakaṃ gaganaṃ etattritayaṃ bījaṃ mahābījaṃ etattritrimukhaṃ pratyekaṃ mahāsaṃjñam ।।
viśeṣo'tra ।
bījapākaṃ pravakṣyāmi jāraṇārthaṃ rasasya tu ।
sūtrakramo'yaṃ bījena samajīrṇena śudhyati ।
iti ।।
avāntaratvena ca pratyekaṃ dravyaṃ bījasaṃjñābhimatam ।।

mākṣīkakāntaśulbaṃ śulbābhrakamākṣikaṃ cāpi ।
kāntābhrakamākṣīkaṃ tāpyakaśulbābhrakaṃ mahābījam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha mākṣīketyādi ।।
mākṣīkakāntaśulbaṃ mākṣīkaṃ tāpyaṃ kāntaṃ cumbakaṃ śulbaṃ tāmraṃ etadapi mahābījaṃ jñeyam ।।
punaḥ śulbābhrakamākṣīkaṃ punaḥ kāntābhrakamākṣīkaṃ kāntaṃ kāntapāṣāṇaṃ abhrakaṃ gaganaṃ mākṣīkaṃ tāpyaṃ tathā tāpyakaśulbābhrakaṃ etadapi ca mahābījaṃ jñeyamiti ।।

mākṣīkatīkṣṇaśulbaṃ tīkṣṇaśulbābhrakaṃ mahābījam ।
mākṣīkakāntakanakaṃ kanakāruṇamākṣikaṃ mahābījam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha mākṣīketyādi ।।
mākṣīkatīkṣṇaśulbaṃ mākṣikaṃ tāpyaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ sāralohajātiḥ śulbaṃ tāmram ।।
punastīkṣṇaśulbābhrakaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ sāraṃ śulbaṃ tāmraṃ abhrakaṃ gaganam ।।
punarmākṣīkakāntakanakaṃ mākṣīkaṃ tāpyaṃ kāntaṃ kāntapāṣāṇaṃ kanakaṃ svarṇam ।।
punaḥ kanakāruṇamākṣikaṃ kanakaṃ svarṇaṃ aruṇaṃ tāmraṃ mākṣikaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ ceti catuṣṭayaṃ mahābījaṃ pravarabījam ityarthaḥ ।।
caturṇāṃ pratyekaṃ mahābījasaṃjñeti ।।

mākṣīkatīkṣṇatāraṃ tārāruṇamākṣikaṃ caivam ।
kāntaṃ tu śulbatāpyaṃ śulbābhratāpyakāṃcanaṃ cāpi ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha mākṣīkatīkṣṇatāramiti ।।
mākṣīkaṃ tāpyaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ sāraṃ tāraṃ rūpyam ।।
punastārāruṇamākṣikaṃ evamuktavidhānena idamapi tāraṃ rūpyaṃ aruṇaṃ tāmraṃ mākṣīkaṃ tāpyam ।।
punaḥ kānte cumbake'bhivyāpake adhikaraṇe śulbaṃ tāmraṃ tāpyaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ yat prayuktam ।।
apīti niścayena ।।
śulbābhratāpyakāñcanaṃ vā śulbaṃ tāmraṃ abhraṃ gaganaṃ tāpyaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ kāñcanaṃ hema etaccatuṣṭayamapi mahābījaṃ jñeyam ।।
mahābījasaṃbandhaḥ pratyekamiti vyaktiḥ ।।

kāntendusasyatāpyaṃ kāntābhrakatīkṣṇamākṣikaṃ caiva ।
hemābhraśulbatāpyaṃ hemābhrakaśulbamākṣikaṃ vāpi ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha kāntendusasyatāpyamiti ।।
kāntaṃ kāntapāṣāṇaṃ industāraṃ sasyaṃ capalā tāpyaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ ceti ।।
punaḥ kāntābhrakatīkṣṇamākṣikaṃ tathā hemābhraśulbatāpyaṃ punarhemābhrakaśulbamākṣikaṃ vā hema kanakaṃ abhrakaṃ gaganaṃ śulbaṃ tāmraṃ mākṣīkaṃ tāpyaṃ etaccatuṣṭayamapi mahābījaṃ jñeyam ।।
pratyekadravye bījasaṃjñā ceti dhvanyarthaḥ ।।

kāntābhraśulbatāpyaṃ saṅkarabījaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha kāntetyādi ।।
kāntābhraśulbatāpyaṃ kāntaṃ cumbakaṃ abhrakaṃ gaganaṃ śulbaṃ tāmraṃ tāpyaṃ mākṣikaṃ ityapi mahābījam ।।
eteṣāṃ mahābījānāṃ cet saṃkarabījaṃ pratyekaṃ dravyasya bījasaṃjñā sā tarhi catuḥṣaṣṭipramāṇā syādityarthaḥ ।।

mahābīja production
sarveṣāṃ bījānāmādau kṛtvā yathoktasaṃyogam ।
śatavāpyaṃ yadvahnau drāvitaṃ hi bījaṃ viśuddhamidaṃ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

bījavidhānam āha sarveṣām ityādi ।।
ādau prathamaṃ sarveṣāṃ bījānāṃ yathoktaṃ saṃyogaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭīnāṃ uktasaṃjñānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ saṃyogaṃ ekatrīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā yadekatrīkṛtaṃ vahnau drāvitaṃ bhavati tatsarvaṃ śatavāpyaṃ bījaṃ siddhaṃ prayatnena syāditi śabdārthaḥ ।।

cāraṇa, garbha- and bāhyadruti necessary for bandhana
na patati yadi ghanasatvaṃ garbhe no vā dravanti bījāni ।
na ca bāhyadrutiyogastatkathamiha badhyate sūtaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sūtabandhane hetūnāha netyādi ।।
yadi garbhe rasodare ghanasattvaṃ abhrakasāraṃ na patati na prāpnoti vā garbhe bījāni asminnadhyāye abhihitāni mākṣikakāntaśulbādīni yāvanno dravanti ca punarbāhyadrutistasyā yogo rase drutimelanaṃ na syāt tattasmāddhetoḥ sūta ihāsyāṃ kriyāyāmasatyāṃ kathaṃ badhyate ghanatvaṃ dhatte ।।
garbhadrutibāhyadrutibhyāṃ sūto badhyate niyatamityabhiprāyaḥ ।।

production of gold preparing the mercury

samād adhi ca yajjīrṇaṃ bījaṃ tenaiva cāvartatā kāryā ।
kartavyaṃ tatkaraṇaṃ yasmātkhalu jāyate hema ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

śaradi śāradamegho varṣati varṣāsu vārṣiko vārdaḥ ।
madhusamaye parapuṣṭaḥ pravarajavaḥ śobhate satatam ।।
bījajāraṇātkiṃ bhavati tadāha samādītyādi ।।
samaṃ sūtatulyaṃ adhiśabdād aparimitaṃ samādadhikaṃ yajjīrṇaṃ jāraṇamāptaṃ bījaṃ niṣpannabījaṃ tenaiva jīrṇena bījena saha āvartatā kāryā āvarta iti āvartaḥ ।।
kiṃ tat yasmādvidhānāddhema kanakaṃ jāyate khalu niścayena tatkaraṇaṃ tasya vidhānasya karaṇam ।।
samādijīrṇasya sūtasya rūpyādiṣu prayogātkanakaṃ bhavediti vyaktiḥ ।।

rasabīja production
pradrāvya śastrapātre gandhapādena sūtakaṃ dadyāt ।
svarasena cauṣadhīnāṃ vaṭikāṃ niṣpiṣya kurvīta ।।
saṃsthāpya lohaphalake chāyāśuṣkāṃ tu tāṃ vaṭikām ।
laghulohakaṭorikayā sthagayitvā lepayetsudṛḍham ।।
lavaṇārdramṛdā liptāṃ sudṛḍhaṃ kurvīta dhūmrarodhāya ।
dattvā sudṛḍhāṃgārān bhastrādvayavahninaiva nirdhūme ।।
tāvadyāvaddhmātā raktābhā khoṭikā bhavati ।
apanīya tato'ṅgārān svabhāvaśītāṃ kaṭorikāṃ matvā ।।
utkhanyotkhanya tataḥ kaṭorikāyā raso grāhyaḥ ।
eṣaḥ mṛtasūtarājo golakavadbhavati ca sa sukhādhmātaḥ ।।
śikhigalatām ekaraso'tidhmātaḥ kācaṭaṃkaṇataḥ ।
triguṇaṃ vaṅgaṃ dadyātkrameṇa nāgam alpālpadānena ।।
paścāddhemnā yojyaṃ rasabījaṃ sūtabandhakaram ।
sūtamāraṇavidhānam āha pradrāvyetyādi ।।
śastrapātre tīkṣṇamayapātre aupaśleṣike'dhikaraṇe saptamī ।।
gandhapādena gandhasya turyāṃśavibhāgena sūtakaṃ dadyāt tatpātroparibhāge dattaṃ pradrāvya vahninā iti śeṣaḥ ।।
punaḥ oṣadhīnāṃ svarasena auṣadhyo granthāntare yathā ।
mṛdnīyātkhalu tāvat piṣṭamañjanasadṛśaṃ bhavedyāvat ।
tadanu ca niyāmakānāṃ śatāvarīkandukīsudhādīnām ।
iti ।।
śatāvaryādīnāṃ svakīyarasena niṣpiṣya pramardya vaṭikāṃ badarākarāṃ kurvīteti ।।
taccāha saṃsthāpyetyādi ।।
tāṃ pūrvoktāṃ vaṭikāṃ chāyāśuṣkāṃ lohaphalake śastrapātre saṃsthāpya punaḥ laghulohakaṭorikayā pūrvoktalohaphalakāt laghvī yā lohakaṭorikā tayā sthagayitvā ācchādya dṛḍhaṃ gāḍhaṃ yathā syāttathā lepayet vakṣyamāṇeneti śeṣaḥ ।।
taccāha lavaṇetyādi ।।
tāṃ pūrvoditāṃ laghulohakaṭorikāṃ sudṛḍhaṃ yathā syāttathā lavaṇārdramṛdā lavaṇena saindhavādinā yutā yā ārdrā jalasiktā mṛt tayā liptāṃ kurvīta ।।
kimarthaṃ dhūmrarodhāya yathā yantrādbahirdhūmodgamo na syāt ।।
punaḥ sudṛḍhāṅgārān khadirādīnāṃ dattvā bhastrādvayavahninā khalu dvayāgninā dhamyād iti agrimaślokasaṃbandhāt ।।
kva sati nirdhūme sati rase dhūmaniḥsaraṇavarjite sati ।।
taccāha tāvadityādi ।।
sandhiliptā pūrvoktā lohaśarāvikā tāvadavadhau dhmātā kāryā yāvatkālapramāṇaṃ raktābhā raktadyutiyuktā khoṭikā bhavati khoṭasyeva ākṛtiryasyāḥ sā khoṭikā ।।
tato'nantaraṃ kaṭorikāṃ svabhāvaśītalāṃ svato himāṃ matvā jñātvā punaraṅgārānapanīya apasārya kaṭorikāmutkhanya raso grāhya iti śeṣaḥ āgamiślokasaṃbandhāt ।।
taccāha utkhanyetyādi ।।
tato'nantaraṃ laghulohakaṭorikāṃ pūrvavarṇitāṃ utkhanyotkhanya prabalatvenotpāṭya rasaḥ sūto grāhyaḥ ।।
utkhanyotkhanyeti kaṭhinataratvādvā atyādareṇa vīpsā ।।
kutaḥ kaṭorikāsakāśāt eṣa itthamutpanno mṛtasūtarājo jñeyaḥ ।।
sa ca sukhādhmātaḥ san golakavadbhavati vajramūṣāyāṃ iti śeṣaḥ ।।
kācaḥ pratītaḥ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ saubhāgyaṃ tataḥ raso ati maryādāmatikramya dhmātaḥ san ekaraso bhavati samarasa ityarthaḥ ।।
keṣāṃ śikhigalatāṃ śikhini galantīti vigrahaḥ śikhigalatāṃ dhātūnāṃ evaṃ galite rase triguṇaṃ vaṅgaṃ raṅgaṃ dadyāt tato vaṅgadānānantaraṃ krameṇa alpamalpadānena nāgaṃ sīsakaṃ ca dadyāditi ।।
taccāha paścādityādi ।।
paścāt triguṇasīsakadānānantaraṃ hemnā kanakena saha rasabījaṃ mahābījaṃ yojyaṃ hemnā sārdhaṃ mahābījaṃ kīdṛgbhavati ।।

mercury māraṇa
tālakasūtenāpi ca kṛtvā vaṭikāṃ niyāmakauṣadhibhiḥ ।।
evaṃ nigṛhya dhūmaṃ sudhiyā rasamāraṇaṃ kāryam ।
rasabandhakaraṃ pāradabandhapradaṃ ca punaḥ tālakaṃ haritālaṃ sūto rasaḥ tenāpi niyāmakauṣadhibhiśca śatāvaryādibhiḥ pūrvoktābhir guṭikāṃ kṛtvā nigṛhya dhūmaṃ rundhitadhūmaṃ yathā syāttathā sudhiyā matimatā rasajñena evamamunā vidhinā rasamāraṇaṃ kāryaṃ pāradabandhaḥ kārya ityarthaḥ ।।

mercury māraṇa
athavā śilayā sūto mākṣikayogena vā siddhaḥ ।
jāyeta śuklavarṇo dhūmarodhena tābhyāṃ vā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha athavetyādi ।।
athavā vidhyantare śilayā manohvayā kṛtvā vā mākṣikayogena tāpyasaṃyogaṃ kṛtvā sādhitastālakayogavat sūto rasaḥ śuklavarṇo jayeta ।।
kena dhūmarodhena saindhavārdramṛdā lepena vā tābhyāṃ śilāmākṣikābhyām ubhābhyāṃ tālakayogavat sādhitaḥ san sūtaḥ śuklavarṇo bhaved iti ।।

mercury mṛta medic use
mṛtaśulvatāpyacūrṇaṃ kāntayutaṃ tena rañjayetkhoṭam ।
nirvyūḍhaṃ ghanasatvahemayutaṃ tadrasāyane yojyam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha mṛtetyādi ।।
mṛtaśulbatāpyacūrṇaṃ mṛtaṃ ca yat śulbaṃ tāmraṃ tāpyaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ ca taccūrṇaṃ kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ kāntayutaṃ cumbakamiśritaṃ tena mṛtaśulbatāpyacūrṇena kāntayutena pūrvaṃ niṣpannaṃ khoṭaṃ rañjayet ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ ghanasattvahemayutaṃ abhrasatvasvarṇamiśritam ।।
evaṃvidhaṃ tatkhoṭaṃ rasāyane jarāvyādhināśane yojyam ।।

??
balinā triguṇena rasāt parpaṭikayutena marditaṃ sūtam ।
niyāmakadivyauṣadhibhiśchāyāśuṣkā kṛtā vaṭikā ।।
??
mūṣādhṛtaparpaṭikāmadhye saṃchādya nigūḍhasudṛḍhena ।
dhmātaṃ gacchati khoṭaṃ hemayutaṃ sūtabandhakaram ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha balinetyādi ।।
triguṇena balinā gandhakena saha rasaṃ sūtaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ yathā syāttathā marditaṃ kuryāt ityadhyāhāraḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭena balinā parpaṭikayutena parpaṭiko lohaparpaṭikaḥ pratītastena yutena militena niyamasaṃskāroktāḥ niyamakāḥ divyauṣadhayaḥ śatāvarīpramukhās tābhiḥ tato vaṭikā chāyāśuṣkā kāryā chāyāgharmarūpā śuṣkā nīrasā tathā kāryā iti ।।
anyaccāha mūṣetyādi ।।
mūṣādhṛtaparpaṭikā mūṣāyāṃ yā parpaṭikā pūrvoktalohaparpaṭikā sā nigūḍhasudṛḍhena nigūḍhaścāsau sudṛḍhaśca tena mūlakādikṣārabiḍena kṛtvā madhye svāntaḥ ācchādya dhmātaṃ kriyate punas tadūdhmātaṃ sat khoṭaṃ gacchati khoṭatvamāpnoti ।।
tatkhoṭaṃ hemayutaṃ svarṇamilitaṃ sūtabandhakaraṃ syāt rasabandhanapradam ityarthaḥ ।।

mercury māraṇa, khoṭa
baliyuktā parpaṭikā mṛditā snuhyarkabhāvitā guṭikā ।
madhye gartā kāryā sūtabhṛtācchāditā tadanu ।।
bāhye dattvā nigaḍaṃ suliptamūṣodare dṛḍhaṃ nyastam ।
sūtaḥ puṭito mriyate dhmātaḥ khoṭaṃ bhavatyeva ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha balītyādi ।।
pūrvoktā yā parpaṭikā lohaparpaṭikā baliyuktā gandhakamiśritā snuhyarkabhāvitā ca snuhī vajrī arko mandāras tābhyāṃ bhāvitā plutā etayoḥ payaseti bhāvaḥ mṛditā ca gharṣitā ca evaṃ kṛtavidhānā parpaṭikā sati guṭikā vaṭikā kāryā madhye guṭikāntaḥ gartā kāryā sā gartā tataḥ sūtabhṛtā sūtapūritā satī tadanu gartakaraṇānantaraṃ ācchāditā kāryā parpaṭikayeti bhāvaḥ ।।
taccāha bāhya ityādi ।।
bāhye sūtodaraguṭikopari nigaḍaṃ dattvā suliptamūṣodare suliptā sāraṇakarmābhihitauṣadhīriti śeṣaḥ evaṃvidhā yā mūṣā tasyā yadudaraṃ tasmindṛḍhaṃ yathā syāttathā nigaḍaṃ nyastaṃ sthāpitaṃ kuryāditi śeṣaḥ ।।
mūṣodaraguṭikāntasthaḥ sūtaḥ puṭito vahniyogāt mriyate pañcatvamāpnoti ।।
punaḥ dhmātaḥ san khoṭo bhavati ।।
evāvyayamanyaniṣedhavāci ।।

mercury māraṇa, khoṭa
evaṃ tālaśilābhyāṃ mākṣikarasakaiśca daradaśikhisahitaiḥ ।
mriyate puṭasaṃyogād dhmātaṃ khoṭaṃ kṛtaṃ vimalam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha evamityādi ।।
evaṃ lohaparpaṭikāvidhānena tālaśilābhyāṃ dhmātaṃ sat yutaṃ yat khoṭaṃ tadvimalaṃ malavarjitaṃ syāt ।।
ca punaḥ mākṣikarasakaistāpyakharparikaiḥ daradaśikhisahitaiśca hiṅgulaśikhimilitaiśca karaṇarūpairvimalaṃ ca punaḥ puṭayogād vahnisaṃparkāt dhmātaṃ mriyate ।।
ādau malalakṣaṇamuktam ।।

mercury māraṇa
kiṭṭakapurasaṃyogād dhmātaiḥ kiṭṭastu kiṭṭataḥ satvam ।
nipatati satvaṃ rasasākaṃ janayati tadbhasma tasyāpi ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī
taccāha kiṭṭapurasaṃyogāt ।।
kiṭṭaṃ lohamalaṃ puro gugguluḥ tayoḥ saṃyogāt dhmātaiḥ mākṣikarasadaradarūpaiḥ pūrvoktaiḥ kiṭṭo bhavet punaḥ kiṭṭato rasasākaṃ sūtamiśritaṃ sattvaṃ sāraṃ nipatati tatsattvaṃ bhasma janayati utpādayati ।।
tasyāpi bhasmanaḥ sattvaṃ ca nipatatītyarthaḥ ।।

rañjana with smoke and without mercury 
vaṅgarasagandhatālaṃ khaṭikāyā yogataḥ suparpaṭikā ।
rañjayati satvatālaṃ dhūmena vināpi sūtam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha vaṅgarasagandhatālamiti ।।
vaṅgaṃ trapu rasaḥ sūtaḥ gandhako baliḥ tālaṃ haritālaṃ etaccatuṣṭayaṃ khaṭikāyā yogataḥ khaṭikā citrakarajastasyā yogataḥ suparpaṭikāṃ pūrvoktāṃ lohaparpaṭikāṃ rañjayati sūtena vināpi kimuta rasamilitena tālasattveneti vyaktiḥ ।।

bīja for rañjana
evaṃ khoṭaṃ bījaṃ kṛtvā rañjanavidhinā surañjanaṃ kāryam ।
triguṇaṃ rasasya hema saṃyojyaṃ tasya varabījam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

mahābījānāṃ bījānāṃ ca viśeṣavidhānamāha evamityādi ।।
evam uktavidhānena bījaṃ vidhāya rañjanavidhinā rañjanavidhānena surañjanaṃ kāryam ।।
tatkārye rasasya sūtasya triguṇaṃ hema saṃyojyaṃ punas tasya hemnaḥ triguṇaṃ varabījaṃ yojyaṃ iti viśeṣavidhiḥ ।।

abhra sattva druti causes bandhana of mercury

vakṣye tvabhrakasatvād vimaladrutim akhilaguṇagaṇādhārām ।
sā hi nibadhnāti rasaṃ saṃmilitā milati ca sukhena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

bhāratī bharatakhaṇḍamaṇḍitā pacaremānandamañjarī ।
kastayā na rasamalaṃ kuto jayā vakrapadmamadhisthayā sadā ।।
bāhyadrutipraśaṃsāmāha vakṣya ityādi ।।
ahaṃ kaviḥ abhrakasattvādgaganasārato vimaladrutiṃ pakṣe vimalā cāsau drutiśceti vigrahaḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭāṃ akhilaguṇagaṇādhārām akhilāśca te guṇagaṇāśca guṇapaṭalāśca teṣāṃ yā ādhārā tāṃ bahavo guṇās tiṣṭhantyasyāmiti vyaktiḥ ।।
sā rasabhūtā drutiḥ rasaṃ sūtāṃ nibadhnāti niścayena badhnātītyarthaḥ ।।
kiṃbhūtā satī ।।
militā satī tulyamiśritā satī punaḥ drutiḥ sukhena milati patrāder durmilāpatvāt ।।

abhra sattva druti production
vajravallyāḥ svarasena gaganaṃ sauvarcalānvitaṃ piṣṭam ।
paripakvaṃ niculapuṭairnirlepaṃ bhavati rasarūpam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

drutividhānamāha vajravallyā ityādi ।।
vajravallyāḥ svarasena svakīyena rasena gaganamabhrasattvaṃ sauvarcalānvitaṃ rucakasahitaṃ piṣṭaṃ kuryāt iti śeṣaḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ gaganaṃ niculapuṭair vetasadravabhāvanābhiḥ pakvaṃ vahnipuṭitaṃ tatpakvaṃ san nirlepaṃ saṃparkavarjitaṃ rasarūpaṃ bhavati pāradasya rūpamityarthaḥ ।।

abhra sattva druti production
ajajalaśatapariplāvitakapitindukacūrṇavāpamātreṇa ।
drutajātamabhrakasatvaṃ mūṣāyāṃ rasanibhaṃ bhavati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha ajetyādi ।।
drujātarabhrakasattvaṃ abhrakasatvaṃ gaganasāraṃ mūṣāyāṃ vajrasaṃjñāyāṃ drutaṃ sat rasasaṃnibhaṃ bhavati pāradabhūtam ityarthaḥ ।।
kena ajajalaśataparibhāvitakapitindukacūrṇavāpamātreṇa ajaḥ chāgastasya jalena mūtreṇa śataṃ śatavāraṃ paribhāvitaṃ gharmapuṭitaṃ yatkapitindukacūrṇaṃ tasya vāpamātreṇa drute'bhrasattve vāpe ।।

abhra sattva druti production
nijarasaśataplāvitakañcukikandotthacūrṇakṛtaparivāpam ।
drutamāste'bhrakasattvaṃ tadvatsarvāṇi lohāni ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

abhrakasattvaṃ vahniyogena drutaṃ āste dravarūpamevāvatiṣṭhate ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ sattvaṃ nijarasaśataparibhāvitetyādi nijarasena svakīyadraveṇa paribhāvitaṃ yatkañcukikandotthacūrṇaṃ tasya āvāpena yathā śatabhāvitakañcukikandotthacūrṇena sattvaṃ drutamāste tadvatsarvāṇi lohāni drutāni tiṣṭhanti ।।

abhra sattva druti production
gaganaṃ cikuratailaghṛṣṭaṃ gomayaliptaṃ ca kuliśamūṣāyām ।
sudhmātamatra sattvaṃ plavati jalākāramacireṇa ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha gaganetyādi ।।
gaganaṃ abhrasāraṃ cikuratailaghṛṣṭaṃ cikuratailaṃ keśatailaṃ pratītaṃ grantheṣu tena ghṛṣṭaṃ marditaṃ gomayaliptaṃ gomayena liptaṃ yathā syāttathā kuliśamūṣāyāṃ vajrābhidhānāyāṃ sudhmātaṃ sat acireṇālpakālena jalākāraṃ bhavatītyanvayaḥ ।।

abhra sattva druti general rule
gaganadrutiriha satve jñeyo hi rasasya sampradāyo ayam ।
prathamaṃ nipātya satvaṃ deyo vāpo drute tasmin ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sāmānyenābhradrutividhānamāha gaganetyādi ।।
ihāsmin śāstre sattve gaganasāre jāte sāṅgatayā gaganadrutiḥ bhavatītyadhyāhāryam ।।
ayaṃ pratyakṣāntargataḥ hi niścitaṃ rasasya sūtasya saṃpradāyo jñeyaḥ ।।
punaḥ prathamādau sattvaṃ abhrasāraṃ nipātya tasmindrute sattve vahninā dravarūpe sati vāpaḥ kāryaḥ kathitauṣadhīnāṃ iti śeṣaḥ ।।

gold druti
suragopakadeharajaḥ suradāliphalaiḥ samāṃśakairdeyaḥ ।
vāpo drute suvarṇe drutamāste tadrasaprakhyam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha suvarṇadrutividhānamāha suragopakadeharaja iti ।।
indragopaśarīracūrṇaṃ suradālīphalaiḥ samāṃśakaiḥ suragopacūrṇatulyabhāgaiḥ kṛtvā vāpo deyaḥ drute satyuparikṣepa iti suvarṇe vāpe kṛte suvarṇaṃ drutamāste kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ rasaprakhyaṃ jalatulyam ityarthaḥ ।।

gold druti
atha nijarasaparibhāvitasuradālīcūrṇavāpamātreṇa ।
drutamevāste kanakaṃ labhate bhūyo na kaṭhinatvam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha athetyādi ।।
athendragopadevadālīyogakathanānantaraṃ kanakaṃ hema nijarasaparibhāvitaṃ yat suradālīcūrṇaṃ tasya vāpamātreṇa galite hemni kṣepamātreṇa drutamevāste galitam evāvatiṣṭhatītyarthaḥ punaḥ kanakaṃ kāṭhinyaṃ sthiratvaṃ na labhate iti cirakālaprayojanam ।।

tīkṣṇaloha druti
suradālībhasma galitaṃ triḥsaptakṛtvātha gojalaṃ śuṣkam ।
vāpena salilasadṛśaṃ kurute mūṣāgataṃ tīkṣṇam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī
atha tīkṣṇavidhānamāha suradālītyādi ।।
suradālībhasmagalitaṃ suradālī devadālī tasyāḥ bhasma dāhasambhūtaṃ tena galitaṃ trisaptakṛtvā ekaviṃśativāraṃ gojalaṃ surabhimūtraṃ bhāvitaṃ kuryādityadhyāhāraḥ ।।
atha mūṣāgataṃ vajrasaṃjñāyāṃ sthitaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ sāraṃ vāpena nikṣepaṇena jalasadṛśaṃ jalatulyaṃ kurute karmaviditi śeṣaḥ ।।

mākṣikasattvadruti
kūrmāsthiśilājatukameṣīmṛgago'sthivāpitā kāñcī ।
jalasadṛśī bhavati sadā vāpo deyo drutāyāṃ tu ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha mākṣikadrutividhānamāha kūrmetyādi ।।
kūrmāsthi śilājatukaṃ pratītaṃ meṣī meṣapatnī mṛgo hariṇaḥ gauḥ pratītā pratīto vā teṣāṃ yānyasthīni tair nirvāpitā yā kāñcī svarṇamākṣikaṃ sā jalasadṛśī bhavati kiyatkālaparimāṇaṃ sadā nityaṃ punaḥ drutāyāṃ galitāyāṃ vāpo deyaḥ vāpo nikṣepaṇam ।।

abhra druti alchem properties
abhrakadrutiraviśeṣā nirlepā yojitā samāsāttu ।
āroṭaṃ rasarājaṃ badhnāti hi dvandvayogena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sāmānyābhradruter adhikāramāha abhradrutirityādi ।।
gaganadravaḥ aviśeṣā sāmānyāpi vidhānena kṛtā nirlepā asparśā samā sūtatulyabhāgayojitā satī āroṭaṃ rasanajaṃ pūrvasaṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛtaṃ sūtaṃ badhnāti kena dvandvayogena ubhayamelāpakauṣadhena ।।
hiśabdo yuktārtha iti ।।

receipe for dvandvana of druti and mercury
kṛṣṇāgarunābhisitai rasonasitarāmaṭhairimā drutayaḥ ।
soṣṇe milanti rasena mṛditāḥ strīkusumapalāśabījarasaiḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

pūrvoktānāṃ melanam āha kṛṣṇetyādi ।।
imā drutayaḥ soṣṇatuṣakarīṣādinā tāpite khalve mṛditāḥ satyo milanti rasena saha tathā kāryam ।।
kaiḥ kṛtvā kṛṣṇāgarunābhisitaiḥ ।।
kṛṣṇāgarukastūrikāghanasāraiḥ kṛtvā na kevalametaiḥ rasonasitarāmaṭhaiśca laśunaśarkarāhiṅgubhiḥ punaḥ strīkusumapalāśabījarasaiḥ strīkusumaṃ ca palāśasya bījāni ca rasaśceti dvaṃdvaḥ etaistribhiryogaiḥ pṛthagbhūtairmilanti sarvaiśceti ।।

mercury baddha causes longevity
iti baddho rasarājo guñjāmātropayojito nityam ।
ekenaiva palena tu kalpāyutajīvitaṃ kurute ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

itthaṃ baddharasarājasya māhātmyamāha itītyādi ।।
iti pūrvoktena drutividhānena baddho rasarājaḥ sūtaḥ ekena palena ṣoḍaśikayā kalpāyutaṃ jīvitaṃ kurute kalpānām ayutaṃ sahasraparimāṇaṃ jīvitamiti ।।
kasmāt nityaṃ yathā syāttathā guñjāmātropayogataḥ dinaṃ dinaṃ prati raktikāparimāṇasya rasasya yo'sau upayogastena ।।

atha pūrvoktagrāsakramājjarate raso vidhivat ।
etāḥ pūrvadrutayo bhavanti rasarājaphaladāśca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhinā grāsajārito raso guṇavānityāha athetyādi ।।
atha drutiyogānantaraṃ rasaḥ sūtaḥ pūrvoktagrāsakramāt yojitakavalakramāt vidhivat śāstroktavidhānena biḍādinā jarate ca punaretāḥ pūrvoktadrutayo rasarājaphaladā bhavanti sūte prayuktāḥ phaladāḥ syurityarthaḥ ।।

drutijāraṇa vedha potency
samajīrṇaḥ śatavedhī dviguṇena rasaḥ sahasravedhī ca ।
kramaśo hi koṭivedhī dviguṇadviguṇadruteścaraṇāt ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

adhikadruter jāraṇād adhikaguṇe raso bhavatītyāha samajīrṇa iti ।।
iti samā tulyabhāgā drutirjīrṇā yasminniti ।।
drute dviguṇā yā drutiḥ tasyāścaraṇāt kramaśaḥ koṭivedhī koṭyaṃśena vedhakaḥ syāt ।।
drutibhāgo vṛddhau hyadhikaḥ syāditi vyaktiḥ ।।

ṣoḍaśa vā dvātriṃśadvā grāsā jīrṇāścatuḥṣaṣṭiḥ ।
vidhyati tadā rasendro lohaṃ dhūmāvalokanataḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

grāsavṛddhyā guṇānāha ṣoḍaśetyādi ।।
yadā ṣoḍaśagrāsā vā dvātriṃśadgrāsā vā catuḥṣaṣṭigrāsā jīrṇā jāraṇamāpannā bhavanti tadā rasendraḥ sūtaḥ lohaṃ dhātusaṃjñakaṃ vidhyati vedhaṃ karoti kutaḥ dhūmāvalokanataḥ dhūmasya yadavalokanaṃ darśanaṃ ।।

sāraṇa motivation

iti rakto'pi rasendro jāritabījo'pi sāraṇārahitaḥ ।
vyāpī na bhavati dehe loheṣvapyathavāpi hi ṣaṇḍhatāṃ yāti ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

mano manīṣāyatam āyatātmanā samācaretkarma paropakārī ।
arcīva śobhāṃ labhate parātparāṃ parāpavādādapi saṃnivṛttaḥ ।।
sūte satailayantrasthe svarṇādikṣepaṇaṃ ca yat ।
vedhādhikyakaraṃ lohe sāraṇaṃ tatprakīrtitam ।
iti paribhāṣā ।।
sāraṇamutkṛṣṭaṃ matvā stuvannāha itītyādi ।।
iti pūrvoktena vidhānena rakto'pi rāgavānapi rasendraḥ sūtaḥ jaritabījo'pi jāritāni bījāni yasminniti sāraṇarahitaḥ sāraṇā vakṣyamāṇasaṃskārastena varjitaḥ vyāpī na bhavati dehe lohe ca vyāpako na syāt hi niścitaṃ athavāpi sāraṇārahito rasendraḥ ṣaṇḍhatāṃ yāti nirvīryatvam āpnoti ।।

sāraṇātaila
maṇḍūkamatsyakacchapameṣajalaukāhisūkarādīnām ।
saṃyojyaikasya vasāṃ tataḥ pacetsāraṇātailam ।।
jyotiṣmatīvibhītakakarañjakaṭutumbītailamekasmāt ।
dviguṇitaraktakaṣāyaṃ kṣīreṇa caturguṇena pacet ।।
raktavarga
dāḍimapalāśabandhukakusumarajanībhir aruṇasahitābhiśca ।
mañjiṣṭhālākṣārasacandanasahito'pi raktavargo'yam ।।
vidrumabhūnāgamalaṃ viṇmakṣikādhvāṅkṣaśalabhānāṃ ca ।
karṇamalaṃ mahiṣīṇāṃ krameṇa kalkaṃ kalāṃśena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sāraṇāya vasātailamāha maṇḍūketyādi ।।
maṇḍūko bhekaḥ matsyo jalacaraviśeṣaḥ kacchapaḥ kamaṭhaḥ pratītaḥ jalaukāḥ pratītāḥ ahiḥ sarpaḥ sūkaro varāhaḥ ādiśabdād gomahiṣagajoṣṭrakharanarakarkaṭaśiśumārā api grāhyāḥ ।।
atha teṣāṃ madhye ekaikasya pṛthaktvena vasāṃ saṃyojya sāraṇaṃ tailaṃ sāraṇameva tailaṃ tatpacediti vahninā iti śeṣaḥ ।।
sāraṇatailaviśeṣamāha jyotiṣmatītyādi ।।
jyotiṣmatīvibhītakakarañjakaṭutumbītailaṃ jyotiṣmatī kaṅguṇī vibhītakaḥ kalidrumaḥ karañjaḥ pratītaḥ kaṭutumbī kaṭukā yā tumbī etāsāṃ tailaṃ ekaṃ ato dviguṇito yo raktakaṣāyaḥ raktagaṇasya kvāthaḥ taṃ niyojya pūrvasaṃbandhāt ।।
kena saha caturguṇavasayā tathā tailataḥ caturguṇitena dugdhena saha pacet pākaṃ kuryāditi ।।
sāraṇatailavidhānāya raktavargamāha dāḍimetyādi ।।
dāḍimaṃ pratītaṃ palāśo brahmavṛkṣaḥ bandhūkapuṣpaṃ madhyāhnavikāśikusumaṃ rajanī haridrā etābhiḥ aruṇasahitābhiḥ aruṇaṃ āraktaṃ yaddravyaṃ kārpāsakusumādikaṃ tatsahitābhiḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭo'yaṃ raktavargaḥ mañjiṣṭhālākṣārasacandanasahitaḥ mañjiṣṭhā pratītā lākṣārasaḥ alaktakaḥ candanaṃ raktacandanam ।।
sāraṇataile kalkamāha vidrumetyādi ।।
vidrumaṃ latāmaṇir bhūnāgamalaṃ gaṇḍūpadapurīṣaṃ makṣikādhvāṅkṣaśalabhānāṃ makṣikā jīvaviśeṣaḥ dhvāṅkṣāḥ kākāḥ śalabhaḥ pataṅgaḥ iti haimaḥ teṣāṃ viṭ śakṛt punarmahiṣīṇāṃ karṇamalaṃ krameṇa kalāṃśena ṣoḍaśāṃśena kalkaṃ prativāpaṃ dattvā pūrvatailamuttārayet ।।

sāraṇa
paṭagālitaṃ gṛhītvā sūtaṃ sampūrṇadīrghamūṣāyām ।
tadanu khalu taptataile pradrāvya samaṃ kṣiped bījam ।।
mūṣāvaktraṃ sthagayel latādvayaprotavitatanaddhena ।
tailārdrapaṭena tato bījaṃ prakṣipya samakālam ।।
piśitānuguṇaṃ bījaiḥ sāraṇavidhinā niyojitaḥ sūtaḥ ।
akṣīyamāṇo milati ca bījair baddho bhavatyeva ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

siddhatailakṛtyamāha paṭetyādi ।।
tatsiddhatailaṃ paṭagālitaṃ vastrapūtaṃ gṛhītvā tadanu tatpaścāt ।।
sampūrṇadīrghamūṣāyāṃ gostanākārāyāṃ taptataile koṣṇasāraṇataile sūtaṃ kṣipet ।।
kiṃ kṛtvā bījaṃ samaṃ samabhāgaṃ rasatulyaṃ yadbhāvyaṃ mahābījaṃ tat bhāvitaṃ kṛtvetyarthaḥ ।।
sāraṇayantrasya vidhānamāha mūṣetyādi ।
samakālam ekakālaṃ yathā syāttathā bījaṃ mūṣāntarnikṣipya tato'nantaraṃ mūṣāvaktraṃ sthagayet ācchādayet ।।
kena tailārdrapaṭena sāraṇatailārdravastreṇa ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭena latādvayena vastracīradvayena protaṃ ca tadvitataṃ vistīrṇaṃ ca tat naddhaṃ baddhaṃ tena ।।
akṣīyamāṇo milati na kṣīyata ityarthaḥ ।।
sūte milati baddho jñeyaḥ bījaiḥ saha milito baddho bhavatītyarthaḥ ।।
pītādivarṇakathanenāpi kartuṃ sūcitam ।।

mercury pratisāraṇa
tadvadgabhīramūṣe sāraṇatailārdrameva rasarājam ।
sūtāddviguṇaṃ kanakaṃ dattvā pratisārayettadanu ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sūtabījasāraṇānantaraṃ kanakasāraṇamāha tadvadityādi ।।
tadvat pūrvavidhānena gabhīramūṣe dīrghamūṣāyāṃ sāraṇatailārdraṃ sāraṇatailāplutaṃ eva niścayena rasarājaṃ kuryāditi śeṣaḥ ।।
tadanu tatpaścātsūtāddviguṇaṃ yatkanakaṃ hema tadatra dattvā pratisārayetsāraṇaṃ kuryātpūrvavat ।।

mercury anusāraṇa
bījena triguṇena tu sūtakamanusārayetprakāśastham ।
vidhyantaramāha bījenetyādi ।।
prakāśasthaṃ prakāśamūṣāgataṃ sūtaṃ triguṇena bījena anusārayet pratisārayet ।।

īṣannāgaṃ deyaṃ trividhāyāṃ sāraṇāyāṃ tu ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

kiṃ kṛtvā īṣadalpaṃ nāgaṃ dattvā trividhāyāṃ sāraṇāyāmevaṃ vidheyam iti ।।

sāraṇāyantra
kṛtvā mūṣāṃ dīrghāṃ bandhitatribhāgapraṇālikāṃ tāṃ ca ।
tasyāgre prakaṭamūṣā sacchidrā sudṛḍhamṛttikāliptā ।।
tasminprakṣipya rasaṃ sāraṇatailānvitaṃ tapte ।
pradrāvya tulyakanakaṃ kṣipte'smin milati rasarājaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sāraṇayantramāha kṛtvetyādi ।।
prathamaṃ dīrghāṃ mūṣāṃ kṛtvā ca punaḥ tāṃ bandhitatribhāgapraṇālikāṃ bandhitā tribhāge praṇālikā yasyāḥ sā tāṃ ca kṛtvā tasyāgre yantrasyāgre praṇālikāyāṃ mūṣāntarityarthaḥ ।।
sudṛḍhamṛttikāliptā sacchidrā randhrasahitā prakaṭamūṣā prakāśamūṣā kāryeti yantram ।।
tasminyantre sāraṇatailānvitaṃ rasaṃ prakṣipya tato'nantaraṃ tulyaṃ kanakaṃ pradrāvya gālayitvā tasminneva tapte yantre kṣipte sati raso milati ekatāṃ yāti ।।

sāraṇāyantra
kṛtvā nalikāṃ dīrghāṃ ṣaḍaṃgulāṃ dhūrtakusumasaṃkāśām ।
mūṣāpyadho vilagnā kartavyā vai mṛdā lepyā ।।
aparā sūkṣmā nalikā kāryā saptāṃgulā sudṛḍhā ।
madhye praviśati ca yathā tadvatkāryā ca dṛḍhamukhā ।।
tasminsūtaḥ kṣiptaḥ sāraṇatailānvito madanaruddhamukhaḥ ।
tadanu bṛhattamayā hema pradrāvya hemakoṣṭhikayā ।।
tasminmadhye kṣiptvā nalikāgramadhomukhīṃ kuryāt ।
antarūrdhvaṃ bhārākrāntāṃ sarati raso nātra saṃdehaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyadyantramāha kṛtvetyādi ।।
pūrvavaddīrghāṃ dhūrtakusumasaṃkāśāṃ dhattūrapuṣpasaṃkāśāṃ pūrvayantranalikāyāḥ sthāne evaṃvidhāṃ ṣaḍaṅgulāṃ nalikāṃ kuryād iti vyaktiḥ ।।
mūṣāpi adho vilagnā nalikāyāstalabhāge mūṣā vilagnā saṃlagnā kāryā ।।
sā ca mṛdā mṛtsnayā lepyā ।।
punarapi aparā sūkṣmā nālikā saptāṅgulā saptāṅgulaparimāṇā sudṛḍhā manoharakaṭhinā kāryā yathā madhye ṣaḍaṅgulanālikāntaḥ praviśati tadvattathā kāryā ।।
kiṃbhūtā dṛḍhamukhā dṛḍhaṃ mukhaṃ yasyāḥ sā evaṃrūpā tasmin saṃsiddhe yantre sāraṇatailānvitaḥ sūtaḥ kṣiptaḥ san madanaruddhamukhaḥ kāryaḥ madanena sikthakena ruddhaṃ mudritaṃ mukhaṃ yasya saḥ ।।
tadanu tatpaścāt hemakoṣṭhikayā hemno yā koṣṭhī eva koṣṭhikā tayā hema svarṇaṃ pradrāvya drāvayitvā tatra kṣipet ityadhyāhāryam ।।
tasminyantre madhye'ntaḥ nalikāgraṃ nalikāyāḥ saptāṅgulāyā agrabhāgaṃ kṣiptvā adhomukhīṃ kuryāt punarūrdhvaṃ bhārākrāntāṃ kuryāt ।।
iti kṛte sati rasaḥ sarati hemnā milati na saṃdehaḥ niyatamityarthaḥ ।।

sāraṇāyantra
kṛtvāṣṭāṃgulamūṣāṃ dhūrtakusumopamāṃ dṛḍhāṃ ślakṣṇām ।
aparā madhyagatāpi ca sacchidrā ca saptāṃgulā kāryā ।।
niruddhatāṃ ca kṛtvā sūtaṃ prakṣipya tailasaṃyuktam ।
nirdhūmaṃ karṣāgnau sthāpya mūṣāṃ susaṃdhitāṃ kṛtvā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyadyantravidhānamāha kṛtvetyādi ।।
aṣṭāṅgulamūṣāṃ aṣṭāṅgulaparimāṇadīrghāṃ dhūrtakusumopamāṃ kanakapuṣpasadṛśāṃ dṛḍhāṃ kaṭhināṃ ślakṣṇāṃ masṛṇāṃ evaṃvidhāṃ mūṣāṃ kṛtvā aparā dvitīyā saptāṅgulā saptāṅgulaparimāṇadīrghā sacchidrā randhrayuktā sā madhyagatā antaḥpraviṣṭā kāryā apītyavaśyaṃ iti mūṣādvayayantraṃ siddham ।।
taccāha pūrvoktāyāmantaḥpraviṣṭāyāṃ saptāṅgulāyāṃ sūtaṃ tailasaṃyuktaṃ sāraṇatailasahitaṃ prakṣipya niruddhatāṃ ca kṛtvā nirdhūmaṃ yathā syāt tathā karṣāgnau mūṣāṃ sthāpya punaḥ kiṃ kṛtvā susaṃdhitāṃ sandhimudritāṃ kṛtvā pūrvavatsārayedityarthaḥ ।।

sāraṇāyantra
vitastimātranalikāpi kāryā sudṛḍhe tadagrato mūṣe ।
uttānaikā kāryā niśchidrā chidramudritā ca tanau ।।
dattvā sūtaṃ pūrvaṃ sāraṇatailānvitaṃ nidhāpya bhuvi ।
uttānāyāṃ mūṣāyāṃ tasyāṃ bījaṃ samāvṛtya ।।
svacchaṃ jñātvā ca tatastadbījaṃ chidrasaṃsthitaṃ kuryāt ।
bījaṃ sūtasyopari nipatati badhnātyasaṃdeham ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyayantravidhānamāha mūṣe kārye ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭe tadagrato vitastimātranalike vitastiparimāṇe nalike yayoste evaṃvidhe sudṛḍhe ubhe kārye ityabhiprāyaḥ ।।
tayormadhye ekā mūṣā uttānā kāryā aparā nimneti bhāvaḥ ।।
uttānā kiṃviśiṣṭā niśchidrā nirvraṇā chidramudritā chidraṃ mudritaṃ yasyāṃ tanau mūṣāśarīre iti ।।
taccāha pūrvaṃ prathamaṃ sūtaṃ yantre pūrvokte sāraṇatailānvitaṃ dattvā bhuvi nidhāpya tasyāṃ uktāyāṃ uttānāyāṃ mūṣāyāṃ bījaṃ mahābījaṃ samāvṛtya dravīkṛtya dattvetyarthaḥ ।।
tato'nantaraṃ bījaṃ svacchamamalaṃ dravarūpaṃ jñātvā chidrasaṃsthitaṃ kuryāt chidrāntaḥ kṣipedityabhiprāyaḥ chidrāntaḥkṣepaṇāt bījaṃ rasasyopari patati sati sūtaṃ asaṃdehaṃ yathā syāttathā badhnāti bīje chidrāntaḥkṣepaṇānantaraṃ chidramacchidraṃ syādityarthaḥ ।।

sāraṇā 
sā ca prakāśamūṣā nyubjā kāryārdhāṅgulasaṃniviṣṭā ।
nalikā kāryā vidhinā ūrdhve sūtastvadho bījam ।।
mūṣāṃ nirudhya vidhinā dhmātā koṣṭhe drutaṃ bījam ।
jñātvā parivartya tato nibadhnāti sūtarājaṃ ca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

setyādi ।।
punaḥ sā vitastimātranalikā prakāśamūṣā ardhāṅgulasuniviṣṭā mūṣāntaḥ praviṣṭā nyubjā adhomukhī kāryā tasyāḥ prakāśamūṣāyāḥ nalikā praṇālikā vidhinā śāstravārtikasaṃpradāyena kāryā yathordhve sūto bhavedadho bījamityarthaḥ mūṣām ityādi ।।
mūṣāṃ nirudhya randhraṃ dūrīkṛtya vidhinā koṣṭhe koṣṭhīyantre sā mūṣā dhmātā kāryā drutaṃ dravarūpaṃ kṛtaṃ bījaṃ jñātvā parivartya ca mūṣāyāṃ bījasya parivartanaṃ kṛtvā tato bījaṃ sūtarājaṃ badhnātīti ।।

sāraṇā with ḍamaruyantra
athavā ḍamarukayantre sāraṇavidhinā niyojitaḥ sūtaḥ ।
sarati rasendro vidhinā jñātvā tatkarmakauśalyam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

athānyadyantram āha athavetyādi ।।
vidhinā sāraṇavidhānena ḍamarukayantre uktalakṣaṇapātanakaraṇocite yantre sūto niyojitaḥ san sarati bījena milati ।।

jāraṇā after sāraṇā vedha potency
tatsāritaṃ rasendraṃ grāsavidhānena jārayettadanu ।
punarapi sāritasūto vidhyati koṭyaṃśataḥ śulbam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

kiṃ kṛtvā rasendro niyojitaḥ jñātvā tatkarmakauśalyaṃ rasendrakarmaprāvīṇyaṃ jñātveti ।।

sāraṇā with krāmaṇāvasā
krāmaṇavasādiyogādvidhinā sūtaḥ saratyeva ।
capalatvātilaghutvādbījaṃ yato'tha vipluṣaḥ kāryaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

pūrvoktaṃ dṛḍhīkartumāha krāmaṇetyādi ।।
sūto vidhinoktavidhānena krāmaṇocitā yā vasā maṇḍūkādīnāṃ tā eva ādayo yeṣāṃ teṣāṃ yogātsarati sāraṇā syāt punarbījayuto'pi sūtaḥ capalatvātilaghutvāt capalatvaṃ cañcalatvaṃ ca atilaghutvaṃ ca tasmāddhetoḥ avipluṣaḥ sthiraḥ kāryaḥ ।।

sāraṇa, krāmaṇa with lead etc
sarati sukhena ca sūto dahati mukhaṃ naiva hastapādādi ।
kramati rasaḥ phaṇiyogānmākṣikayutahemagairikayā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

pūrvoktaguṇānāha saratītyādi ।।
pūrvavidhānā sūtaḥ sarati sāritaḥ sūto mukhaṃ na dahati hastapādādi ca aṅgavibhāgaṃ naiva dahati ।।
punaḥ phaṇiyogāt nāgasaṃyogataḥ mākṣikayutahemagairikayā saha tāpyamilitasvarṇagairikayā sārdhaṃ krāmati ।।

druti, sāraṇā
mākṣīkasattvayogātphaṇiyogānnāgavad dravati śīghram ।
dravati ca kanake sūtaḥ saṃsāryate vidhinā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sukhena sāraṇavidhānamāha mākṣiketyādi ।।
kanakaṃ hema mākṣikasattvayogāt phaṇisaṃyogānnāgasaṃyogācca śīghraṃ dravati kanake dravati sati vidhinā sāraṇatailādinā saṃsāryate sāraṇā kriyata iti ।।

mercury preparation for vedha
tasmād dravyavidhāyī sūto bījena sārito laghunā ।
samasāritaḥ subaddho mūṣāyāṃ syātsamāvartaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sāraṇayā pāradaguṇānāha tasmādityādi ।।
tasmāddhetoḥ sūto dravyavidhāyī syāt iti śeṣaḥ dravyakartetyartha ।।
alaghunā bījena analpaparimāṇena mahābījena sāritaḥ san samasāritaḥ san baddho bhavet ityadhyāhāraḥ ।।
mūṣāyāṃ samāvarto dravaṇaṃ syāt vahnidhamanāt iti śeṣaḥ ।।

sāraṇā
sāritavartitasūtaḥ samānabījena milati yaḥ sāryaḥ ।
dviguṇena pratisāryaḥ sa cānusāryaśca triguṇena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sāraṇakramamāha sarityādi ।।
sāritavartitasūtaḥ sāritaścāsau vartitaś ceti vigrahaḥ ।।
yaḥ samānabījena tulyamahābījena milati sa sāryaḥ yo dviguṇena milati saḥ pratisāryaḥ yaśca triguṇena so'nusārya iti sāraṇākramo darśitaḥ ।।

sāraṇa vedha potency
śatavedhī sāryaḥ pratisāritaḥ syātsahasravedhī ca ।
anusārito'yutena ca vidhināpi balābalaṃ jñātvā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sāraṇakramasya guṇānāha śatetyādi ।।
yaḥ sāryaḥ samasāritaḥ sa śatavedhī syād ityabhiprāyaḥ ।।
punaḥ pratisāritaḥ dviguṇabījena sārito yaḥ sūtaḥ sa sahasravedhī syāt ।।
ca punaḥ anusāritaḥ triguṇabījena sāritaḥ sa ayutena ayutavedhī syāditi vyaktiḥ ।।
vidhinā ityuktavidhānena ।।
balābalaṃ jñātvā nyūnādhikyaṃ matvā vidhinā yukta iti śeṣaḥ ।।

anusāritena tu samaḥ svacchaḥ sūtaḥ sāritastadanu ।
sa bhavati lakṣavedhī pratisāritaḥ prayutavedhī ca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

sāritapratisāritādanusāritasya viśeṣamāha anvityādi ।।
tu punaḥ svacchaḥ pradhānasaṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛtaḥ sūtaḥ anusāritena samaḥ triguṇabījena sārito'nusāritastena tulyo yadi syātsa ca lakṣavedhī syāt ।।
evaṃ pratisāritaḥ sūtaḥ samena sārito ayutavedhī syāt ।।
evaṃ svecchātisvacchavṛddhau vedhasyāpi vṛddhiḥ syāditi rahasyam ।।

koṭiṃ vidhyati sūto'pyanusāritaḥ sarati bījena ।
pratisārito'nusārito daśakoṭiṃ vidhyate sūtaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

tathottarasattvena guṇādhikyamāha koṭimityādi ।।
sūte sarito bījena grāsanyāyaṃ vihāya samena bījenānusārito yaḥ sa koṭisaṃkhyāṃ dhātūnāmiti śeṣaḥ sūto vidhyati ।।
yathoktasārite sūte daśaguṇavṛddhiḥ sarvatraiveti veditavyam ।।

pratisāritastathābjaṃ tvanusāritaḥ kharvavedhī ca ।
evaṃ sāraṇayogātkurute vedhaṃ yathepsitaṃ vidhinā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

viśeṣamāha pratītyādi ।।
pratisāritaḥ sūto dviguṇabījena vāraikena sārito rasaḥ abjasaṃkhyāṃ vidhyati ।।
tu punar anusāritaḥ triguṇena bījena vāraikena sāritaḥ sūtaḥ kharvavedhī syāt kharvasaṃkhyāke dravyasaṃbandhaṃ karotītyabhiprāyaḥ ।।
evamuktaprakāreṇa vidhinā śāstrajñavārtikasaṃpradāyena sāraṇayogāt yathepsitaṃ vedhaṃ kurute yathāvāñchitam ityarthaḥ ।।

anusāritena sārito vidhyati śulbaṃ nikharvasaṃkhyākam ।
pratisāritastu vidhyati padmaṃ svanusāritaḥ śaṅkham ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

punarviśeṣamāha anvityādi ।।
anusāritena triguṇaprathamagrāsanyāyena bījena sāritaḥ sūto nikharvasaṃkhyākaṃ śulbaṃ vidhyati tu punaḥ pratisāritaḥ ṣaḍguṇaprathamagrāsanyāyena sāritaḥ sūtaḥ padmasaṃkhyākaṃ vidhyati ।।
punar anusārito navaguṇagrāsanyāyena bījena sāritaḥ sūtaḥ śaṅkhasaṃkhyāṃ vidhyatīti ।।

lead vedha 
vidhyed dviguṇaṃ dravyaṃ nāgaṃ dattvānuvāhayecchanakaiḥ ।
tāvadyāvatkanakaṃ divyaṃ pronmīlayetsakalam ।।

iti paramahaṃsaparivrājakācāryaśrīmadgovindabhagavatpādaviracite rasahṛdayatantre sāraṇātmakaḥ ṣoḍaśo'vabodhaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

punarviśeṣamāha vidhyedityādi ।।
kanakaṃ hema dattvā śanakair nīcais tāvadanuvāhayet yāvaddivyaṃ pravaraṃ kanakaṃ bhavediti śeṣaḥ ।।
punaryāvatsakalaṃ samastaṃ nāgaṃ pronmīlayenniḥśeṣaṃ kuryādityabhiprāyaḥ ।।
punastatkanakaṃ dviguṇaṃ svato dravyaṃ vidhyet vā sūtakena sāritaṃ sat dravyaṃ kanakaṃ śatasahasrādisaṃkhyāto dviguṇasaṃkhyākaṃ dravyaṃ śulbādikaṃ vidhyed iti rahasyam ।।

iti kṛtasāraṇavidhirapi balavānapi sūtarāṭ kriyāyogāt ।
saṃveṣṭya tiṣṭhati lohaṃ no viśati krāmaṇārahitaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

susaṃskṛtā mukhāntaḥsthā viśadāśca hitārthakāḥ ।
tathā parocitāḥ pūtā bhavantyamarajā giraḥ ।।
atha krāmaṇapraśaṃsām āha itītyādi ।।
uktavidhānena kṛtaḥ sāraṇasya vidhir yasmin sūtarāje evaṃvidhiḥ sūtarāṭ balavān bhavediti śeṣaḥ ।।
kutaḥ kriyāyogāt kṛtyakaraṇāt ।।
yādṛk kṛtyaṃ kriyate tādṛk balavān syād ityabhiprāyaḥ ।।
evaṃvidho'pi krāmaṇārahitaḥ krāmaṇavarjito lohaṃ na viśati lohāntaḥpraveśaṃ na karoti tato hetor lohaṃ dhātuṃ saṃveṣṭya pariveṣṭanaṃ kṛtvā tiṣṭhati bāhyarāgadāyī syāditi ।।

annaṃ vā dravyaṃ vā yathānupānena dhātuṣu kramate ।
evaṃ krāmaṇayogādrasarājo viśati loheṣu ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

dehalohayoḥ sādṛśyamāha annamityādi ।।
yatheti sādṛśye ।।
annaṃ godhūmādikaṃ vā dravyaṃ auṣadhaṃ anupānena saha jalādinā sārdhaṃ dhātuṣu māṃsādiṣu saptasu kramate vyāpnoti tathā amunā vakṣyamāṇavidhānena krāmaṇayogāt krāmaṇāya yogaḥ kunaṭīmākṣikaviṣādis tataḥ sūtarājo loharūpyādiṣu viśati bāhyābhyantaraṃ vidhyatītyarthaḥ ।।

krāmaṇayoga 
kāntaviṣarasakadaradai raktailendragopikādyaiśca ।
krāmaṇametacchreṣṭhaṃ lepe kṣepe sadā yojyam ।।
krāmaṇayoga 
kunaṭīmākṣikaviṣaṃ nararudhiraṃ vāyasasya viṣṭhā ca ।
mahiṣīṇāṃ karṇamalaṃ strīkṣīraṃ krāmaṇe balakṛt ।।
krāmaṇayoga 
ṭaṅkaṇakunaṭīrāmaṭhabhūmilatāsaṃyutaṃ mahārudhiram ।
krāmaṇametatkathitaṃ lepe kṣepe sadā yojyam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

krāmaṇayogamāha kāntaviṣetyādi ।।
kāntaṃ cumbakaṃ viṣaṃ kandajaṃ viṣaṃ kandaviṣāṇi kālakūṭādīni trayodaśa daradaṃ hiṅgulaṃ taiḥ ca punaḥ raktatailendragopādyaiḥ rakto raktakavargaḥ tailaṃ kaṅguṇyādeḥ indragopo jīvaviśeṣaḥ ityādyāḥ krāmaṇocitās tacca ।।
etat śreṣṭhaṃ sarvottamaṃ krāmaṇaṃ anena sūtaḥ krāmati viśati loheṣviti vyāptiḥ tatkrāmaṇaṃ kathitam ।।
tallepe kṣepe ca yojyamityarthaḥ ।।

krāmaṇayoga für Gold-।Silberherstellung
śilayā nihato nāgo vaṅgaṃ vā tālakena śuddhena ।
kramaśaḥ pīte śukle krāmaṇametatsamuddiṣṭam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha śilayetyādi ।।
nāgaḥ sīsakaḥ śilayā manohvayā nihato māritaḥ punaḥ vaṅgaṃ śuddhena doṣavarjitena tālena nihataṃ kramaśaḥ krameṇa pīte hemakarmaṇi śukle rūpyakarmaṇi etatkrāmaṇaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ samyak prakāśitaṃ pītakarmaṇi nāgaḥ śuklakarmaṇi vaṅgaṃ ca niyojitavyam ityarthaḥ ।।

krāmaṇa
tīkṣṇaṃ daradena hataṃ śulbaṃ vā tāpyamāritaṃ vidhinā ।
krāmaṇametatkathitaṃ kāntamukhaṃ mākṣikairvāpi ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha tīkṣṇamityādi ।।
daradena hiṅgulena hataṃ māritaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ sāro vidhinā arivargavidhānena tāpyena svarṇamākṣikena māritaṃ śulbaṃ tāmraṃ etadapi krāmaṇaṃ kathitaṃ vā kāntamukhaṃ kāntaṃ lohajāti uktaṃ granthādau tat mukhaṃ pradhānaṃ yasya tat mākṣikairvā māritaṃ niyojyaṃ iti śeṣaḥ ।।

mākṣikasattvaṃ nāgaṃ vihāya na krāmaṇaṃ kimapyasti ।
dalasiddhe rasasiddhe vidhāvasau bhavati khalu saphalaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

viśeṣavidhānamāha mākṣikasattvam ityādi ।।
mākṣikasattvaṃ tāpyasāraṃ nāgaḥ sīsakaḥ taṃ vihāya nānyatkimapyasti krāmaṇaṃ na krāmaṇamiti bhāvaḥ ।।
khalviti jijñāsāyām ।।
dalasiddhe vidhau saṃskāraiḥ pūrṇatāṃ nīte sati asau vidhiḥ saphalaḥ ।।

vedhamahattva

anayā khalu sāraṇayā krāmaṇena ca viśati yojito vidhivat ।
asati vedhavidhau na rasaḥ svaguṇānprakāśayati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vyavāyibheṣajopete dravye kṣipto rasaḥ khalu ।
vedha ityucyate tajjñaiḥ sa ca naikavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
iti paribhāṣā ।।
krāmaṇasaṃskārādhikāramāha anayetyādi ।।
anayā uktayā sāraṇayā saha krāmaṇasaṃskāre kṛte sati raso viśati krāmati punarvedhavidhau kṛte sati rasaḥ svaguṇān prakāśayatīti veditavyam ।।

hemakṛṣṭi
rasadaradatāpyagandhakamanaḥśilārājavarttakaṃ vimalam ।
puṭamṛtaśulbaṃ tāre nirvyūḍhaṃ hemakṛṣṭiriyam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vedhavidhānamāha rasetyādi ।।
rasaḥ sūtaḥ daradaṃ hiṅgulaṃ tāpyaṃ mākṣikaṃ gandhakaḥ pratītaḥ manaḥśilā manohvā rājavarttakaṃ rājāvartaṃ vimalaṃ raupyamākṣikaṃ ekavadbhāvadvandvaḥ ।।
puṭamṛtaśulbaṃ rasādīnāṃ puṭena mṛtamityarthaḥ ।।
evaṃvidhaṃ śulbaṃ tāre nirvāhitaṃ iyaṃ hemakṛṣṭiḥ svarṇakaraṇamityarthaḥ ।।

śatāṃśavidhi।-vedha 
aṣṭānavatirbhāgāstārastveko'pi kanakabhāgaḥ syāt ।
sūtasyaiko bhāgaḥ śatāṃśavidhireṣa vikhyātaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vedhavidhānamāha aṣṭānavatir ityādi ।।
eṣa rasadaradetyādiśatāṃśavedhavidhiḥ kathaṃ atra śatāṃśe aṣṭānavatirbhāgāstārasya rūpyasya punariha kanakabhāgaḥ syāt eka eveti punaḥ sūtasya daradādimilitarasasyaiko bhāgaḥ ekāṃśaḥ iti sarve śatāṃśāḥ śatāṃśena vedha iti ।।

śatāṃśavidhi 
ekonapañcāśadbhāgāstārasyeha tathaiva śulvasya ।
kanakasyaiko bhāgo vedhaścaikena sūtasya ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha ekonapañcāśadityādi ।।
ekonapañcāśadbhāgāḥ tārasya rūpyasya kāryāḥ tathaiva śulvasya tāmrasya ekonapañcāśadbhāgāśca kāryāḥ punaḥ kanakasya hemnaśca eko bhāgaḥ kāryaḥ sūtasya ca ekena bhāgena vedha iti eṣo'pi śatāṃśavidhiḥ ।।

Definition sahasravedhin und hṆher
evaṃ sahasravedhī niyujyate koṭivedhī ca ।
jāraṇabījavaśena tu sūtasya balābalaṃ jñātvā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

pūrvoktavidher viśeṣamāha evamityādi ।।
evaṃ śatāṃśavedhanyāyena daśavṛddhivibhāgena sahasravedhī syāt ।।
evaṃ ca jāraṇabījavaśena jāraṇāyāṃ yadbījaṃ kiyadguṇajāritamiti bhāvaḥ tadvaśena koṭivedhī ca syāt ।।
kiṃ kṛtvā tenaiva jāraṇabījavaśena yattasya balābalaṃ nyūnādhikyaṃ tat jñātvetyabhiprāyaḥ ।।

kuntavedha
dattvādau prativāpaṃ lākṣāmatsyādipittabhāvanayā ।
tāre vā śulbe vā tārāriṣṭe tathā kṛṣṭau ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

viśeṣeṇa vedhavidhānamāha dattvetyādi ।।
ādau prathamaṃ lākṣāmatsyādipittabhāvanayā lākṣā pratītā matsyādipittāni matsyamāhiṣamayūrājasūkarasaṃbhavāni pittāni teṣāṃ bhāvanayā kṛtvā prativāpaṃ galite nikṣepaṃ tattāre dattvā athavā śulbe prativāpaṃ kuryāt athavā kṛṣṭau hemakaraṇe vāpaṃ dattvā niyuñjyāditi śeṣaḥ ।।

tadanu krāmaṇamṛdite tatkalkenāpi piṇḍitarasena ।
atividrute ca tasmin vedho'sau kuntavedhena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

viśeṣāccāha tadanvityādi ।।
tadanu lākṣāmatsyādipittabhāvanāyā anantaraṃ tasmin lākṣādikalke krāmaṇamṛdite kāntarasakadaradaraktatailendragopādyair mṛdite sati punastatkalkena taccūrṇenāpi piṇḍitarasena vedhaḥ kartavya iti śeṣaḥ ।।
kasmin tāre vā śulbe vā vidrute jalarūpe kārya ityarthaḥ ।।

krāmaṇa 
tattailārdrapaṭena sthagayet palalena bhasmanā vāpi ।
vidhivadvedhyaṃ dravyaṃ rasarājakrāmaṇārthaṃ hi ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

viśeṣamāha tadityādi ।।
vedhyaṃ vedhocitaṃ dravyaṃ rasarājakrāmaṇārthaṃ yathā raso viśati tadarthaṃ taṃ tailārdrapaṭena sāraṇatailārdravastreṇa sthagayet ācchādayet vā palalena kenacinmāṃsena vā bhasmanā ācchādayedityarthaḥ ।।

iti sāritasya kathitaṃ rasasya vedhādi krāmaṇaṃ karma ।
viśeṣamāha itītyādi ।।
sāritasya uktavidhānena sāraṇākṛtasya vedhādi krāmaṇaṃ karma vedhavidhānoditakrāmaṇaṃ karma kathitam ।।

lepavedha।pattrarañjana
pādādijīrṇabījo yujyate patralepena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

pādādijīrṇabījaḥ pādādinā pādārdhena samato nyūnena ca jīrṇaṃ bījaṃ yasmin saḥ patralepena yujyate ataḥ patrarañjanaṃ syādityabhiprāyaḥ ।।

pattrarañjana durch lepa
amlādyudvartitatārāriṣṭādipatram atiśuddham ।
ālipya rasena tataḥ krāmaṇalipte puṭeṣu viśrāntam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atiśuddhaṃ nirmalaṃ amlādyudvartitaṃ tārāriṣṭaśabdātsitaṃ svarṇaṃ grāhyaṃ tataḥ rasenālipya tataḥ kramaṇālipte krāmaṇapiṇḍena lepe kṛte sati puṭeṣu utpalāgnau viśrāntaṃ sthāpitaṃ kuryāt ।।
patrarañjanavidhir ayam ।।

Weiterverarbeitung des pattras; varṇapuṭa
ardhena miśrayitvā hemnā jyeṣṭhena taddalaṃ puṭitam ।
kṣitikhagapaṭuraktamṛdā varṇapuṭo'yaṃ tato deyaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha svarṇavidhānamāha ardhenetyādi ।।
ardhena ardhavibhāgena rañjitadalādita iti jñeyam ।।
jyeṣṭhena hemnā pravarakanakena taddalaṃ rañjitapatraṃ miśrayitvā puṭitaṃ kuryāt yathā milati ।।
punaḥ kṣitikhagapaṭuraktamṛdā kṛtvā kṣitiḥ sphaṭikaḥ khagaḥ pītakāsīsaṃ paṭu saindhavaṃ lavaṇaṃ raktamṛt gairikaṃ ekavadbhāvadvandvaḥ tena kṣityādinopari liptaṃ dalaṃ prati ayaṃ puṭo deyaḥ vanopalair iti śeṣaḥ ।।

vedha white gold red gold
bhūpativartakacūrṇaṃ śirīṣapuṣparasabhāvitaṃ bahuśaḥ ।
sadyaḥ karoti raktaṃ sitakanakam aśītibhāgena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

varṇavidhānamāha bhūpatītyādi ।।
bhūpativartakacūrṇaṃ rājāvartarajaḥ bahuśo bahuvāraṃ śirīṣapuṣparasabhāvitaṃ kuryāt ityadhyāhāryam ।।
bhāvitaṃ gharmapuṭitamiti vidhānavit iti śeṣaḥ ।।

vedha silver gold
rasadaradavimalatāpyaṃ paṭuśilāmākṣīkanṛpāścaiva ।
pravālakaṃkuṣṭhaṭaṅkaṇagairikaprativāpitaṃ sitaṃ kanakam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha rasetyādi ।
rasaḥ sūtaḥ daradaṃ hiṅgulaḥ vimalaṃ tāpyabhedaḥ paṭu saiṃdhavaṃ śilā manohvā mākṣikaṃ pratītaṃ vaṇigdravyaṃ nṛpo rājāvartaḥ pravālaṃ vidrumaṃ kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ viraṅgaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ saubhāgyaṃ gairikaṃ pratītaṃ etaiḥ prativāpitaṃ sitadravyaṃ kanakaṃ bhavet ityadhyāhāryam ।।

colouring of gold
tāpībhavanṛpāvartabījapūrarasārditam ।
karoti puṭapākena hema sindūrasannibham ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha tāpībhavetyādi ।।
tāpībhavaṃ mākṣikasattvaṃ nṛpāvartaṃ rājāvartakaṃ etaddvayaṃ bījapūrarasārditaṃ mātuluṅgarasamarditaṃ kuryāt etadubhayoryogāt kanakaṃ puṭapākena vahnividhānena kanakaṃ pūrvoktaṃ yatkanakaṃ vā hīnavarṇakanakaṃ sindūrasannibhaṃ karoti ।।
sindūravannibhā yasyeti samāsaḥ ।।

silver improvement of colour
vaṅgābhraṃ sitamākṣīkaṃ śailaṃ vā vāhayetsite ।
tattāraṃ ca daśāṃśena tārotkarṣaṃ karoti hi ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha tāravarṇavidhānamāha vaṅgetyādi ।।
vaṅgābhramiti vaṅgaṃ trapu abhraṃ śvetābhraṃ punaḥ sitamākṣīkaṃ vimalaṃ śailaṃ śvetaśilājatu vā site tāre vāhayet ।।
punardaśāṃśena etadauṣadhanicayaṃ tārato daśamavibhāgena kṛtvā hi niścitaṃ tārotkarṣaṃ karoti hīnavarṇata uttamaṃ karotītyabhiprāyaḥ ।।

nirvāhaṇa of diff substances phys results
nāgaḥ karoti mṛdutāṃ nirvyūḍhastāṃ ca raktatāṃ ca raviḥ ।
tāṃ pītatāṃ ca tīkṣṇaṃ kācastatkālikavināśaṃ ca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

tāre viśeṣamāha nāga ityādi ।।
nāgaḥ sīsakas tāre nirvyūḍho mṛdutāṃ komalatvaṃ karoti ।।
punaḥ ravistāmraṃ nirvyūḍhaṃ sat tāṃ mṛdutāṃ ca punaḥ raktatāṃ lohitanibhāṃ karoti ।।
ca punastīkṣṇaṃ tāranirvyūḍhaṃ tāṃ raktatāṃ pītatāṃ ca karoti ।।
punaḥ kācaḥ pratīto loke sa kālikavināśaṃ karotīti tāre nirvyūḍha iti saṃbandhaḥ ।।

gold improvement
kanakāruṇasamamākṣikakarañjatailāpluto dhmātaḥ ।
pāte pāte daśa daśa vindati yāvaddhi koṭimapi ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

hemno viśeṣamāha kanakāruṇetyādi ।।
kanakaṃ hema aruṇaṃ tāmraṃ samaṃ tulyabhāgaṃ mākṣikaṃ tāpyaṃ ayaṃ gaṇaḥ karañjatailapluto dhmātaḥ kāryaḥ ।।
punaḥ pāte pāte vāraṃvāraṃ nikṣepe sati daśa daśa guṇotkarṣaṃ vidanti dhmāta ityadhyāhāraḥ ।।
hi niścitam ।।
kiyatkālaṃ yāvatkoṭisaṃkhyāṃ vindati ।।

gold bīja for improvement of colour
sa cāyamativilīnaḥ kaṃguṇītailasecito bahuśaḥ ।
mākṣīkaravinivāpaṃ vidhyati kanakaṃ śatāṃśena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

viśeṣamāha sa ityādi ।।
saḥ karañjatailapluto yogo bahuśo vāraṃvāraṃ kaṅguṇītailena secito yathā syāttathāyaṃ ati vilīnaḥ san mākṣikaravinivāpāṃ punaḥ kārya evaṃvidhaṃ ca kanakaṃ śatāṃśena śatavibhāgena vidhyati sitakanakam iti ।।

gold bīja for improvement 
śulbahataṃ rasagandhāhatakhagapītaṃ daśāṃśena ।
vidhyati kanakaṃ kurute tannirvyūḍhaṃ marditaṃ sudṛḍham ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

viśeṣamāha śulbetyādi ।।
śulbahataṃ śulbena saha hataṃ rasagandhaṃ sūtagandhaṃ tena āhataṃ pañcatvam āpannaṃ yatkhagapītaṃ pītakāsīsaṃ etadauṣadhasamuccayaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ yathā syāttathā marditaṃ kuryāt punastat nirvyūḍhaṃ daśāṃśena vidhyati sitakanakaṃ kurute svarṇamiti viśeṣaḥ ।।

vedha
rasakasamaṃ sudhmātaṃ kanakaṃ bhuktvā tato'rkacandralepena ।
mākṣikasattvaṃ hemnā karoti jīrṇo rasaḥ śatāṃśena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha rasaketyādi ।।
tato'nantaraṃ arkacandralepena kanakaṃ rasakasamaṃ dhmātaṃ kuryāt punaretadauṣadhaṃ bhuktvā kanakaṃ syāt punarmākṣikasattvaṃ hemnā saha jīrṇaṃ rasaṃ śatāṃśena vidhyatītyarthaḥ ।।

vedha; silver gold
aṣṭaguṇaṃ mṛtaśulbaṃ kaladhautena mūkamūṣayā liptam ।
tatṣoḍaśāṃśajīrṇaṃ vidhyati tāraṃ śatārdhena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha aṣṭaguṇetyādi ।।
aṣṭaguṇaṃ mṛtaśulbaṃ arivargeṇa saha hataṃ yat śulbaṃ tāmraṃ tataḥ kaladhautena ṣoḍaśāṃśena jīrṇaṃ śatārdhena pañcāśadvibhāgena tāraṃ vidhyati kanakaṃ karotītyarthaḥ ।।

vedha daśāṃśa~; silver gold
āvṛtya kanakakariṇau śilayā prativāpitau tato bhuktvā ।
dolāyantre gandhakajīrṇastāre daśāṃśavedhī syāt ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha āvṛtyetyādi ।।
kanakakariṇau samahemanāgau āvṛtya gālayitvā śilayā manohvayā prativāpitau tato'nantaraṃ dolāyantre kanakakariṇau bhuktvā gandhakajīrṇo yo rasaḥ sa tāre daśāṃśavedhī syāt daśāṃśena vidhyatītyarthaḥ ।।

vedha śatāṃśa; bronze gold
ripunihatalohaṣaṭkaṃ jīrṇo dhānyasthitaścaturmāsam ।
sahitaḥ purasurābhyāṃ vidhyati ghoṣaṃ śatāṃśena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha ripunihatetyādi ।।
ripunihatalohaṣaṭkaṃ ripubhir arivargair nihataṃ māritaṃ yat lohaṣaṭkaṃ svarṇatāratāmranāgavaṅgalohābhidhānaṃ tat caturmāsaṃ yathā syāttathā dhānyasthito'nnakoṣṭhīdhṛto raso jīrṇaḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭo dhānyasthitaḥ purasurābhyāṃ guggulumadirābhyāṃ sahito militaḥ śatāṃśena ghoṣaṃ kāṃsyaṃ vidhyati kanakaṃ karotītyarthaḥ ।।

vakṣye samprati samyagyad bījaṃ samarase jīrṇam ।
piṣṭistambhādividhiṃ prakāśyamānaṃ budhāḥ śṛṇuta ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

viśeṣamāha vakṣya ityādi ।।
bho budhāḥ mayā prakāśyamānaṃ sat śṛṇuta sāvadhānā ityadhyāhāryam ।।
tatkiṃ saṃprati yad bījaṃ samarase tulyasūte samyak jīrṇaṃ jāraṇamāpannaṃ tadahaṃ govindanāmā vakṣye kathayāmi ।।
punaḥ piṣṭistambhādividhiṃ piṣṭistambha ādir yasya vidhestaṃ vidhiṃ pāṭakhoṭajalaukākhyaṃ ca vakṣye ।।

vedha; ghoṣākṛṣṭa gold
rājāvartakavimalapītābhragandhatāpyarasakaiśca ।
kāṃkṣīkāsīsaśilādaradaiśca samanvitaṃ nāgam ।।
ahimārarasaiḥ puṭitaṃ māraya nāgaṃ nirutthakaṃ yāvat ।
tadanu ca tasya hi madhye śulbaṃ gandhaṃ ca lavaṇakaṃkuṣṭham ।।
tatsarvaṃ śatavārān bhāvaya pakvārkapatrasalilaiśca ।
ghoṣākṛṣṭe śulbe cūrṇaṃ nirvāhayecchataśaḥ ।।
śulbena tena hi samaṃ rasakapītābhrasatvavimalaṃ ca ।
gairikamākṣikasattvaṃ ṭaṅkaṇanāgaṃ ca tīkṣṇayutam ।।
etair dvandvaṃ kṛtvā mākṣikavāpena rañjayecchulvam ।
vārāṃśca viṃśatirapi galitaṃ secayettadanu ।।
nirguṇḍīkākamācīkanyārasamelanaṃ kṛtvā ।
vārān sapta ca vidhinā tadapi ca nirvāpayeddhemni ।।
yāvaccaturviṃśatiguṇaṃ bījavaraṃ rañjayettacca ।
pakvaṃ mākṣikameva hi tena ca vidhinā tadapi caturviṃśatiguṇam ।।
tadbījaṃ laghumātraṃ rasarāje saṃskṛte pūrvam ।
mūṣāyāṃ khalu dattvā daśaguṇaṃ ca gandhakaṃ dāhyam ।।
athavā vālukayantre sudṛḍhe caturdaśāṃgulamūṣāyām ।
madhye sūtaṃ muktvā laghutarapuṭayogataḥ pihitā ।।
tena samaṃ bījavare piṣṭiḥ pādāṃśataḥ kāryā ।
aṃgulinavaparimāṇe mūṣāmadhye ca piṣṭikāṃ dattvā ।।
nirguṇḍīkākamācīgojihvādugdhikāraktā ।
gṛhakanyāmadhusaindhavapiṇḍairapi samantataśchādyā ।।
tāvatkāryaḥ puṭayogo yāvad dṛḍhatāṃ samāyāti ।
ṣaḍguṇagandhakatālakakāṃkṣīkāsīsalavaṇakṣāram ।।
tāpyaṃ tatsarvasamaṃ deyaṃ bāhye tadauṣadhipiṇḍam ।
ṣaḍguṇaṣaḍguṇasahitaṃ piṣṭīṃ yantre'tha kacchape dattvā ।।
svedyaṃ puṭayogena tu tridinaṃ ghaṭikātrayaṃ yāvat ।
uddhṛtya tato yatnāt piṣṭvā sucūrṇitāṃ kṛtvā ।।
samabījena tu sāryo nāgaṃ triguṇaṃ tataḥ samuttārya ।
pratisāraṇā ca kāryā jāritasūtena bījayuktena ।।
anusāraṇā ca paścāttriguṇaṃ bījaṃ bhavedyatra ।
prāguktaṃ tasyopari mṛtanāgaṃ śataguṇaṃ vāhyam ।
tena ca ghoṣākṛṣṭe śulbe vedho'tha saptaśataiḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha nāgamāha rājāvartaketyādi ।।
rājāvartakaṃ prasiddhaṃ vimalaṃ śvetamākṣikaṃ pītābhraṃ pītavarṇaṃ yadabhraṃ gandho gandhakaḥ tāpyaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ rasakaṃ kharparikaṃ etaiḥ punaretaiḥ kāṅkṣī kāhīti loke kāsīsaṃ pītakāsīsaṃ śilā manohvā daradaṃ hiṅgulaṃ taiśca samanvitaṃ militaṃ nāgaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ ।।
taccāha ahītyādi ।।
pūrvauṣadhasaṃyutaṃ nāgaṃ ahimārarasaiḥ karavīradrāvaiḥ puṭitaṃ kuryāt ।।
nāgaṃ sīsakaṃ tāvanmāraya yāvannirutthakaṃ yathā punarutthitaṃ na syāt ।।
tadanu tatpaścāt tasya nāgasya madhye śulbaṃ tāmraṃ gandhaṃ pratītaṃ lavaṇaṃ saindhavaṃ kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ viraṅgaṃ etatsarvaṃ miśritaṃ kuryāt ityadhyāhāryam ।।

kṣepavedha
krāmaṇam etatprāgapi mākṣikadaradagandhakaśilābhiḥ ।
rājāvartakavimalapravālakaṅkuṣṭhatutthaviṣaiḥ ।।
kāntagairikaṭaṃkaṇabhūmilatārudhiraśakragoparasaiḥ ।
mahiṣīṇāṃ karṇamalair mṛtalohaṃ vāyasasya viṣṭhā ca ।।
pārāvatasya viṣṭhā strīpayaḥ sarvam ekataḥ kṛtvā ।
krāmaṇakalkaṃ caitacchatavārān raktapītagaṇaiḥ ।।
bhāvyaṃ kaṃguṇitaile krauñcīpittabhāvanāḥ sapta ।
kalkenānena pacet sāritapiṣṭiṃ ca haṇḍikāyāṃ hi ।।
yāvadraktā bhavati hi gacchati nāgaṃ samuttārya ।
tāvatkṣepaṃ ca kṣipetsarvasminsāraṇādau ca ।।
evaṃ hi koṭivedhī rasarājaḥ krāmito bhūtvā ।
puṃstvāderucchrāyaprado bhūtvā bhogāndatte ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

krāmaṇamāha krāmaṇam ityādi ।।
prāgapīti pūrvādhyāye'pi proktaṃ iti śeṣaḥ ।।
punaretadvakṣyamāṇaṃ krāmaṇaguṇaṃ kuryād ityadhyāhāraḥ ।।
sa kathaṃ tadāha mākṣiketyādi ।।
mākṣikaṃ tāpyaṃ daradaṃ hiṅgulaṃ gandhakaḥ pratītaḥ śilā manohvā tābhiḥ ।।
punaḥ rājāvartaketyādi ।।
rājāvartakaṃ lājavarada iti bhāṣāyāṃ vimalaṃ sitamākṣikaṃ pravālaṃ vidrumaṃ kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ viraṅgaṃ tutthakaṃ śikhigrīvaṃ viṣaṃ saktukādikandajaṃ etaiśca ।।
kāntetyādi kāntaṃ cumbakaṃ gairikaṃ pratītaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ saubhāgyaṃ bhūmilatā bhūnāgaḥ rudhiraṃ śakragopaḥ raso viṣaṃ punaruktādviṣamatra dviguṇaṃ taiḥ ।।
ca punar mahiṣīṇāṃ karṇamalair hayāripatnīnāṃ śravaṇayor malāni taiḥ saha mṛtalohaṃ mṛtaṃ ca tallohaṃ ceti vāyasasya kākasya viṣṭhā śakṛt ।।
pārāvatasya viṣṭhā kapotaśakṛt strīpayo nārīkṣīraṃ etatsarvaṃ mākṣikādistrīkṣīrāntam ekataḥ kṛtvā miśritaṃ vidhāya ca punaretatkrāmaṇakalkaṃ raktapītagaṇaiḥ kiṃśukādiharidrādyaiḥ śatavārān bhāvayedityāgāmiślokasaṃbandhāt ।।
sāraṇakalkavidhānamāha bhāvyam ityādi ।।
pūrvoktasāraṇakalkaṃ kaṅguṇītaile jyotiṣmatīsnehe bhāvyaṃ tataḥ krauñcīpittabhāvanāḥ sapta deyāḥ dātavyāḥ ।।
punaḥ sāritapiṣṭiṃ sāritā yā rasendrabījapiṣṭis tām anena kalkena haṇḍikāyāṃ pacet vahninā pākaḥ kartavyaḥ ।।
sāraṇakalkapācanamāha yāvadityādi ।।
pūrvakalkasaṃyutāṃ piṣṭiṃ kiyatkālaṃ pacet yāvadraktā bhavati nāgaṃ ca gacchati nāganāśaḥ syāt nāge gacchati sati samuttārya punastāvatsarvasminsāraṇādau ca kṣepakrameṇa kṣepaṃ kṣipet ।।
puṃstvādyān ākāśagamanaparyantān bhogān dadātītyabhiprāyaḥ ।।

silver gold
abhrakamākṣikakanakaṃ nāgayutaṃ militaṃ vidhinā ।
sūte piṣṭiḥ kāryā divyauṣadhiyogataḥ puṭitā ।।
ṣaḍguṇagandhakadāhaḥ śilayā nāgaṃ samuttārya ।
tāre hemākṛṣṭirmilitā syāt ṣoḍaśāṃśena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

piṣṭividhyantaramāha abhrakam ityādi ।।
abhrakaṃ pratītaṃ mākṣikaṃ tāpyaṃ kanakaṃ hema nāgayutaṃ nāgena sīsakena yutaṃ sahitaṃ vidhinā kartavyopadeśena etatsarvaṃ sūte militaṃ sat piṣṭiḥ kāryā divyauṣadhiyogataḥ puṭitā piṣṭiḥ kāryā iti ।।
tāre hemākṛṣṭim āha ṣaḍityādi ।।
pūrvoktāyāṃ piṣṭyāṃ ṣaḍguṇagandhakadāhaḥ kāryaḥ punaḥ ṣaḍguṇaśilayā kṛtvā nāgaṃ samuttārya sīsakamapahāya sā niṣpannā piṣṭī ṣoḍaśāṃśena tāre rūpye militā satī hemākṛṣṭiḥ syātkanakoddhāraṇaṃ bhavet tāmranāgādiṣu dhātuṣu hema sthitameva tata ākṛṣṭiśabdo yuktaḥ ।।

silver gold
mākṣikanihataṃ śulbaṃ śilayā nihataṃ ca nāgatulyāṃśam ।
puṭitaṃ jambīrarasaiḥ saindhavasahitaṃ pacetsthālyām ।।
taccūrṇaṃ ghṛtamadhukaṭaṅkaṇasahitaṃ ca guptamūṣāyām ।
tāre triguṇaṃ vyūḍhaṃ hemākṛṣṭirbhaveddivyā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

nāgamāraṇavidhānamāha mākṣiketyādi ।।
mākṣikeṇa nihataṃ māritaṃ yat śulvaṃ śilayā manaḥśilayā nāgaṃ ca nihataṃ māritaṃ ubhayaṃ tulyāṃśaṃ samabhāgaṃ kāryaṃ punar jambīrarasaiḥ jambīradrāvaiḥ saindhavasahitam ubhayaṃ puṭitaṃ bhāvitaṃ satpacedvahninā pakvaṃ kuryāt ।।
kva sthālyāṃ mṛdbhājane ityarthaḥ ।।

copper silver gold
śulbaṃ balinā nihataṃ tīkṣṇaṃ daradena nihatasamabhāgam ।
ekīkṛtvā puṭayetpacen mātārasenaiva ।।
tāre vyūḍhaṃ triguṇaṃ mārjārākṣanibhaṃ bhavettacca ।
liptaṃ rasena puṭitaṃ hemārdhena mātrayā tulyam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

nāge tāre hemākṛṣṭimāha śulvamityādi ।।
balinā gandhakena nihataṃ sat samabhāgaṃ tulyāṃśaṃ kuryāt iti śeṣaḥ ।।
ubhayamekīkṛtya saṃmiśrya mātārasenaiva nārīkṣīreṇa puṭayet paced iti ślokārthaḥ ।।
hemākṛṣṭervidhānamāha tāre ityādi ।।
pūrvoktaṃ cūrṇaṃ śulbajaṃ tīkṣṇajaṃ vā tāre triguṇaṃ vyūḍhaṃ vāhitaṃ sat mārjārākṣasaṃnibha otunetrābhaṃ tāraṃ bhavet ।।
hemārdhena mātrayā tārārdhabhāgena parimāṇena hemnā tulyam anyūnādhikaṃ rasena payasā ।।

lead gold
liptaṃ tadanu puṭitaṃ nāgaṃ hi rasena pādayuktena ।
kharparakasthaṃ kṛtvā kāryaṃ vidhinā dṛḍhaṃ tāpyam ।।
nirguṇḍīrasabhāvitapuṭitaṃ śilayā vartitaṃ ślakṣṇam ।
tāvanmṛditapuṭitaṃ nirutthabhāvaṃ vrajedyāvat ।।
tāre tannirvyūḍhaṃ yāvatpītaṃ bhavedruciram ।
hemasamena ca militaṃ mātrātulyaṃ bhavetkanakam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

punarnāgavidhānamāha liptamityādi ।।
triguṇaṃ yathā syāt tathā pādayuktena rasena caturthāṃśasahitasūtena saha nāgaṃ sīsakaṃ kharparakasthaṃ mṛdbhājanakhaṇḍasthitaṃ kṛtvā vidhinā rasajñopadeśena dṛḍhaṃ tāpyaṃ vahniyutaṃ sat nihataṃ kuryāditi vākyārthaḥ ।।
taccāha nirguṇḍītyādi ।।
pakvaṃ nāgacūrṇaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ śreṣṭhavidhānaṃ yathā syāttathā śilayā vartitaṃ san nirguṇḍīrasabhāvitapuṭitaṃ pūrṇaṃ bhāvitaṃ gharmapuṭitaṃ paścātpuṭitaṃ vahnipuṭitaṃ kuryāt ।।
punaryāvannirutthabhāvaṃ aśīratvaṃ vrajet tāvanmṛditapuṭitaṃ marditapācitaṃ kuryād ityarthaḥ ।।
taccāha tāre ityādi ।।
tannirutthanāgacūrṇaṃ yāvatpītaṃ pītavarṇaṃ tāraṃ bhavet tāvadvāraṃ nirvyūḍhaṃ kuryāt ।।
punarhemasamena kanakatulyāṃśena mātrātulyaṃ militaṃ sat ruciraṃ manoramaṃ kanakaṃ sarvaṃ bhavedityarthaḥ ।।

svarṇamākṣika gold
tāpyaṃ cāṃgulisaṃjñaṃ cūrṇaṃ kṛtvā tadantare dattvā ।
śulbasya guptamūṣā kāryā puṭitāpyatha ca dhmātā ।।
hemnā militaṃ vidhinā mātrātulyaṃ bhavatyeva ।
tāpyavidhānamāha tāpyamityādi ।।
aṅgulisaṃjñaṃ tāpyaṃ svarṇamākṣikaṃ cūrṇaṃ kṛtvā tadantare taccūrṇam antare madhye dattvā śulbasya tāmrasya guptamūṣā andhamūṣā kāryā tatra nale ityabhiprāyaḥ ।।
sā mūṣā puṭitā dhmātā kāryeti vidhānam uktam ।।
taccāha hemnetyādi ।।
pakvaṃ yanmākṣikacūrṇaṃ taddhemnā kṛtvā ।।

gold rañjana 
pādādijīrṇasūte lihyāt patrāṇi hemakṛṣṭīnām ।।
krāmaṇayogena tato vilipya vidhinā nidhāya tulyādhaḥ ।
paścāddhemnā sahitaṃ dhmātaṃ mūṣodare samāvartya ।।
yantraṃ haṇḍyāṃ pakvaṃ pañcamṛdāvāpya puṭapakvam ।
pādādijīrṇasūte pādādinā pādārdhasamānadinā jīrṇo yo'sau sūtaḥ tasmin hemakṛṣṭīnāṃ patrāṇi kaluṣakanakānāṃ patrāṇi lihyāt krāmaṇayogena lepayedityāgāmiślokāt ।।
taccāha krāmaṇetyādi ।।
tato rasalepānantaraṃ krāmaṇayogena kunaṭīmākṣikaviṣam ityādinoktena vilipya tulyādhaḥ tulyaṃ yathā syāttathā adhobhāge nidhāya mūṣodare dhmātaṃ kuryāt ।।
punaḥ paścāddhemnā kanakena sahitaṃ āvartya dhmātaṃ kuryāt ।।

gold production 
vakṣyāmi cālepavidhiṃ kramati ca sūto yathā hi patreṣu ।
rañjati yena vidhinā samāsataḥ sūtarājastu ।।
kṛtvālaktakavastraṃ liptamanusnehamupari cūrṇena ।
avacūrṇitaṃ tu kṛtvā gandhakaśilayā vidhānena ।।
tadupari śṛtaṃ ca dattvā gandhakaśilācūrṇaṃ ca sūtavare ।
paścādvartiḥ kāryā pātre dhṛtvāyase ca same ।।
dīpaṃ pratibodhya tatastailaṃ dattvā tataḥ stokam ।
pākaṃ yāmasyārdhaṃ svāṅge śītaṃ tataḥ kāryam ।।
gṛhṇīyādatha sūtakṛṣṭīṃ liptā tatastena ।
krāmaṇayogairliptvā puṭitā sā hemni nirdhmātā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha yantramityādi ।।
vā yantraṃ pañcamṛdā valmīkamṛt gairikaṃ khaṭikā saindhavaṃ iṣṭikā ceti pañcamṛdaḥ tayā kṛtvā haṇḍyāṃ sthālyāṃ pakvaṃ kāryam ।।
atha puṭapakvaṃ gajapuṭādinā pācyamityarthaḥ ।।
lepanavidhiṃ vakṣyāmi yathā patreṣu lepaḥ kāryaḥ punar yathā patreṣu kramati svaguṇān prakāśayati punaryena vidhinā rañjanaṃ rāgaṃ dadāti samāsataḥ saṃkṣepataḥ vidhinā vidhānataḥ sūtarāja evaṃvidho bhavet tamupāyaṃ vakṣyāmīti ।।
atha lepakrāmaṇaṃ rañjanavidhānamāha kṛtvālaktakavastram ityādi ।।
prathamaṃ ālaktakaṃ vastraṃ alaktena rañjitaṃ yadvastraṃ tad ālaktakaṃ anu paścāt snehaṃ kaṅguṇyādīnāṃ tailaṃ liptaṃ kāryaṃ tattailaliptavastropari vakṣyamāṇauṣadhānāṃ cūrṇena avacūrṇanaṃ kuryāt tailaliptavastraṃ gandhakaśilayā avacūrṇitaṃ kṛtvā tadupari dātavyaṃ darśayati ।।
punastadupari gandhakaśilācūrṇopari śṛtaṃ dattvā punargandhakaśilācūrṇaṃ sūtavare sūtarājopari dattvā paścāttatkaraṇānantaraṃ vartiḥ kāryā sā vartir āyase lohamaye same samabhūmau pātre dhṛtvā tatropari kāryā ।।
vidhyantaraṃ darśayati dīpam ityādi ।।
tato varteḥ pātropari karaṇānantaraṃ dīpaṃ pratibodhya prajvālya tato vāraṃvāraṃ stokamalpaṃ tailaṃ dattvā yāvadyāmasya praharasya ardhaṃ syāttāvatpākaṃ kuryāt iti śeṣaḥ ।।
tato'nantaraṃ tatpatitaṃ tailaṃ svāṅgaśītaṃ kāryaṃ aṅge tailadravarūpe śarīre yathāsvaṃ svayameva śītaṃ yathā syāttathā kāryam ।।
taccāha gṛhṇīyād ityādi ।।
atha śītakaraṇānantaram ।।
sūtakṛṣṭīṃ ca gṛhṇīyāt karmavit iti śeṣaḥ ।।
tato'nantaraṃ sā sūtakṛṣṭī tena patreṇa liptā satī krāmaṇayogair liptvā hemni suvarṇe nirdhmātā kāryeti ।।

gold production
athavā daradaśilālair gandhakamākṣīkapakvamṛtanāgaiḥ ।
kaṃkuṣṭhapravālasahitaiḥ piṣṭaiśca kaṅguṇītaile ।।
madhye sūto yukto mṛditaḥ khalve tathāyase vidhinā ।
saṃsvedya vaṃśanalikāṃ dolāyantreṇa sveditaṃ tridinam ।।
etairliptvā kṛṣṇaiḥ patraṃ pūrvoktavidhānena ।
nāgaṃ dattvā prakaṭaṃ stokaṃ stokaṃ krameṇaiva ।।
bhavati hi kanakaṃ divyamakṣīṇaṃ devayogyaṃ ca ।
evaṃ jāritasūte sakalāḥ khalu haṇḍikāḥ sarvāḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha athavetyādi ।।
darado hiṅgulaḥ śilā manohvā ālaṃ haritālaṃ taiḥ gandhakaḥ pratītaḥ mākṣikaṃ yatpakvaṃ sindūrīkṛtaṃ mṛtanāgaśca taiḥ ।।
punaḥ kaṅkuṣṭhapravālasahitaiḥ kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ viraṅgaṃ pravālaṃ vidrumaṃ tābhyāṃ sahitaiḥ ।।
punaretaiḥ kaṅguṇītaile jyotiṣmatītaile piṣṭaiś cūrṇīkṛtaiḥ madhye sūto yuktaḥ kārya ityagrimaślokasaṃbandhāt ।।
taccāha madhye ityādi ।।
pūrvoktairauṣadhaiḥ kṛtvā madhye auṣadhāntaḥ sūto yuktaḥ kāryaḥ ।।
punarmardayitvā vaṃśanalikāṃ riktodarāṃ prati saṃvedya dinatrayaṃ dolāyantreṇa sveditaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ ।।
taccāha liptvetyādi ।।
etāni sveditauṣadhāni saṃyuktāni taiḥ kṛṣṇaiḥ kṛṣṇalavaṇaiḥ pūrvoktavidhānena sūtakṛṣṭīvidhānena patraṃ liptvā punaḥ prakaṭaṃ yathā syāt tathā stokaṃ alpamalpaṃ krameṇa nāgaṃ dattvā kanakaṃ jāyate ityagrimaślokasaṃbandhaḥ ।।
evaṃ kṛte sati akṣīṇaṃ akṣayaṃ divyaṃ pravaraṃ devayogyaṃ devā indrādayastadyogyaṃ kanakaṃ bhavati ।।
yukto'yamarthaḥ ।।
evaṃ jāritasūte jāritakarmakṛte rase khalu niścitaṃ sarvā haṇḍikāḥ sarve dhātvādyāḥ sakalāḥ saprasavāḥ syurityarthaḥ ।।

relation between bīja and gold 
nirbījaṃ samajīrṇe pādaikenaiva ṣoḍaśāṃśena ।
ardhena pādayogaṃ pādenaikena tulyakanakaṃ ca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

viśeṣamāha nirbījamityādi ।।
nirbījaṃ yathā syāttathā samajīrṇaṃ pādena turyāṃśena phalaṃ dadāti tathā ardhena jīrṇena ṣoḍaśāṃśena phalaṃ dadāti ca punastadardhena jīrṇena tatpādayogaṃ tatpādena ekena tatpādayogaṃ phalaṃ dadātīti sarvatra vācyam ।।
tulyakanakaṃ ca jīrṇaṃ pūrṇaṃ phalaṃ dadātīti ।।

tārākṛṣṭi
tārākṛṣṭiṃ vakṣye mṛtavaṅgaṃ tālakena tulyāṃśam ।
lambitamatha nirdhmātaṃ tāmraṃ tārachaviṃ vahati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

hemākṛṣṭyanantaraṃ tārākṛṣṭiṃ vakṣye ahaṃ kaviḥ kathayāmi mṛtavaṅgaṃ māritaṃ vaṅgaṃ tālakena haritāleneti ।।
atha tāmraṃ tulyāṃśaṃ lambitaṃ vistīrṇaṃ yathā syāt tathā nirdhmātaṃ sat tārachaviṃ vahati rūpyadyutiṃ prāpnotītyarthaḥ ।।

paścānnāgaṃ deyaṃ prakāśamūṣāsu nirmalaṃ yāvat ।
tāvad dhmātaṃ vidhinā sunirmalaṃ nistaraṅgaṃ tu ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha paścādityādi ।।
paścādvaṅgatāmrayogānantaraṃ prakāśamūṣāsu yāvat nirmalaṃ malavarjitaṃ syāttāvannāgaṃ deyaṃ punaryāvannirmalam ujjvalaṃ nistaraṅgaṃ nāgormivarjitaṃ syāt tāvadvidhinā dhmātaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ ।।

??
tālaśilāsarjikābhiḥ saindhavalavaṇena nayanahitasahitaiḥ ।
ekaikaṃ sahitaṃ vā vedhaṃ dattvā punaḥ śulbe ।।
chagaṇaṃ māhiṣatakraṃ snuhīkṣīreṇa sarpiṣā kramaśaḥ ।
saguḍadugdhamadhuvimiśraiḥ kramaśo vedhe niṣekaśca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

viśeṣamāha tāletyādi ।।
tālaṃ haritālaṃ śilā manohvā sarjikā pratītā tābhiḥ saindhavaṃ ca tat lavaṇaṃ ca tena nayanahitasahitaiḥ etaiḥ kṛtvā ekaikaṃ pṛthaktvena vā sahitam ekatvena punaḥ śulve tāmre vedhaṃ pratidadhyāditi ।।
tāravedhaniṣekānyāha chagaṇam ityādi ।।
chagaṇaṃ vanotpannaṃ māhiṣaṃ takraṃ mahiṣyāḥ idaṃ māhiṣaṃ snuhikṣīreṇa sehuṇḍadugdhena saha punaḥ sarpiṣā ghṛtena saha guḍadugdhamadhubhir miśraiḥ militaṃ kṛtvā kramaśo vedhakarmaṇi niṣekaḥ kāryaḥ ।।

tārakṛṣṭī; copper silver
kāñcī brāhmī kuṭilaṃ tālakaṃ samabhāgayojitaṃ dhmātam ।
śulbaṃ viddhamanena tu tārākṛṣṭirbhaveddivyā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

tārākṛṣṭimāha kāñcītyādi ।।
kāñcī svarṇamākṣikaṃ brāhmī somāhvā kuṭilaṃ sīsaṃ tālakaṃ pratītaṃ etatsamayojitaṃ samāṃśamelitaṃ sat dhmātaṃ kuryāt punaranena kāñcyādigaṇena viddhaṃ śulbaṃ divyā manoramā tārākṛṣṭirbhavet ।।

silver optimization
evaṃ tārākṛṣṭirliptvā viddhā rasena sāritena ।
tāraṃ karoti vimalaṃ lepaṃ vā pādajīrṇādi ।।
iti miśrīkṛtaviddhaṃ kramitaṃ tvatha mātṛkātulyam ।
tāradalaṃ bhavati chedanatāḍananikaṣaiśca nirdoṣam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

tārākṛṣṭimāha evamityādi ।।
evaṃ uktavidhānena sāritena sāraṇākarmakṛtena liptvā viddhā satī tārākṛṣṭirbhavet ।।
punariyaṃ tārākṛṣṭiḥ tāraṃ vimalaṃ malavarjitaṃ karoti vā pādajīrṇādi pādena jīrṇaṃ yasmin ādiśabdād ardhasamagrahaṇaṃ kāryaṃ tat lepamiti ।।
viśeṣamāha itītyādi ।।
iti pūrvoktavidhānena miśrīkṛtaṃ militaṃ viddhaṃ kramitaṃ mātṛkātulyaṃ samāṃśaṃ sat tāradalaṃ rūpyapatraṃ bhavati tadrūpyadalaṃ chedanatāḍananikaṣaiḥ chedanaṃ khaṇḍanaṃ tāḍanaṃ ghanaghātaḥ nikaṣaṃ śilopari parīkṣaṇaṃ tairiti tāpaiśca nirdoṣaṃ tadbhavati ।।

evaṃ vedhavidhānaṃ śāstravidhijñena karmakuśalena ।
jñātvā gurūpadeśaṃ kartavyaṃ karmanipuṇena ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

evaṃ amunā prakāreṇa śāstravidhijñena śāstrasya vidhiṃ jānātīti saḥ tena karmanipuṇena saṃskārapravīṇena kuśalena kartrā gurūpadeśaṃ gururuktalakṣaṇo granthādau tasya upadeśaṃ jñātvā vedhavidhānaṃ kartavyam ityarthaḥ ।।

iti rasarājasya vidhau vedhavidhānaṃ prasaṃgataḥ proktam ।
adhunā proktānapi vakṣyāmi rasāyane yogān ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha bhakṣaṇavidhānamāha itītyādi ।।
rasarājasya vidhau rasendrakarmavidhāne vedhavidhānaṃ prasaṅgataḥ prastāvataḥ proktaṃ na tu svaprajñāsamam ।।
adhunā proktānapi api śabdādanubhūtānapi rasāyane jarāvyādhināśanavidhau yogān dravyasamudāyātkān vakṣyāmi kathayāmītyarthaḥ ।।

kṣetrīkaraṇa 
ādau prātaḥ prātaḥ saindhavayuktaṃ ghṛtaṃ pibettridinam ।
tadanu kvāthaṃ tridinaṃ yuñjīyāt ketakītanujam ।।
vidhinā svedyo dehaḥ kartavyo vārtikendreṇa ।
kvathitaṃ kaṭurohiṇyāḥ saṃśodhanam anuprayuñjīta ।।
tadanu ca śuddhādūrdhvaṃ śleṣmānte recite sakalam ।
yāvakapathyaṃ tridinaṃ ghṛtasahitaṃ tatprayuñjīta ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

kāyaśodhanamāha ādāvityādi ।।
prathamaṃ prātaḥ prātaḥ pratyūṣe tridinaṃ saindhavamilitaṃ ghṛtam ājyaṃ pibet ।।
anyasaṃyogamāha tadanu ghṛtasaindhavānantaraṃ ketakītanujaṃ kvāthaṃ ketakyāḥ tanuḥ śarīraṃ tasmājjātaṃ ketakīmūlasaṃbhavam ityarthaḥ aṅge'pyanukte vihitaṃ tu mūlaṃ iti nyāyāt tridinaṃ prayuñjīyādityarthaḥ ।।
vidhyantaram āha vidhinetyādi ।।
tato vidhinā svedavidhānena dehaḥ śarīraṃ vārtikendreṇa rasasaṃpradāyavidā svedyaḥ svinnaḥ kartavyaḥ ।।
anyatkiṃ kaṭurohiṇyāḥ tiktāyāḥ kvathitaṃ prasādhitaṃ samyak śuddhikaraṇaṃ anuprayuñjīta svedānantaram ityabhiprāyaḥ ।।
vidhyantaramāha tad ityādi ।।
tadanu kaṭukarohiṇīsevanānantaraṃ śuddhād ūrdhvaṃ yathā syāt tathā śleṣmāntarecite sati yathā śleṣmaṇo'ntaḥ syāttathā recite sati tridinaparimāṇaṃ yāvakapathyaṃ ghṛtasahitaṃ prayuñjīteti ।।

punarapi ca pānayogaṃ vakṣyāmi ca sakalabhuvanahitakṛtaye ।
pītvā prathame yāme coṣṇodakasamamidaṃ cūrṇam ।।
pathyāsaindhavadhātrīmaricavacāguḍaviḍaṅgarajanīnām ।
śuṇṭhīpippalyor api cūrṇaṃ tridinaṃ prayuñjīta ।।
amunā śuddhaśarīraḥ parihatasaṃsargadoṣabalī ।
pītvā payasā sahitaṃ yāvakamamunā bhavecchuddhaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha punarapītyādi ।।
punarapīti yāvakapathyayogānantaraṃ ca punaḥ pānayogaṃ vakṣyāmi kimarthaṃ sakalabhuvanahitakṛtaye samastasaṃsārahitakaraṇāya idaṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ cūrṇaṃ pathyādyaṃ uṣṇodakasamaṃ taptajalena saha prathamayāme prathamapraharāntaḥ pītvā śuddhaśarīro bhaved ityāgāmiślokasaṃbandhāt ।।
śodhanāya cūrṇamāha pathyetyādi ।।
pathyā harītakī saindhavaṃ pratītaṃ dhātrī āmalakaṃ marīcam ūṣaṇaṃ vacā ugragandhā guḍaḥ pratītaḥ viḍaṅgaṃ kṛmighnaṃ rajanī haridrā śuṇṭhīpippalyor apīti śuṇṭhī nāgaraṃ pippalī māgadhī āsāṃ auṣadhīnāṃ cūrṇaṃ tridinaṃ prayuñjīta ।।
uṣṇajalasamamiti jñeyam ।।
amunetyādi ।
amunā vakṣyamāṇavirecanena yāvakādinā śuddhaśarīraḥ san parihatasaṃsargadoṣabalī bhavati saṃsargeṇa ye doṣāḥ śarīrābhyantarāste saṃsargadoṣāḥ te parihatā jitā yena saḥ parihatasaṃsargadoṣaḥ tena balī balayuktaḥ doṣanivṛttau guṇapravṛttir ityavaśyam ।।
kiṃ kṛtvā parihatadoṣaḥ amunā payasā uṣṇodakena yāvakaṃ alaktaṃ pītvā śuddho bhavedityarthaḥ ।।

akṛtakṣetrīkaraṇe rasāyanaṃ yo naraḥ prayuñjīta ।
tasya krāmati na rasaḥ sa rasaḥ sarvāṅgadoṣakṛdbhavati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

saṃśodhanasyākaraṇe doṣamāha akṛtetyādi ।।
yo naraḥ pumān akṛtakṣetrīkaraṇe dehe iti śeṣaḥ na kṛtaṃ akṛtaṃ kṣetrīkaraṇaṃ yasmin tasminsati rasāyanaṃ jarāvyādhivināśanauṣadhaṃ prayuñjīta tasya puṃso raso na krāmati svaguṇānna prakāśayati tarhi kiṃ sarvāṅgadoṣakṛdbhavati bāhucaraṇādiṣu ṣaṭsvaṅgeṣu vikārakṛt syāt ।।

iti śuddho jātabalaḥ śālyodanayāvakākhyamudgarasaḥ ।
kṣetrīkṛtanijadehaḥ kurvīta rasāyanaṃ vidhivat ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

rasāyanādhikāratvam āha itītyādi ।।
pūrvoktavidhānena śuddhaḥ san yo jātabalo bhavati sa kṣetrīkṛtanijadehaḥ akṣetraṃ kṣetraṃ kriyata iti kṣetrīkṛto nijadehaḥ śarīraṃ yena saḥ matimān rasāyanaṃ vidhivatprakurvīta ।।
kaiḥ jātabalaḥ śālyodanaṃ ca yāvakākhyaṃ ca mudgāśca taiḥ ।।

suratarutailaghṛtamadhudhātrīrasapayāṃsi nirmathya ।
pītvā viśuddhakoṣṭho bhavati pumānantaritaśuddhaḥ ।।
māsena kāntimedhe dvābhyāṃ praśamayati doṣanikaraṃ ca ।
māsatritayena punaḥ svādamaravapurmahātejāḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidhyantaramāha suratarvityādi ।।
antaritaśuddhaḥ antaritaṃ śuddhaṃ yasya saḥ grahaṇīrogādivarjita ityarthaḥ etāni auṣadhāni nirmathya pītvā viśuddhakoṣṭho bhavati viśuddhaṃ malavarjitaṃ koṣṭhaṃ udaraṃ kasyetyevaṃvidho bhavati ।।
tāni kāni suratarutailetyādīni suratarur devavṛkṣaḥ tattailapeṣaṇaṃ tailamityarthaḥ ghṛtaṃ ājyaṃ madhu kṣaudraṃ dhātrīrasaḥ āmalakīsalilaṃ payo dugdhaṃ etāni sarvāṇi nirmathya ekīkṛtyetyarthaḥ ।।
etadauṣadhabhakṣaṇaguṇaṃ māsakrameṇāha māsenetyādi ।।
asya auṣadhasya māsena māsapramāṇena bhakṣaṇāt kāntir bhavati medhā ceti dvābhyāṃ dvimāsābhyāṃ doṣanikaraṃ gadasamudāyaṃ praśamayati śāntiṃ nayati punarmāsatritayena trimāsapramāṇena svāt svasāmānyaśarīrāt amaravapurdevaśarīro mahātejāḥ dīptimān syādityarthaḥ ।।

suradārutailamājyaṃ triphalārasasaṃyutaṃ ca samabhāgam ।
pītaṃ tat saptāhānnayanavikāraṃ śamaṃ nayati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

yogāntaramāha suradārvityādi ।।
suradārutailaṃ devadārutailaṃ ājyaṃ ghṛtaṃ triphalārasasaṃyutaṃ triphalāyā rasena draveṇa saṃyutaṃ sahitaṃ ca punaḥ samabhāgaṃ tulyāṃśaṃ tatpītaṃ sat saptāhāt saptadinapramāṇataḥ nayanavikāraṃ netrasaṃbhavaṃ rogaṃ śamaṃ nayati śāntiṃ prāpayati ।।

suratarutailaṃ saghṛtaṃ pītvā śālyodanaṃ ca sakṣīram ।
jīrṇāhāre bhuktvā harati hi sakuṣṭhān pīnasādīṃśca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

yogāntaramāha suratarutailam ityādi ।।
devadārutailaṃ saghṛtaṃ sājyaṃ etadubhayaṃ pītvā sakṣīraṃ śālyodanaṃ bhuktvā ṣaṣṭikaudanam ityabhiprāyaḥ punarjīrṇāhāre pratidinaṃ dināntavīradvaye veditavyam ।।
ca punaḥ sakuṣṭhān kuṣṭhaiḥ saha vartante evaṃvidhān pīnasādīn rogān harati dūrīkaroti ।।

ghṛtasahitaḥ pittakṛtāntailayukto vātasaṃbhavān rogān ।
guḍasahito madhunā vā kaphajān hantyamaradārurasaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

yogāntaramāha ghṛtasahita ityādi ।।
amaradāruraso devadārujalaṃ ghṛtasahitaṃ ājyamiśritaḥ pittakṛtān rogān harati nāśayati ।।
punastailayutastailena miśrito devadārurasaḥ vātasaṃbhavān rogān hanti ।।
punarguḍasahitaḥ vā madhunā kṣaudreṇa sahito devadārurasaḥ vātasaṃbhavān rogān hanti ।।
punar guḍasahitaḥ vā madhunā kṣaudreṇa sahito devadārurasaḥ kaphajān rogān hantīti vākyārthaḥ ।।

varjitakāṃjikaśākaṃ payasā śālyodanaṃ ca yuñjīta ।
dvicatuḥṣaṭpalamānaṃ mātrādhamamadhyamajyeṣṭhāḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

rasāyane bhojyābhojyamāha varjitetyādi ।।
varjitakāñjikaśākaṃ varjitaṃ kāñjikaṃ sauvīraṃ śākaṃ vāstukādi ca yasmin tattathā payasā kṣīreṇa saha śālyodanaṃ bhuñjīta ।।
punaḥ śālyodanaṃ kiyanmānaṃ dvicatuḥṣaṭpalamānam ।।
atra mātrādhamamadhyamajyeṣṭhā dvicatuḥṣaṭpalapramāṇā adhamamadhyamottamabaleṣu prayojyetyarthaḥ ।।

tadanu pātanaśuddhaṃ sūtakam āroṭam aśnīyāt ।
svedanamūrcchotthāpanapātanarodhāśca niyamaśca ।।
abhrakasahitaḥ pātyo vidhinā yāvatsthiro bhavati ।
athavā mākṣikasahitaḥ pātyaḥ sūto vidhānena ।।
ityāroṭaḥ sūtaḥ kṣetrīkaraṇe niyujyate prathamam ।
atha rasayogamāha tadityādi ।।
tadanu pathyamātropayogānantaraṃ pātanaśuddhaṃ pātanena śuddhaṃ sūtakaṃ āroṭam eva sāmānyam evāśnīyāt bhakṣayet ।।
ca punaḥ svedanamūrchotthāpanarodhāśca svedanaṃ ca mūrchā ca utthāpanaṃ ca pātanāni ca nirodhaśceti dvandvaḥ ete yadyapi santi niyamaśca yadyapyasti tathāpyāroṭaḥ pātanena syād ityarthaḥ ।।
prasaṅgataḥ pātanamāha abhraketyādi ।।
sūtaḥ abhrakasahitaḥ gaganamilitaḥ san pātyaḥ ।।
kena vidhānena ḍamarukayantrādinā ।।
punastāvadyāvatsthiro bhavati ।।
athavā vidhyantare sūto mākṣikasahitaḥ pātyo vidhānena ayamapi yāvatsthiro bhavati ।।
rasāyane sūtasya āroṭādividhānamāha itītyādi ।।
āroṭa iti pūrvoktena pātanakarmaṇā ūrdhvādhastiryagbhavena sādhita āroṭaḥ saḥ prathamaṃ yathā syāttathā rasāyane jarāvyādhināśane niyujyate iti ।।

athavā kalkayogena rasādisambhūtena raso bhasma kṛtvā ।।

athavā bhasma ca kṛtvā baddho vā kalkayogena ।।
mākṣikaśilājatulohacūrṇapathyākṣaviḍaṅgaghṛtamadhubhiḥ ।
saṃyuktaṃ rasamādau kṣetrīkaraṇāya yuñjīta ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

dvividhaṃ bhasma ūrdhvagaṃ talabhasma ca varṇabhedena ṣaḍvidhaṃ śvetaṃ bhasma pītaṃ bhasma haritaṃ bhasma raktaṃ bhasma kṛṣṇaṃ bhasma karburaṃ bhasma iti ṣaḍvidhaṃ tatkṛtvā kṣetrīkaraṇe niyujyate prathamam ।।
rasayogamāha mākṣiketyādi ।।
mākṣikaṃ tāpyaṃ śilājatu prasiddhaṃ lohacūrṇaṃ māritamuṇḍasya rajaḥ pathyā harītakī akṣo vibhītakaḥ viḍaṅgaṃ kṛmighnaṃ ghṛtam ājyaṃ madhu kṣaudraṃ etaiḥ samprayuktaṃ rasaṃ kṣetrīkaraṇāya prayuñjīteti vākyārthaḥ ।।

iti kalkīkṛtasūtaṃ ghanakāntamadhughṛtādisaṃyuktam ।
bhuktvāmaratāṃ gacchetkṣetrīkaraṇaṃ pradhānamidam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

ityuktavidhānena kalkīkṛtaṃ sūtaṃ bhuktvā amaratāṃ devatvaṃ gacchet ।।
iti kiṃ ghanakāntamadhughṛtādisaṃyuktaṃ ghano'bhrakaḥ kāntaṃ lohajāti madhu kṣaudraṃ ghṛtam ājyaṃ ādiśabdāt sitā grāhyā etaiḥ saṃyuktaṃ sat kalkīkṛtaṃ idaṃ ca pradhānaṃ kṣetrīkaraṇaṃ kṣetrī kriyate'neneti ।।
ityāroṭakriyā ।।

atha kṛṣṇaṃ vā pītaṃ vā saṃyojyaṃ ghanaṃ śikhiprabhaṃ bahuśaḥ ।
surabhīkṣīraniṣiktaṃ gatagiridoṣaṃ rasāyane yojyam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha patrābhrakriyā ।।
kṛṣṇaṃ śyāmavarṇaṃ ghanaṃ abhraṃ pītaṃ pītavarṇaṃ ghanaṃ vā bahuśo naikavāraṃ śikhiprabhaṃ agniprabhaṃ sat surabhīkṣīraniṣiktaṃ secitaṃ kāryaṃ punargatagiridoṣaṃ yathā syāttathā gatā girijā doṣā mahīdharasaṃbhavā doṣā yasmāt tadevaṃ saṃśodhayitvā tat ghanaṃ rasāyane jarāvyādhivināśakaraṇe yojyam ।।

niścandrikamapi śuddhaṃ viḍaṃgatriphalājyamadhusamāyuktam ।
pratidivasaṃ palamekaṃ bhuktvā kṣīrāśano vidhinā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

abhrakayogamāha niścandrikamityādi ।।
ghanaṃ niścandrikamapi śuddhaṃ candrikārahitamapi nirdoṣaṃ viḍaṅgatriphalājyamadhurasamāyuktaṃ kṛmighnaharītakīvibhītakāmalakaghṛtakṣaudramilitaṃ pratidivasaṃ pratidinaṃ ekapalapramāṇaṃ sarvaṃ bhuktvā vidhinā śuddhaśarīravidhānena kṣīrāśano bhavet kṣīreṇa saha śālyodanāśanaṃ samācaredityarthaḥ ।।

trikaṭukaviḍaṅgatriphalāmākṣikaśilājatuyutaṃ vyoma ।
kṣīraudanam aśnīyājjīvati jantuḥ śataṃ varṣam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha trikaṭuketyādi ।।
vyoma abhrakaṃ trikaṭukaviḍaṅgatriphalāmākṣikaśilājatuyutaṃ pippalīmaricanāgaraharītakīvibhītakāmalakakṣaudraśilājatumilitaṃ aśnīyād bhakṣayet ।।
punaḥ kṣīraudanaṃ pathyamaśnīyāt ।।
eva kṛte sati jantuḥ śataṃ jīvati jantujanyuśarīriṇaḥ ityamaraḥ ।।
iti patrābhrakaprakriyā ।।

ityevamādayo'nye kāñjikayuktāśca kīrtitā bahuśaḥ ।
patrābhrakaprayogā varjyā niryuktikāste hi ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

abhrakasyottarottaraṃ darśayannāha itītyādi ।।
ityevamādayaḥ iti pūrvoktā yogā ādayo yeṣāṃ te anye kāñjikayuktāśca kāñjikenāranālena yuktāḥ yogīkṛtāḥ granthāntare rasāvatārādau bahuśaḥ kīrtitāḥ kathitāḥ te patrābhrakayogāḥ niryuktikāḥ niryukte bhavā ikpratyayāntās te varjyāḥ sevane'yogyā ityarthaḥ ।।

ye patrābhrakayogā rasāyanārthaṃ kīrtitā vidhinā ।
ajñātadravyaguṇaistairupadiṣṭo jarāmṛtyuḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

avidhinā patrābhrakayogo vikārāyetyata āha ya ityādi ।।
ye ajñātadravyaguṇaiḥ ajñātā dravyāṇāṃ abhrādināṃ guṇā yais tair evaṃvidhaiḥ puṃbhiḥ vidhinā sāmānyavidhānena patrābhrakayogāḥ rasāyanārthaṃ kīrtitās tair eva jarā mṛtyuśca upadiṣṭaḥ jarā pālityaṃ mṛtyur vyādhiḥ ।।

aprāptalokabhāvaṃ ghano'sya jaṭharāgnimupaśamaṃ nayati ।
agniṃ vināpi naśyati paribhūto vividharogagaṇaiḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

jarāmṛtyorupadeśe hetumāha aprāptetyādi aprāptalokabhavaṃ yathā syāttathā asya kartuḥ ghanaḥ ।।
jaṭharāgniṃ vināpi pumān naśyati nāśaṃ prāpnoti ।।
