kiṃbhūtaḥ san vividharogagaṇaiḥ nānārogasamūhaiḥ paribhūto vijitaḥ san iti vākyārthaḥ ।।
kāṣṭhe sthitam api ghanapaṭalamadhye'pi abhre'bhrasattvaṃ sthitaṃ tadāha abhrasatvaṃ ghanasāraṃ ghanapaṭale sthitamapi nijakāryaṃ svakīyakṛtyaṃ tathā na kurute vahniragniḥ ।।
kāṣṭhe dāruṇi sthitaḥ san nijakāryaṃ na kurute tu punaḥ yathā ghṛtaṃ payasi dugdhe sthitaṃ sat svīkāryaṃ na kurute cāgrahir iva dhanasthamiva madhye sthitaṃ kāryaṃ kurute'tiniḥsṛtaṃ sat pṛthagbhūtaṃ sat nijakāryaṃ kuruta iti bhāvaḥ ।।

abhra inedible
abhrasya rasāyanināṃ bhakṣyamiha kīrtitaṃ paraṃ satvam ।
trividhaṃ gaganamabhakṣyaṃ kācaḥ kiṭṭaṃ ca pattrarajaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

bhakṣyābhakṣyam abhramāha abhrasyetyādi ।।
abhrakasatvamiha kṣetrīkaraṇe rasāyanināṃ jarāvyādhivināśecchūnāṃ param utkṛṣṭaṃ bhakṣyaṃ aśanayogyaṃ kīrtitam ।।
punastrividhaṃ triprakāraṃ gaganamabhraṃ abhakṣyaṃ abhojyam ।।
kiṃ tat kācaḥ kācarūpaṃ kiṭṭaṃ malarūpaṃ pattrarajaḥ sāmānyābhracūrṇaṃ ceti trividhamityarthaḥ ।।

ādau ghanaloharajastriphalārasabhāvanaiś ca nirghṛṣṭam ।
kurvītāñjanasadṛśaṃ sthagitavastreṇa sūryakaraiḥ ।।
itthaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ kṛtvā vividhakāntalohacūrṇasamam ।
lohaghanaṃ ca tadevaṃ bhṛṅgeṇa ca sādhayed bahuśaḥ ।।
triphalāghṛtamadhumiśritam amṛtam idaṃ māsasthitaṃ dhānye ।
śastrakaṭorikasampuṭamadhyagataṃ pūjitaṃ mantraiḥ ।।
māsena tu taduddhṛtya jñātvā balaṃ tatprayuñjīta ।
kāntaṃ vinātha gaganaṃ gaganaṃ vinā tathā ca kāntam ।।
sthaulyaṃ paṭalaṃ kācaṃ timirārbudakarṇanādaśūlāni ।
hantyarśāṃsi bhagandaramehaplīhādi pālityam ।।
etatkurvanmatimān gorasamastupradhānam aśnīyāt ।
jāṅgalamudgājyapayaḥ śālyodanaṃ brahmacaryeṇa ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

adhunā ghanasattvalohasādhanam āha ādāvityādi ।।
ādau prathamaṃ ghanaloharajaḥ ghanamabhrasatvaṃ loharajaḥ kāntacūrṇaṃ triphalārasabhāvanaiḥ harītakīvibhītakāmalakadravapuṭanair nirghṛṣṭaṃ sat añjanasadṛśaṃ sauvīrāñjanatulyaṃ kurvīta kaiḥ kṛtvā sūryakaraiḥ kena sthagitavastreṇa ācchāditapaṭena vastreṇācchādya sūryakarasannidhau dhāryamityarthaḥ ।।
itthamityādi ।।
itthamamunā prakāreṇa ślakṣṇam añjanasannibhaṃ yathā syāt tathā ghanasatvakāntaṃ kṛtvā punarlohaghanaṃ lohaṃ muṇḍādi ghanaṃ abhrasatvaṃ etadubhayaṃ vividhakāntalohacūrṇasamaṃ vividhā nānājātayaḥ ayaskāntabhedāḥ teṣāṃ cūrṇaṃ tatsamaṃ kṛtvā bhṛṅgeṇa ca bahuśo'nekavāraṃ sādhayedbhāvayedityarthaḥ ।।
taccāha triphaletyādi ।।
tadbhṛṅgarājena bahuśo bhāvitaṃ ghanasatvakāntaṃ idam amṛtaṃ sudhāsamaṃ na mṛtamamṛtaṃ tat triphalāmadhughṛtamiśritaṃ harītakīvibhītakāmalakaghṛtakṣaudramilitaṃ dhānye kasyacidannasyāntaḥ māsasthitaṃ kuryāt māsaikaparimāṇaṃ tatra vidhātavyamiti vyaktiḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ mantraiśca sampūjitam ।।
tathā mantrastu ।
mandāramālākulitālakāyai kapālamālāṅkitaśekharāya ।
divyāmbarāyai ca digambarāya namaḥ śivāyai ca namaḥ śivāya ।
ityādibhiḥ ।।
taccāha māsenetyādi ।।
dhānyānmāsena māsaikaparimāṇenoddhṛtya bahirnītvā punarapi balaṃ jñātvā prayuñjīta bhoktre dadyāt atha viśeṣaṃ darśayati kāntaṃ vinā abhrakasatvameva kṛtvā prayuñjīta ca punargaganaṃ vinā kāntaṃ kevalaṃ pūrvavidhānena sādhayitvā prayuñjītetyarthaḥ ।।
phalamāha sthaulyam ityādi ।।
sthaulyamiti medorogaḥ paṭalakācatimirāṇi netrarogāḥ arbudaṃ granthiviśeṣaḥ karṇanādaḥ pratītaḥ śūlamaṣṭavidhaṃ etāni hanti arśāṃsi gudajāni bhagandaramehaplīhādi bhagandaraḥ gudavraṇaṃ mehaḥ pramehaḥ bījavikāraḥ plīhā plīharogaḥ ete rogā ādiryasya tat hanti pālityaṃ jarāṃ ca nāśayatītyarthaḥ ।।
pathyam āha etadityādi ।।
etanniṣpannauṣadhabhakṣaṇaṃ kurvan matimān puruṣaḥ gorasamastupradhānaṃ goraso godugdhaṃ mastu dadhimastu evaṃpradhānamannamaśnīyāt bhuñjīta ।।
punarjāṅgalamudgājyapayo'śnīyāt jāṅgalasyedaṃ jāṅgalaṃ svalpāmbuśākhīdeśaḥ jāṅgalaḥ mudgaḥ pratīto'nnaviśeṣaḥ ājyaṃ ghṛtaṃ payo dugdhaṃ vā salilaṃ yanmudgājyapayaḥ taccāśnīyāt ।।
ca punaḥ śālyodanamaśnīyāt ।।
etatsarvaṃ brahmacaryeṇa kartavyamityarthaḥ ।।
iti satvābhrakriyā ।।

ghanasatvapādajīrṇaḥ kāntajīrṇo yattīkṣṇasamajīrṇaḥ ।
kṣetrīkaraṇaḥ paramaḥ prayujyate'pi punarāroṭaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha jīrṇarasasyādhikyaṃ darśayannāha ghanetyādi ।।
ghanasatvaṃ pādapramāṇaṃ jīrṇaṃ yasmin saḥ ।।
kāntajīrṇa iti pādapramāṇakāntajīrṇa ityarthaḥ ।।
punastīkṣṇaṃ samaṃ jīrṇaṃ yasminnevaṃvidho rasaḥ ।।
kṣetrīkaraṇaṃ pradhānaṃ sarvatretyarthaḥ ।
baddho yaḥ khoṭatāṃ yāto dhmāto dhmātaḥ kṣayaṃ vrajet ।
khoṭo bandhaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ śīghraṃ sarvagadāpahaḥ ।
iti granthāntare ।।

ghanasatvakāntasūtaṃ mṛtahema śatāvarīrasopetam ।
ghṛtamadhulīḍhaṃ varṣānnihanti mṛtyuṃ jarāṃ caiva ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

ghanasatvam abhrasāraḥ kāntaṃ cumbakotthaṃ sūto rasaḥ ekavadbhāvo dvandvasamāsāt tathā mṛtaṃ hema pañcatvamāptaṃ kanakaṃ ca etaccatuṣkaṃ śatāvarīrasopetaṃ śatamūlīdravabhāvitaṃ punarghṛtamadhulīḍhaṃ ghṛtamadhubhyāṃ līḍhaṃ āsvāditaṃ sat varṣādvarṣaparimāṇāt mṛtyuvyādhiṃ jarāṃ ca hanti nāśayatītyarthaḥ ।।

eṣāmekaṃ yogaṃ kṣetrīkaraṇārthamāditaḥ kṛtvā ।
saṃvatsaramayanaṃ vā niḥśreyasasiddhaye yojyam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

viśeṣamāha eṣāmityādi ।।
eṣāṃ pūrvoktānāṃ yogānāṃ madhye ādita ārambhataḥ ekaṃ yogaṃ kṛtvā niḥśreyaso mokṣaḥ tatsiddhaye niṣpattaye saṃvatsaraṃ varṣaparimāṇaṃ ayanaṃ ṣaṇmāsaparyantaṃ yojyaṃ bhoktṛṣu iti śeṣaḥ ।।
muktiḥ kaivalyanirvāṇaśreyoniḥśreyasāmṛtam ityamaraḥ ।।

abhrakasasyakamākṣikarasakadaradavimalavajragirijatubhiḥ ।
vaikrāntakāntatīkṣṇair hāṭakatārāratāmraiśca ।।
saṃyuktairvyastairvā dvitricaturbhir yathālābham ।
jīrṇahato rasendro rasāyane śasyate sadbhiḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

bahūnnirdiśan viśeṣamāha abhraketyādi ।।
abhrakaḥ prasiddhaḥ sasyakaś capalaḥ mākṣikaṃ tāpyaṃ rasakaṃ kharparaṃ daradaṃ hiṅgulaṃ vimalaṃ sitamākṣikaṃ vajrakaṃ hīrakaṃ girijatu śilājatu etaiḥ ।।
punar vaikrāntetyādi vaikrāntaṃ vajrabhūmijaṃ rajaḥ kāntaṃ lohajāti tīkṣṇaṃ sāraḥ etaiśca ।।
hāṭakatārāratāmraiś ca hāṭakaṃ hema tāraṃ rūpyaṃ āraṃ rājarītiḥ tāmraṃ śulbaṃ etaiśca etair uddiṣṭaiḥ abhrakāditāmrāntaiḥ samastair ekatrīkṛtair vyastairvā pṛthakkṛtairvā yathālābhaṃ lābhamanatikramya bhavatīti yathālābhaṃ dvitricaturbhirvā abhrādyairjīrṇahato rasendro jīrṇābhrādīnāṃ hatiryasmin sa tathoktaḥ rasāyane jarāvyādhivināśane rasaśāstramarmajñaiḥ śasyate abhrādayaḥ praśastā uktā ityarthaḥ ।।
yugmam ।।
vajrādibhirhataḥ sūto hatasūtasamo'paraḥ ।
śṛṅkhalābaddhanāmā syāddehalohavidhāyakaḥ ।
asya prabhāvādvegena vyāptirbhavati niścitam ।
iti granthāntare ।।

viṣanāgavaṅgabaddho bhukto hi rasaḥ karoti kuṣṭhādīn ।
uparasabaddhe tu rase sphuṭanti bhukte tathāṅgāni ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

kutsitavidhānaṃ darśayannāha viṣetyādi ।।
viṣanāgavaṅgabaddho rasaḥ viṣaṃ saktukādikaṃ nāgaḥ sīsakaḥ vaṅgaṃ trapu etairbaddho bandhanamāptaḥ sa bhuktaḥ san hi niścitaṃ kuṣṭhādīn kuṣṭhajvarakṣayādīn ।।
uparasabaddhe rase uparasair gandhādibhiḥ aṣṭabhiḥ baddho bandhanam āpanno yo'sau rasaḥ tasmin bhukte sati bhokturaṅgāni hastapādādīni sphuṭanti ।।

ghanasattvakāntakāñcībhāskaratīkṣṇaiś ca cīrṇajīrṇasya ।
sūtasya guñjāmātrā māṣakamekaṃ parā mātrā ।।
śatavedhino dviguñjā tathā sahasraikavedhino guñjā ।
ardhā ca lakṣavedhinaḥ siddhārthaḥ koṭivedhinaḥ sūtāt ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

jīrṇarasasya mātrām āha ghanetyādi ।।
etaiścīrṇajīrṇaṃ pūrvaṃ cīrṇaṃ kavalitaṃ paścājjīrṇaṃ jāraṇam āpannaṃ tasya sūtasya guñjā mātrā bhakṣaṇāya guñjā yathā ।
ṣaṭsarṣapair yavastveko guñjaikā tu yavaistribhiḥ ।
iti ।।
parā anyā mātrā anyajīrṇasūtasya mātrā māṣamekaṃ māṣako yathā ।
guñjābhirdaśabhiḥ prokto māṣako brahmaṇā purā ।
iti ।।
etaiḥ kaiḥ ghanasattvakāntakāñcībhāskaratīkṣṇaiḥ abhrakasattvacumbakatāpyatāmrasārair iti ।।
atha vedhaviśeṣeṇa parimāṇamāha śatetyādi ।।
śatavedhinaḥ sūtasya guñjāpramāṇā mātrā jñeyā tathā tena prakāreṇa sahasraikavedhinaḥ sūtasyāpi guñjāmānameva lakṣavedhinaḥ sūtāt ardhā raktikā punaḥ koṭivedhinaḥ sūtāt siddhārthaḥ sarṣapamānā ।।
śatāṃśena vedho vidyate yasmin sa śatavedhī tasya śatavedhinaḥ ।।
evaṃ sarvatra jñeyam ।।

hemaniyojitasūtaṃ kāntamaṇiṃ vividhaguṭikāśca ।
japahomadevatārcananirataḥ pumāniti dhārayet ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

japaḥ aghorādijapaḥ homastaddaśāṃśena havanaṃ devatārcanaṃ devatānāṃ gaṇeśaviṣṇuraviśivacaṇḍīnāṃ arcanaṃ eteṣu nirataḥ saktaḥ evaṃvidhiḥ pumān ।।
iti kiṃ hemaniyojitasūtaṃ dhārayet hemnā saha niyojito miśrito yaḥ sūtaḥ taṃ kāntamaṇiḥ kāntaścāsau maṇiśca vā kāntamaṇiḥ kāntasaṃjñako maṇiḥ ca punaḥ vividhaguṭikāḥ vividhāśca tā guṭikāśceti ।।

śālestu piṣṭakodbhavabhojanam ājyaṃ ca mudgamāṃsarasaiḥ ।
yavagodhūmānnāni ca gokṣīraṃ mastu ca viśeṣāt ।।
pāne jalamakṣāraṃ madhurāṇi yāni kāni śastāni ।
peyaṃ cāturjātakarpūrāmodamuditamukham ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha pathyānāha śālerityādi ।।
śāleḥ ṣaṣṭikādeḥ piṣṭodbhavabhojanaṃ piṣṭakotpannaṃ ca tadbhojanaṃ ceti ।।
ājyaṃ ghṛtam ।।
kaiḥ saha mudgamāṃsarasaiḥ saha mudgāḥ pratītāḥ atra viśeṣāt māṃsāni bhojyāni gokṣīraṃ ca bhojyaṃ punarmastu gorasasaṃbhavaṃ viśeṣāt bhojyam ।।
pāne akṣāraṃ jalaṃ miṣṭajalaṃ prayojyaṃ punaḥ yāni kāni miṣṭāni dravyāṇi atrānuktatamāni praśastāni śreṣṭhāni punaḥ caturjātakakarpūrāmodamuditamukhaṃ yathā syāt tathā dravyaṃ peyaṃ pātavyaṃ caturjātakaṃ tvakpatrailānāgakesaraṃ karpūraṃ ghanasāraṃ eṣām āmodena parimalena muditaṃ yanmukhaṃ vāsitamukham ityarthaḥ ।।
yuvatyā jalpanaṃ kāryaṃ yuvatyā cāṅgamardanam ।
tasyāḥ sparśanamātreṇa dehe kramati sūtakaḥ ।
iti viśeṣo granthāntarāt ।।

madyāranālapānaṃ tailaṃ dadhi vā rase neṣṭam ।
kaṭutailenābhyaṅgaṃ vapuṣi na kuryādrasāyane matimān ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

apathyānyāha madyetyādi ।।
madyāranāletyādi madyaṃ surā āranālaṃ kāñjikaṃ tayoḥ pānaṃ neṣṭaṃ na praśastaṃ vā tailaṃ dadhi na neṣṭaṃ tailaṃ tilodbhavaṃ dadhi dugdhavikāraḥ etayorapi pānaṃ na praśastaṃ kaṭutailena sarṣapatailena vapuṣi abhyaṅgaṃ mardanaṃ na kuryāt ।।
matimān rasāyane adhikaraṇe ityarthaḥ ।।

dagdham apakvam amadhuram uṣṇaṃ kṣīraṃ na naṣṭamāṃsaṃ tu ।
paryuṣitaṃ phalamūlaṃ bhakṣyaṃ naivātra nirdiṣṭam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

dagdhaṃ dravyaṃ rasāyane neṣṭaṃ apakvaṃ ca neṣṭaṃ amadhuraṃ kaṭutiktakaṣāyāmlalavaṇaṃ ca neṣṭaṃ uṣṇaṃ vahnitaptamiti tu punaḥ naṣṭamāṃsaṃ ninditamāṃsaṃ neṣṭaṃ punaḥ paryuṣitaṃ saṃdhānīkṛtaṃ evaṃvidhaṃ phalamūlaṃ phalaṃ mūlaṃ ca atra rasāyane bhakṣyaṃ na nirdiṣṭaṃ kathitaṃ ।
kūṣmāṇḍaṃ karkaṭī caiva kaliṅgaṃ kāravellakam ।
kusumbhikā ca karkoṭī kadalī kākamācikā ।
kakārāṣṭakametaddhi varjayedrasabhakṣakaḥ ।
iti granthāntare ।।

atha laṅghanaṃ na kāryaṃ yāmādho bhojanaṃ naiva ।
ityapanīya niṣiddhaṃ rasarāje dhīmatā kāryam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

asmin rasāyane laṅghanaṃ na kāryaṃ punar yāmādhaḥ praharamadhye bhojanaṃ na kāryam ityarthaḥ ।।

varjitacintākopaḥ kuryācca sukhāmbunā snānam ।
noccāṭayed grahajvararākṣasabhūtāni mātṛdevīṃśca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha varjitetyādi ।।
varjitacintākopa iti cintā ca kopaśceti cintākopau tau varjitau yena saḥ evaṃvidhaḥ san sukhāmbunā sukhoṣṇāmbunā snānaṃ kuryāt ।।
graharākṣasabhūtāni noccāṭayet grahaṇādgrahāḥ piśācādayaḥ jvaro rogarājaḥ rākṣasāḥ kravyādāḥ bhūtāni devayonayaḥ etāni noccāṭayet svasthānānna cālayet ।।
punarmātṛdevīṃśca mātaraḥ saptamātaraḥ devyo dakṣiṇyādayaḥ tā api noccāṭayet ।।

parame brahmaṇi līnaḥ praśāntacittaḥ samatvamāpannaḥ ।
āśvāsayan trivargaṃ vijitya rasānandaparitṛptaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

cintākopanirodhe hetum āha parame ityādi ।।
rasāyanakartā parame brahmaṇi citsvarūpe līnaḥ tanmayatāṃ prāpto bhavet praśāntacittaśca viṣayebhyo nivṛttamanā bhavet samatvamāpannaḥ svasute śatrau ca nirvairo yathā syāt tathā trivargaṃ dharmārthakāmarūpaṃ vijitya rasānandaparitṛpto bhavet harṣaparipūrita ityarthaḥ ।।

yastyaktvā śāstravidhiṃ pravartate svecchayā rase mūḍhaḥ ।
tasya viruddhācārād ajīrṇamutpadyate nitarām ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vidherniyatatvaṃ darśayannāha ya ityādi ।।
yaḥ pumān śāstravidhiṃ tyaktvā svecchayā ucchṛṅkhalamanasā rase sūte pravartate sa mūḍhaḥ jñānaśūnyaḥ tasya puṃsaḥ viruddhācārāt nitarāmatiśayena ajīrṇam utpadyate tadrasājīrṇamiti ।।

sambhavatīhājīrṇe nidrālasyaṃ jvarastamo dāhaḥ ।
nābhitalaśūlamalpaṃ jaḍatāruciraṅgabhaṅgaśca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

rasājīrṇalakṣaṇamāha sambhavatītyādi ।।
iha rasāyane ajīrṇaṃ yadā sambhavati utpadyate tadā etāni lakṣaṇāni syuḥ ।।
nidrā atiśayena nidrā ālasyaṃ aṅgāṅgaśaithilyaṃ jvaraḥ prasiddhaḥ tamo mūrchā dāha ūṣmā punarnābhitale bastau alpamalpaṃ śūlaṃ jaḍatāsyasya aruciḥ nirabhilāpitā bhaṅgo'ṅgasya aṅgamardanaṃ bhokturetāni lakṣaṇāni rasājīrṇe syur ityarthaḥ ।।

jñātvetyevam ajīrṇam asya pracchādanāya yogo'yam ।
kāryo divasatritayaṃ saṃtyajya rasāyanaṃ sudhiyā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

ajīrṇe'pyupāyamāha jñātvetyādi ।।
ityevam uktaprakāreṇa nidrādilakṣaṇenājīrṇaṃ jñātvā dhīmatā puṃsā asyājīrṇasya pracchādanāya vināśāya rasāyanaṃ saṃtyajya divasatritayaṃ yogaḥ kāryaḥ ।।

karkoṭīmūlarasaṃ kaṣāyam atha sindhunā pibettridinam ।
sauvarcalasahitaṃ vā gojalasahitaṃ rasājīrṇe ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha karkoṭītyādi ।।
karkoṭīmūlarasaṃ karkoṭī yā vallī tasyāḥ mūlarasaṃ tridinaṃ pibet vātha kaṣāyaṃ kathaṃ sindhunā saindhavena sahitaṃ pibet vā tatkvāthaṃ gojalasahitaṃ gomūtramilitaṃ rasājīrṇe pibet sauvarcalasahitamiti sauvarcalasya prativāpaṃ karkoṭīrase nikṣipya pibet tridinaṃ sarvatretyarthaḥ ।।

piṣṭvātha mātuluṅgīṃ pibati rasaṃ śuṇṭhisaindhavaṃ prātaḥ ।
kvathitaṃ gosalilena tu rakṣati samyak rasājīrṇam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

anyaccāha piṣṭvetyādi ।।
mātuluṅgasyeyaṃ jaṭā mātuluṅgī tāṃ piṣṭvā tasyā rasaṃ śuṇṭhī saindhavaṃ ca yaḥ pumān prātaḥ pibati tu punaḥ kvathitaṃ tasyāḥ kaṣāyaṃ gosalilena yaḥ pibati rasājīrṇe taṃ puruṣaṃ rakṣati na vināśayatītyarthaḥ ।।

kathamapi yaccājñānāt nāgādikalaṅkito raso bhuktaḥ ।
tannodanāya ca pibet gojalakaṭukāravalliśiphāḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

nāgādiyuktarasabhuktopāyam āha katham apītyādi ।।
ca punaḥ yat yasmāt nāgādikalaṅkito rasaḥ nāgavaṅgasahito raso'jñānātkathamapi bhuktaḥ tannodanāya tasya nāgavaṅgāṅkitarasasya nodanāya gojalakaṭukāravalliśiphāḥ gojalaṃ gomūtraṃ kaṭutiktā kāravallīśiphā kāravallīlatāyāḥ śiphā jaṭā etadauṣadhaṃ pibet tena nāgavaṅgādidoṣo vinaśyati ।।

śarapuṃkhāsuradālīpaṭolabimbīśca kākamācī ca ।
ekatamā ceduditā śṛtāmajīrṇe hi seveta ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha śarapuṅkhetyādi ।।
āsāṃ auṣadhīnāṃ madhye ekatamā yā uditā kathitā śṛtā kvathitā tāṃ hi niścitaṃ ajīrṇe seveta tena ajīrṇaṃ naśyatīti bhāvaḥ ।।
tāḥ kā auṣadhyaḥ śarapuṅkhā prasiddhā suradālī devadālī paṭolaṃ pratītaṃ nāma bimbī golā kākamācī prasiddhā etā ityarthaḥ ।।

atyamlalavaṇakaṭukai rasasaṃsrāvo jaro bhavati ।
atimadhuraiśca vinaśyati jaṭharavahniḥ satatabhuktaiśca ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

taccāha atyamletyādi ।।
atyamlaṃ cukrādi atilavaṇaṃ kṣārādi atikaṭukaṃ nimbakaṭukītyādi etai rasasaṃsrāvo jaro jāraṇakaro bhavati jaratīti jaraḥ ।।
punarapi madhuraiḥ ikṣurasādibhiḥ satatabhuktaiḥ jaṭharavahniḥ koṣṭhāgniḥ vinaśyati abhyāśrayo vinaśyatītyabhiprāyaḥ ।।

yaḥ punarevaṃ satataṃ karoti mūḍhaḥ samāhāram ।
tasya vinaśyatyagnirna khalu krāmati raso bhaved vyādhiḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

tadviśeṣamāha ya ityādi ।।
yaḥ punar mūḍho mūrkho ajīrṇānantaraṃ atyamlalavaṇakaṭukāhāraṃ satataṃ nirantaraṃ karoti tasyāgniḥ koṣṭhāgnir vinaśyati rasaśca na krāmati svaguṇānna prakāśayati ।।
tarhi kiṃ bhavedityāha vyādhirbhaved ityarthaḥ ।।

yastu mahāgnisahatvād rasācchatasahasralakṣavedhīśaḥ ।
anayā kriyayā sidhyati sa yatnādrasakriyāyogāt ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

rasācchatasahasralakṣavedhī bhavet sa yatnāt anayā pūrvoktakriyayā sidhyati ।।

śatasahasralakṣavedhī koṭir athārbudanirbudaṃ vāpi ।
piṣṭaṃ bhuñjīta rasaṃ balisahitaṃ siddhido bhavati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

athottaravidhānena lakṣaṇamāha śatetyādi ।।
śatasahasralakṣavedhī rasaḥ ।।
balisahitaṃ piṣṭaṃ rasaṃ bhuñjīta balinā gandhakena sahitam śatādārabhya sahasralakṣakoṭyarbudānāṃ krameṇa daśaguṇottaraṃ saṃkhyā jñātavyā ।।
evaṃ kṛtaḥ san rasaḥ siddhido yathoktaguṇakṛdbhavatītyarthaḥ ।।

krāmati tato hi sūto janayati putrāṃśca devagarbhābhān ।
strīṣu ca niścalakāmo bhavati valīpalitanirmuktaḥ ।।
buddhirbalaṃ prabhāvaḥ saha cāyuṣā vardhate rasāyaninaḥ ।
prāptasya divyabuddhiṃ divyāśca guṇāḥ pravardhante ।।
evaṃ rasasaṃsiddho duḥkhajarāmaraṇavarjito guṇavān ।
khegamanena ca nityaṃ saṃcarate sakalabhuvaneṣu ।।
dātā bhuvanatritaye sraṣṭā so'pīha padmayoniriva ।
bhartā viṣṇuriva syātsaṃhartā rudravadbhavati ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

pūrvavidhānaṃ praśaṃsayann āha krāmatītyādi ।।
tataḥ pūrvavidhānataḥ sūtaḥ krāmati svaguṇān prakāśayati sūte krāmati sati devagarbhābhān putrān janayati devagarbhavat ābhā kāntir yeṣāṃ te tān punaḥ strīṣu niścalaḥ sadāsthāyī kāmo ratyabhilāṣo vā madano yasya sa tathoktaḥ punar valīpalitanirmuktaḥ valyaśca palitāni ca tair nirmukto vivarjitaḥ valiścarma jarākṛtaṃ ityamaraḥ palitaṃ keśaśvetatvaṃ evaṃvidho bhavati pumān iti śeṣaḥ ।।
punaḥ kiṃ syādityāha buddhirityādi ।।
rasāyaninaḥ rasāyanaṃ prāptasya hi puṃsaḥ buddhirvardhate balaṃ ca vardhate kena saha āyuṣā jīvitakālena saha punar divyabuddhiṃ prāptasya rasāyaninaḥ divyāḥ prakaraṇādguṇā medhādayaḥ pravardhante prakāśanta ityarthaḥ ।।
taccāha evamityādi ।।
evamamunā prakāreṇa rasasaṃsiddhaḥ puruṣaḥ rasaḥ pāradaḥ saṃsiddhaḥ samyak siddho yasya vā rasena saṃsiddhaḥ jarāmaraṇavarjito bhavati vṛddhatvavyādhirahita ityarthaḥ guṇavāṃśca bhavati guṇā medhādayaḥ ।।
punaḥ khegamanena ākāśagamanena nityaṃ sakalabhuvaneṣu samastalokeṣu saṃcarate ityarthaḥ ।।
dātā bhuvanatritaye svargamṛtyupātāle bhavati sarvādhika ityabhiprāyaḥ ।।
so'pi pumān iha bhuvanatritaye svargamṛtyupātāle sraṣṭā sarjako bhavati ।।
ka iva padmayoniriva brahmeva ।।
punaḥ bhartā pālanārthaṃ trikasya viṣṇuriva ca bhavati ।।
punaḥ saṃhartā rudravat bhavati sṛṣṭisthitivināśeṣu brahmādīnāṃ trayīva syādityarthaḥ ।।

amarasundarīguṭikā
kāntābhrasattvahematāraṃ cārkaḥ samāṃśataḥ saṃkhyā ।
baddhaṃ sūtasamāṃśaṃ dhmātaṃ golaṃ kṛtaṃ khoṭam ।।
bāhye rasena liptaṃ vadanagataṃ śastravārakaṃ rogān ।
hanti hi śarīrasaṃsthān nāmnāmarasundarī guṭikā ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

amarasundarīguṭikāvidhānaṃ guṇāṃścāha kāntetyādi ।।
kāntaṃ cumbakaṃ abhraṃ yugmam ।।
abhrakasattvaṃ pratītaṃ hema kanakaṃ tāraṃ ca tat ekavadbhāvo dvandvatvāt punararkaḥ tāmram eṣāṃ kāntādīnāṃ saṃkhyā gaṇanā samāṃśataḥ samabhāgato jñeyā ।।
punaḥ sūtasamāṃśaṃ pāradena tulyabhāgaṃ dhmātaṃ kuryāt andhamūṣāyāṃ iti śeṣaḥ ।।
kiṃkṛtaṃ sat bāhye baddhagolopari rasena māraṇāyām uktadraveṇa liptaṃ sat dhmātaṃ kuryāt ।।
itthaṃ kṛtaṃ khoṭaṃ piṣṭistambhaḥ golākāraṃ bhavati ।।
tat vadanagataṃ mukhāntaḥsthitaṃ śastravārakaṃ syāt asmiṃśca vadanaṃ gate sati śarīre khaḍgādīnāṃ prahāro na lagati ।।
guṭir iyaṃ nāmnā abhidhānena amarasundarīguṭikā jñeyā ।।
iyaṃ śarīrasthā mukhe anyasthale vā sthitā satī śarīrasthān rogān hanti vināśayati ।।
anuktamapi mānaṃ pañcaniṣkapramāṇaṃ jñeyamityarthaḥ ।।
ityamarasundarī guṭikā ।।
hemnā vā rajatena vāpi sahito dhmāto vrajatyekatāmakṣīṇo niviḍo guḍaśca guṭikāḥ karoti dīrghojjvalāḥ ।।
cūrṇaṃ tatpaṭuvatprayāti vihitaghṛṣṭo na muñcenmalaṃ nirgandho dravati kṣaṇātsa hi mato baddhābhidhāno rasaḥ ।
iti granthāntare ।।

mṛtasaṃjīvanīguṭikā
yaḥ pūrvoktaḥ sūto lakṣādūrdhvaṃ ca vedhate lohān ।
baddhe sāraṇayogair mukhāsthe ca jārayedratnam ।।
yuktaḥ samāṃśanāgaiḥ suralohāyaskāntatāpyasattvaiśca ।
abhrakasattvasametā guṭikā mṛtasaṃjīvanī nāma ।।
hemayutā gulucchake mukuṭe vā kaṇṭhasūtrakarṇe vā ।
mṛtyubhayaśokarogaviṣaśastrajarāsatataduḥkhasaṅghātam ।।
yasyāṅge nihiteyaṃ guṭikā mṛtasaṃjīvanī nāma ।
so'surayakṣakinnarapūjyatamaḥ siddhayogīndraiḥ ।।
prakṣālya toyamadhye guṭikā ghaṭikādvayaṃ tataḥ kṣiptvā ।
tacceyaṃ vadanagatā mṛtakasyotthāpanaṃ kurute ।।
toyaṃ tadeva pibati svasthaṃ pathyānvitastataḥ puruṣaḥ ।
labhate divyaṃ sa vapurmṛtyujarāvarjitaḥ sudṛḍham ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

mṛtasaṃjīvanīguṭikāvidhānaṃ guṇāṃścāha ya ityādi ।।
yaḥ pūrvoktaḥ sūto lakṣādūrdhvaṃ koṭyarbudādi lohān rūpyādīn vedhate tasminbaddhe sūte mukhasthe prakāśamukhayantre sthāpite sāraṇayogaiḥ sāraṇatailādibhiḥ ratnaṃ vajrādikaṃ jārayet ।।
punaḥ samāṃśanāgais tulyāṃśasīsakaiḥ sūto yuktaḥ kāryaḥ suralohāyaskāntatāpyasattvaiśca yuktaḥ kāryaḥ suralohaṃ kanakaṃ ayaskāntaḥ kāntalohaṃ tāpyasattvaṃ mākṣikasāraṃ etaiḥ abhrakasattvasametā satī mṛtasaṃjīvanī nāma guṭikā bhavati punastatra mūṣāyāmiyaṃ hemayutā kāryā ।।
punar iyaṃ guṭikā nityaṃ yasya gulucchake nihitā bhavati vā mukuṭe kirīṭe vā kaṇṭhasūtrakarṇe kaṇṭhasūtraṃ ca karṇaśca kaṇṭhasūtrakarṇaṃ tasmin vā aṅge hastapādādau tasya mṛtyubhayaśokarogaśastrajarāsatataduḥkhasaṃghātaṃ naśyati ityadhyāhāraḥ ।।
eteṣu sthāneṣu yasyeyaṃ nihitā sthāpitā bhavati sa asurayakṣakinnarapūjyatamaḥ asurā daityāḥ yakṣā devayonayaḥ kinnarāḥ turaṅgavaktrāḥ teṣāṃ pūjyatamo bhavati atiśayena pūjyaḥ pūjyatamaḥ ।।
siddhayogīndraiḥ pūjyatamaḥ siddhā devaviśeṣāḥ yogīndrā nāgārjunādayaḥ tato'nantaraṃ mṛtajīvanī jalamadhye kṣiptvā prakṣālya ghaṭikādvayaṃ vadanagatā satī mṛtakasya puruṣasyotthāpanaṃ prabodhanaṃ kurute yaḥ pumān puruṣaḥ tadeva toyaṃ guṭikākṣālanaṃ svacchaṃ nirmalaṃ pibati kiṃviśiṣṭaḥ pathyānvito hitāvahadravyabhakṣaṇayuktaḥ sa puruṣo divyaṃ vapuḥ devaśarīraṃ labhate kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ divyaṃ punaḥ mṛtyujarāvarjitaṃ vyādhipālityarahitaṃ punaḥ sudṛḍhaṃ vajravad guṭikāparimāṇaṃ pākavidhānaṃ ca pūrvavad ityarthaḥ ।।
iti mṛtajīvanīguṭikā ।।

vajriṇīguṭikā
kāntaghanasattvakamalaṃ hema ca tāraṃ yathā kṛtadvandvam ।
samajīrṇaṃ bījavaraṃ vajrayutaṃ vajriṇī guṭikā ।।
eṣā mukhakuharagatā kurute navanāgatulyabalam ।
tadvapurapi durbhedyaṃ mṛtyujarāroganirmuktam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

vajriṇīguṭikāvidhānaṃ guṇāṃścāha kāntetyādi ।।
kāntaṃ ca ghanaṃ ca anayoḥ sattvaṃ kāntaghanasattvaṃ kāntasattvaṃ cumbakasattvaṃ ghanasattvaṃ abhrakasāraṃ kamalaṃ ceti kamalaṃ tāmraṃ ca punarhema svarṇaṃ tāraṃ ca rūpyaṃ pūrvavat yathā yena vidhānena kṛtadvandvaṃ kṛtaṃ ca tat dvandvaṃ ceti bījavaraṃ samajīrṇaṃ kāryaṃ kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ bījavaraṃ vajrayutaṃ hīrakayutam iyaṃ guṭikā nāmato vajriṇī punareṣā vajriṇīguṭikā mukhakuharagatā satī mukhāntaḥprāptā satī navanāgatulyabalaṃ navasaṃkhyākā nāgāḥ hastinastaistulyaṃ tatsamaṃ yadbalaṃ tatkurute tadvapustasya mukhe guṭikādhāriṇo vapuḥ śarīraṃ durbhedyaṃ duḥkhena bhettuṃ śakyaṃ punarmṛtyujarāvyādhibhir nirmuktam ityarthaḥ ।।
iti vajriṇī guṭikā ।।

khecarīguṭikā
dhūmāvalokitarase pañcamahāratnajārite sārite ।
bījena gaganasattve mākṣikakāntaprayuktena ।।
khecarasaṃjñā guṭikā patati mukhe kṣiptamātreṇa ।
devāsurasiddhagaṇaiḥ pūjyatamo bhavati cendrādyaiḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

khecarīguṭikāvidhānaṃ guṇāṃścāha dhūmetyādi ।।
dhūmāvalokite dhūmavedhini rase sūte pañcamahāratnajārite pañcasaṃkhyākair mahāratnair vajrādibhiḥ tathā ca ।
vajraṃ ca mauktikaṃ caiva māṇikyaṃ nīlameva ca ।
marakataṃ ca vijñeyaṃ mahāratnāni pañcadhā ।
iti ।।
punar mākṣikakāntaprayuktena tāpyacumbakamilitena bījena rase gaganasattve sārite sati khecarasaṃjñā guṭikā bhavati ।।
tasmin guṭikārūpe rase kṣiptamātreṇa mukhe patati sati indrādyaiḥ devāsurasiddhagaṇaiśca pūjyatamo bhavati indro maghavā ādyo yeṣāṃ te taiḥ ।।
devā amarāḥ asurāḥ daityāḥ siddhā devaviśeṣāḥ teṣāṃ ye gaṇāḥ samūhāḥ taiḥ kṛtvā atiśayena pūjyo bhavatītyarthaḥ ।।
iti khecarasaṃjñāguṭikā ।।

rasavādo'nantaguṇo dravagolakakalkabhedena ।
kalitaḥ pradhānasiddhairyair dṛṣṭaste jayanti narāḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

rasavādasyānantatvaṃ sūcayannāha rasetyādi ।।
rasavādo anantaguṇaḥ anantā guṇā yasya sa tathoktaḥ ।।
anantā aparimitāḥ ।।
kena kṛtvā rasavādo'nantaḥ dravagolakakalkānāṃ pratyekamanantatvāt rasavādo'pyanantaḥ ।।
kiṃbhūtaḥ pradhānasiddhaiḥ nityanāthādibhiḥ kalitaḥ racitaḥ ।।
yairmahadbhiḥ siddhaiḥ rasavādo dṛṣṭaste narā jayanti sarvotkarṣeṇa vartante ।।

śītāṃśuvaṃśasambhavahaihayakulajanmajanitaguṇamahimā ।
sa jayati śrīmadanaśca kirātanātho rasācāryaḥ ।।
yasya svayamavatīrṇā rasavidyā sakalamaṅgalādhārā ।
paramaśreyasahetuḥ śreyaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ pūrvam ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

atha granthakārayitur vaṃśavarṇanam āha śītāṃśuvaṃśetyādi ।।
śrīmadano madanābhidho rājā jayati sarvotkarṣeṇa vartate ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaḥ kirātanāthaḥ kirātāḥ bhillāsteṣāṃ svāmī ।।
punaḥ kiṃviśiṣṭaḥ śītāṃśuvaṃśasaṃbhavahaihayakulajanmajanitaguṇamahimā śītāṃśuvaṃśe candravaṃśe saṃbhava utpattiryasya tat evaṃvidhaṃ yat haihayakulaṃ tatra kule janmanā udbhavena janito guṇānāṃ mahimā yena sa tathoktaḥ ।।
punaḥ kiṃviśiṣṭo madanaḥ rasācāryaḥ rasavidyājanaka ityarthaḥ ।।
atha cāsya kārayitur guṇavarṇanamāha yasyetyādi ।।
yasya kārayituḥ śrīmadanasaṃjñasya rasavidyā svayaṃ svarūpatvenāvatīrṇā prādurbhūtā ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭā rasavidyā sakalamaṅgalādhārā sakalāni ca tāni maṅgalāni uttamarūpāṇi teṣāmādhāraḥ āśrayo yasyāṃ sā ।।
eṣā rasavidyā śarīraṃ ajarāmaraṇaṃ ajarāmaraṃ kurute śarīraṃ ca dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ mūlaṃ ataḥ sakalamaṅgalādhāreti yuktam ।।
punaḥ rasavidyā śreyase muktau parama utkṛṣṭo hetuḥ kāraṇam ।।
anayaiva rasavidyayā parameṣṭhino brahmaṇaḥ pūrvaṃ prathamaṃ śreyo ajarāmaraṇarūpaṃ saṃjātam ।।

tasmāt kirātanṛpater bahumānam avāpya rasakarmanirataḥ ।
rasahṛdayākhyaṃ tantraṃ viracitavān bhikṣugovindaḥ ।।

Comm Mugdhāvabodhinī

kartā svanāmamahattvaṃ sūcayannāha tasmādityādi ।।
idaṃ rasatantraṃ śāstraṃ viracitavān kṛtavāniti bhāvaḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ idaṃ tantraṃ rasahṛdayākhyaṃ kiṃ kṛtvā tasmādityādi ।।
